## 2026-07-10 (LATEST) — D301: colour styling-lift routes by DB ROLE (not a property-name list) + concrete-value fallback; 6 universal pill-cloning bugs fixed

**D301 — the styling-lift resolves a colour value by the DB-owned attr `role='color'`, never a hardcoded `css_property` allowlist, and keeps the concrete hex/rgba when no palette token matches.** Branch main; commits `5bb622d4` (3 bugs + BgColour migration), `1d15d491` (border shorthand), `2b43a6df` (border-color + rgba preservation), `89dcaf41` (role-based routing refactor). 440 converter tests pass throughout; verified on the live page-8 clone. D-ceiling was D300.

- **Bean-reported:** cloned pack pills rendered uniform taupe (D299 made them cloneABLE but the converter never populated the pill colours — the R11–R13 items the D299 report flagged UNVERIFIED, now proven broken on a real clone). Root-caused to 6 UNIVERSAL styling-lift bugs (benefit every clone, not per-block):
  1. **`BgColour` suffix gap** (`migrations/2026-07-10-property-suffixes-bg-colour.py`): `property_suffixes` had `BackgroundColour`+`Bg`+`Colour` but not `BgColour` — the framework's 7-block `*BgColour` naming peeled only `Colour`→`color`, so every bg-colour attr grabbed the element's TEXT colour. Added `BgColour`→`background-color`.
  2. **Compound-selector matching** (`styling_helpers.py::collect_css_decls_for_element`): a compound class selector `.a.b` had `last_part[1:]="a.b"` (dot inside), never a single class → dropped. The draft's selected rule `.__pill.__pill--active` was unmatched, so every SELECTED colour resolved to the RESTING value. Now parses the final compound's class tokens + matches iff the element carries all (higher class-count → higher specificity → compound wins).
  3–4. **`background` + `border` shorthand → longhand** (`styling_content.py`): drafts declare flat colour via the shorthand (`.pill{background:var(--cream)}` / `border:2px solid var(--border)`); the lift resolved `background-color`/`border-color` and missed the shorthand key. Now falls back to the colour-only shorthand (background: excludes gradient/url; border: extracts the colour token).
  5. **`border-color` never resolved** — `_compute_value` ran the colour resolver only for `color`/`background-color`; border-color fell to raw-string, so `var(--border)` stored the DRAFT's own var (dangling on SGS).
  6. **rgb()/rgba()/hsl() dropped** — `extract_token_or_hex` returned None for functional colours (only var()/#hex); a pale `rgba(230,138,149,0.1)` was dropped, or token-snapped to an opaque slug (alpha lost).
- **Bean anti-cheat correction (the load-bearing refactor).** Fix 5 initially added `border-color` to a hardcoded `(color,background-color,border-color)` list — Bean: that's a cheat (the NEXT colour property silently breaks; routing depends on the property NAME, not on whether the value resolves — a value can snap on one client's global palette and be missing on another). **Corrected:** `_compute_value` branches on the DB-owned `role=='color'` (threaded from `lift_styling_content` through `_emit_value`), so ANY colour property routes through `extract_token_or_hex`, whose match-vs-no-match branch keeps the concrete hex/rgba on no token match. R-31-1 + Spec 31 §3 step 6 (per-client divergences emit as raw instance values). **Do NOT reintroduce a css_property allowlist for colour routing.**
- **Result (live page 8):** pill 7/8 draft-accurate — resting cream bg / beige border (`border-subtle`) / muted text; selected pink border + dark text. **REMAINING (not converter):** selected FILL renders solid pink not the 10% tint — the attr extracts + stores the rgba correctly, but the picker defaults to `colourPreset='solid'` whose CSS sets `--sgs-op-sel-bg`=primary; the clone should set `colourPreset=''` when it supplies explicit per-pill colours (`P-PILL-SELECTED-FILL-PRESET`).

## 2026-07-10 — D300: INTEGRATION session — all no-inline tracks merged; box_family made fully DECLARATIVE (block.json, not the sgs-update dict); hero dark-pink bug fixed

**D300 — the split-edit/serial-land rollout was integrated: 6 branches (Tracks A–E + D299 option-picker) merged to main, and `box_family` seeding moved ENTIRELY from the `sgs-update-v2.py` hardcoded dict to declarative `block.json supports.sgs.boxFamilies`.** Branch main; commits `0a1f2d8f` (D299 merge + product-card reconcile), `6b4473de` (declarative box_family), `95707585` (post-grid + F3), `423609bb` (hero R6), `6c8260cf` (hero bg fix). D-ceiling was D299.

- **Merge + 2 collisions.** Tracks A/C/D merged clean. Two collisions D299 introduced (it also migrated option-picker + product-card): **option-picker** → took D299 wholesale (strict superset of Track B); **product-card** → 3-way reconcile, D299 draft-fidelity base + Track E's no-inline layered (removed the dead legacy `.pill` CSS + the forced-pink `--sgs-op-border` hardcode). **Brand-purge:** every client-hex `#e68a95`/`#c56a7a`/pink-rgba fallback → framework brand teal (`grep '#e68a95' == 0`; Spec 32 FR-32-6 — framework default is a theme token, never a client hex).
- **Declarative box_family (Bean-directed "stop hardcoding into sgs-update").** 40 blocks now declare `supports.sgs.boxFamilies` (family→[object-attrs]) in their own block.json; `sgs-update`'s scan (`_collect_boxfamily_overrides`) derives the `box_family` column — same mechanism it already uses for `arrayItemSchema`/variants. Removed all 137 box_family entries from `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` (now role/derived_selector only). VERIFIED: the declarative derivation == the old dict for all 24 landed blocks (0 regressions) + 64 new entries; live `/sgs-update --stage 1` `applied=363, 0 missing`, box_family column = 205 correct. **Spec 31 §4 / Spec 32 §6.1(c) still name the dict — reconcile to the declarative mechanism (open).**
- **hero dark-pink bug (Bean-reported) FIXED (`6c8260cf`).** hero rendered dark pink not the main primary the trust-bar uses. Root cause: draft `.sgs-hero` is flat `var(--surface-pink)` #F5C2C8, transferred correctly — but hero/style.css's default `linear-gradient(135deg, primary-dark, primary)` background-IMAGE painted over it. The suppression `.sgs-hero:not(.has-background)` only added `has-background` for a PRESET bg slug; the no-inline migration moved the transferred bg to a scoped `#uid` rule so the inline `[style*=background]` selector stopped matching. FIX: render.php re-adds `has-background` for a custom `style.color.background`/gradient. Verified live: hero bg = trust-bar bg (flat #F5C2C8, no gradient).
- **Residuals resolved:** post-grid REST-include (`class-post-grid-rest.php`) inline colour/bg/aspect → CSS-var VALUES on the card root (AJAX-injected cards carry their own vars); product-card `7px 13px` F3 baseline row drained; hero R6 flat root padding/margin tiers → box-object (mirrors cta-section) + declared boxFamilies. Bean priorities verified live: hero responsive padding 375/768/1440 matches draft; custom hex colours + custom px padding render via the scoped-var channel with zero inline (not preset-locked).

## 2026-07-10 — D299: universal state-styling lift unblocked (stale hover-ban removed) + sgs/option-picker cloning-fidelity build dispatched

**D299 — the styling lift's stale `__hover/__active/__focus` exclusion is removed, and the option-picker is being made faithfully cloneable (resting + selected pill styling) via the universal pipeline, not a bespoke mechanism.** Branch: converter fix on `main` (`247dc544`); option-picker build on `feat/option-picker-cloning` (dispatched, files-only, PENDING land). D-ceiling was D298.

- **Root cause + reframe (Bean-directed).** Typed and bound pack pickers already render the SAME `sgs/option-picker` block (product-card renders it via `render_block` from `packSizes`), but the clone showed a FIXED SGS pink design regardless of the draft. Not because the picker is special — because (a) a stale styling-lift exclusion dropped state styling, and (b) the picker's pill-state colours weren't declared as liftable attrs. **The universal pipeline routes every element's CSS by `derived_selector`+`role` (§3.B.0) — the option-picker is not exempt.**
- **Converter fix SHIPPED (`247dc544`, 440 tests pass).** Removed the blanket `__hover/__active/__focus` skip in `resolvers/styling_content.py` (Spec 31 §3.B B2) — a temporary stopgap never removed. State attrs (hover / persistent-selected — `hoverBackgroundColour`, `pillSelectedBgColour`, …) now lift via their own state-keyed `derived_selector`, like every non-state attr. Unblocks hover/state cloning across the ~10 blocks that declare hover colour attrs + the option-picker. Spec 31 §3.B B2 updated; **do NOT re-introduce a state-selector exclusion.**
- **Option-picker build DISPATCHED (`/subagent-driven-development`, strict contract, feat/option-picker-cloning).** Scope: make resting + selected pill colour/border-radius attrs LIFTABLE (role=color + derived_selector: resting `.__pill`, selected `.__pill--active`); add `pillSelectedBorderColour` (decouple selected border from fill) + `pillSelectedBorderRadius` + `showSelectedTick`; ship **soft** (draft cream/tint, no tick) + **solid** (bound pink-fill + tick) presets on the button-preset token pattern (Spec 32/D291); product-card forwards the pill-style attrs to `render_block` + gains its own liftable pill-state attrs; **remove the `--sgs-op-border:primary` hardcode**; DB seeds via `sgs-update-v2.py` overrides; theme preset tokens. PLUS the full no-inline DONE-checklist (all 11 conditions) for `sgs/option-picker` — every new AND old attr. LANDED (deploy + live 375/768/1440 + reclone) is the integration step, not the build.
- **Cloning model (Bean-locked):** copy the draft's EXACT colours per-instance (the draft's pill vars are theme-token-aligned → a var-name→token mapping), presets are the manual-authoring library. Structural limits fixed by the build: the outlined selected state coupled border to fill; the always-on tick.
- **F3-gate blind-spot noted:** the hardcoded-defaults gate can't see a hardcode with no matching attr (why `--sgs-op-border:primary` slipped) — a gate-precision follow-up once the pill-state attrs exist.
- **Track E (parallel):** `sgs/product-card` no-inline migration + typed↔bound picker parity + dead-CSS cleanup landed on `feat/no-inline-track-E` (files-only, `100d41e7`/`ae33cca6`/`286176c8`) — the picker-parity CSS gap (typed missed the `--live`-gated overrides) is superseded by this D299 cloning build.

## 2026-07-10 — D298: no-inline Wave-2 — 10 blocks LANDED (4 leaf/inline + 4 array/timeline + 2 keep-structure navs)

**D298 — no-inline rollout Wave 2: all 10 blocks migrated + LANDED across 3 dispatch rounds.** Branch main; commits `d8923f4c` (R1), `eeb17be4` (R2), `60d55b23` (R3); D-ceiling was D297. Continues D294–297. Orchestrated (Opus) + solo-Sonnet-per-block (disjoint dirs, parallel-safe FR-31-6.1/STOP-39); every block gated by me (STOP-16): `npm run build` prebuild gates + `check-box-family-guard.py --check` (0) + converter suite (440 pass) re-run; LANDED via the reusable harness `scripts/no-inline-land-verify.js` (asymmetric instances on page 1356, zero-inline + computed box at 375/768/1440), OPcache+LiteSpeed purged before each verify; visual-diff reports at repo-root `reports/visual-diff/`; path-scoped commits; no version bumps/deprecations (D293).

- **R1** (`d8923f4c`): collapsible-text, table-of-contents, decorative-image, countdown-timer. ToC's "broken" bug ROOT-CAUSED + fixed (a custom attr literally named `style` collided with WP's reserved `style` object → renamed `tocStyle`). decorative-image was a pure inline-render fix (position/transform/opacity/z-index → scoped) + a parallax `view.js` re-inline trap closed (→ CSS var).
- **R2** (`eeb17be4`): icon-list, brand-strip, timeline, process-steps (2 carry `shadow` support → skip-serialised + scoped). Two border routes both valid+used (quote-route custom `borderWidth` object vs media-route native). brand-strip `view.js` `animationPlayState` inline → class; its fade-edge `[style*=background]` sniff → `.has-background`.
- **R3** (`60d55b23`): mega-menu + mobile-nav — KEEP-STRUCTURE InnerBlocks navs (mobile-nav is content-KIND but a genuine 7-zone drawer → NOT block-private; D294 default overridden per-block). mega-menu panel inline `style="position:fixed;width:100vw;…"` → scoped; its `color` support was a dead no-op, now paints. mobile-nav: 5 `view.js` swipe `.style.transform/transition` → `.is-swiping` class + CSS vars; stray 768/480 → 1023/767.
- **F3-drain**: the REAL dead-control overrides on both navs drained to `var()`; but 3 baseline rows (mega-menu `align-items`×2 → panelAlignment; mobile-nav `max-width:100vw` → drawerMaxWidth) traced to structural CSS / a viewport safety clamp — **MIS-TAGGED, not dead-control debt**. Per prove-the-cause NOT force-wired; Bean-decided (defer): left baselined, gate-precision fix tracked (`P-F3-NAV-MISTAG-GATE`).
- **Roster: 15/59 → 25/59; ~34 remain** (Wave 3 content-KIND composites → block-private; Wave 4 section/layout composites keep-wrapper; then Task 4 wire the 2 gates zero-tolerance). **NEXT = Wave 3.**
- **Reconcile follow-on (`ee01c887`):** an audit found 4 already-box-migrated blocks (button/container/business-info/social-icons) still declared an ENABLED native `color`/`typography` support WITHOUT skip-serialisation → that property auto-inlined via WP native Styles (the box-only harness never exercised it). All 4 fixed (skip-serialise + scoped; container via the shared wrapper's `extra_classes` seam — no shared-file edit) + LANDED (live-curl-confirmed the colour/typography paints scoped, not inline, not vanished — D291/D292). `text`+`media` false-positives (`color:false` = disabled). **Parallel-rollout plan written** (`c49da804`, `.claude/plans/2026-07-10-no-inline-parallel-rollout.md`): split-edit/serial-land model for the remaining 35 — parallel worktree edit-tracks A–E (files-only, disjoint, report seeds) + one integration/LAND session; avoids the whole-plugin-deploy clobber. Per-track next-session prompts under `.claude/next-session-prompts/`.
- Lessons: a JS block comment containing `*/` (e.g. `style.spacing.*/style.border`) closes the comment early + breaks the webpack build — caught by the build (STOP-16), fixed, baked into every subsequent subagent prompt. The `var(--x, <literal>)` F3-drain form is contract-sanctioned but the hardcoded-defaults gate still counts the literal in the fallback — fully zeroing a row needs the default emitted from render.php.

## 2026-07-10 — D297: no-inline Wave-1 — 8 leaf blocks LANDED + hero L4 per-area object-routing converter gap fixed

**D297 — no-inline rollout Wave 1: 8 single-element/leaf blocks migrated block-private + LANDED; plus a real D295 converter gap (hero L4 per-area padding cloning) found and fixed.** Branch main; commit `ec5063a9`; D-ceiling was D296. Continues D294–296.

- **8 leaf blocks (label, icon, counter, whatsapp-cta, social-icons, star-rating, business-info, breadcrumbs)** migrated to the no-inline contract, block-private (heading/text/button pattern). Each: every declared WP styling support (`spacing`/`color`/`__experimentalBorder`/`typography`) flipped to `__experimentalSkipSerialization` + emitted scoped via `wp_style_engine_get_styles($style,['selector'=>"#uid"])`; box padding/margin (+ counter/whatsapp-cta border-radius) → named objects with Tablet/Mobile tiers; device tiers 1023/767 only; semantic element as root (no useless wrapper); free-text keyword sanitisers + `wp_strip_all_tags`. **box_family seeds added centrally** in `sgs-update-v2.py` (FR-31-22.1). No version bumps, no deprecations (D293). Block-specific: social-icons renamed its own `style` variant attr → `iconStyle` (collided with WP-native `style` object); whatsapp-cta collapsed its wrapper to the `<a>` root (D288 pattern); label merged 4 flat padding attrs → `padding` object, kept `borderRadius` scalar-but-scoped; counter guarded a top-level function (`function_exists`, redeclare-fatal fix); icon kept `backgroundPadding` scalar (single-value, §6.1c).
- **LANDED (dispatched to 8 solo Sonnet subagents, disjoint dirs, FR-31-6.1; orchestrator gated every block):** built once, deployed to sandybrown, verified live on page 1356 at 375/768/1440 via a NEW reusable harness `scripts/no-inline-land-verify.js` + `no-inline-wave1-manifest.json` — RESULT ALL PASS: zero inline property declarations on the whole subtree + asymmetric computed padding/border-radius correct at every tier. (margin left/right is owned by WP-core `is-layout-constrained` centering `!important` — a non-block-fidelity axis; the harness asserts margin top/bottom, the block-controlled axis.) 8 visual-diff reports at repo-root `reports/visual-diff/`.
- **Roster: 15/59 styling-support blocks migrated (7 prior + 8); ~44 remain** (phased waves — Wave 2 = more leaf blocks + F3-drains; see next-session-prompt.md).
- **Hero L4 converter gap (found + fixed):** the routine `--stage 10` aggressive prune correctly removed hero's orphaned flat `contentPaddingTop/Left/…` attrs (D295 migrated hero's per-area padding flat→OBJECT `contentPadding`), which surfaced 4 stale converter tests + a REAL latent gap: the L4 per-area CLONING path (`fold_helpers.route_area_css_to_block_attrs` — the live path via assembly step 3d — AND `resolvers/grid_area.py`) was left on the flat model, so `attr_for_area_property` returned None and **hero content-padding silently gapped on every clone** (D295's earlier "72/64 LANDED" was an authored value, not cloned — the coincidental-default false-win Spec 31 §7b warns about; hero style.css has NO padding default). Fix: made BOTH L4 paths box-object-aware, mirroring `content_band._content_band_box_write` — route the four padding sides into the `{area}Padding{Tier}` object, gated on `db_lookup.box_family_for` (a `box_family` VARIABLE ref to satisfy the FR-31-22.2 AST gate), never a name regex. 4 stale flat-asserting tests updated to the object contract + 1 new test locking the live fold_helpers path. **Converter suite 440 pass; cheat/excluded/ledger/db-consistency/box-family gates all green. LANDED on a page-8 reclone:** hero `.sgs-hero__content` padding now clones from the draft → **72/64 @1440, 28/20/40 @375, zero inline** (was gapped). Lessons: STOP-34 (a synthetic unit test passed while the real draft still gapped — the fix's first location `grid_area` wasn't even the live path; the trace showed 0 grid_area dispatches, `route_area_css_to_block_attrs` is the live path), R-31-11 (verify rendered output, not internal metrics), prove-the-cause (D295's LANDED claim fact-checked against the draft + style.css before trusting the fix).

## 2026-07-09 — D296: universal grid-scoping — SGS_Container_Wrapper grid/flex CSS inline→scoped (STOP-68 CLOSED)

**D296 — the shared wrapper's grid engine no longer emits base grid/flex REAL properties inline; they route to a scoped `.uid` rule. Closes STOP-68 (the hero `display:grid` residual) universally.** Branch main; a wrapper-only PHP change (no rebuild). Base `display:grid`/`display:flex` + `grid-template-columns`/`rows` + `grid-auto-rows` + `align-items`/`justify-*`/`flex-*` now accumulate into `$base_grid_real_decls` → emitted as ONE scoped rule on `$grid_sel` (`.uid` outer / `.uid>.sgs-container__inner` grid-on-inner), appended BEFORE the `@media` grid tiers (source-order wins, no `!important`); `$needs_uid` gains `$has_base_grid` (base-only grids still get a uid). `--sgs-gi-*` grid-item CUSTOM PROPERTIES stay inline (contract §A allows `--vars`). Latent bug fixed: base `grid-template-rows`/`grid-auto-rows` previously always targeted the outer even when grid-on-inner (inert) — now follow `$grid_sel`. Non-grid blocks byte-identical; `php -l` + `phpcs` clean. **LANDED page 8 (live, anonymous Playwright, post purge):** scanned all 95 SGS elements — ZERO inline grid/flex real-property declarations framework-wide; all grids intact (hero split 360px, container--grid 320px, feature-grid `152px 152px`, flex containers flex). Fixed ONCE in the shared wrapper because grid CSS affects EVERY grid composite (Spec 31 §3.A treats display/grid-template-* specially). STOP-68 CLOSED — hero + every grid composite is now fully zero-inline (bar unmigrated child blocks). **Scope reality-check (Bean, 2026-07-09):** the "~26 remaining blocks" in the prompt was a narrow slice; the real remaining no-inline scope is the FULL styling-support roster — DB: 59 blocks declare styling supports, 7 migrated (button/container/heading/text/quote/media/hero) → **52 remaining** + 6 F3-debt blocks + no-support inline-render blocks. Task 3 is a phased, multi-session waved programme, not one task.

## 2026-07-09 — D295: no-inline rollout Task 2 — sgs/hero LANDED (6 per-area box-object families + F3-drain, keeps wrapper)

**D295 — `sgs/hero` (the biggest block, section-KIND composite) migrated to no-inline + box-object, LANDED live on page 8.** Branch main; continues D294. Hero KEEPS `SGS_Container_Wrapper` for the section (D294 principle: section/layout composites keep the wrapper; only content-KIND go block-private) and renders its 6 per-area families block-privately.

- **6 per-area families flat→object:** `contentPadding`/`mediaPadding`/`imagePadding`/`imageBorderWidth`(base-only)/`imageBorderRadius`/`contentBandPadding`, incl. Tablet/Mobile tiers. Normalised the NON-STANDARD tier-infixed `imageBorderRadiusTabletTL` → `imageBorderRadiusTablet.topLeft`. ~65 flat attrs removed; 16 box_family seeds added centrally; 69 orphans pruned (STOP-66). All 4 WP supports flipped to `__experimentalSkipSerialization`; hero emits its section color/border/typography scoped to `.wp-block-sgs-hero` (NOT via the wrapper's inlining `extra_styles`). `$is_split` gating preserved. `contentBandPadding` is wrapper-consumed (object mirror of container).
- **F3-drain:** `align-items:center` style.css hardcode → `verticalAlignment`-driven scoped `.uid` rule (default center byte-identical); hero deleted from the F3 baseline (10→9).
- **blub-255 2-rater pre-commit panel: SHIP + SHIP.** Rater A (no-inline/double-emit) traced that the wrapper only serialises `style.spacing` while hero emits color/border/typography on its own uid → NO property emitted twice; skipSerialization suppresses WP auto-inline. Rater B (controls/F3) confirmed the dropped `ContainerWrapperControls` aggregator's 8 sub-panels were each re-added individually → zero lost controls, zero dead controls. The automated security review + panel caught an `$overlay_colour` sibling-sanitiser asymmetry → refactored to sanitise once at the concat site (`sgs_colour_value`), matching siblings.
- **LANDED page 8 (live, anonymous Playwright, post reclone + purge):** `contentPadding` object LANDED across tiers — 72/64 @1440 (base), 36/16 @768/375 (`contentPaddingTablet`); F3 `align-items:center` correct at all 3 breakpoints; zero inline from hero's own supports/per-area render; reclone regression clean (content 100%, parity 67/68/69 steady, no ConservationError).
- **KNOWN RESIDUAL (tracked, NOT a hero defect):** the hero section root carries one inline `display:grid` from the shared wrapper's grid engine (pre-existing; split-hero is a grid container). Grid-CSS scoping was deliberately deferred — it affects EVERY grid composite (card-grid/feature-grid/container grids) and belongs in ONE universal grid-scoping pass (Spec 31 §3.A treats `display`/`grid-template-*` specially). The child `sgs/label` inline is unmigrated (Task 3 roster). NEW STOP-68: hero/grid composites are NOT "100% zero inline" until the universal wrapper grid-scoping lands — do not claim framework-wide zero-inline before Task 4 without scoping `display:grid`/`grid-template-*`.

## 2026-07-09 — D294: no-inline rollout Task 1 — quote + media LANDED block-private; content-KIND→block-private principle (qc-council); shared wrapper max-width/contentWidth de-inlined

**D294 — the no-inline rollout advances to quote + media (both LANDED block-private), a shared-wrapper inline residual is fixed, and a qc-council settles how content-KIND composites migrate.** Branch main; D-ceiling was D293. Continues the D292/D293 pilot into the roster.

- **qc-council (3 raters, UNANIMOUS) — content-KIND composites go BLOCK-PRIVATE, not keep-wrapper (REVERSES an over-application of composite-mirror).** Question: should `sgs/quote` (DB `wraps_block='sgs/container'`, `container_kind='content'`) keep `SGS_Container_Wrapper` (P1) or go block-private like button/heading (P2)? Verdict P2, on evidence: (A) **converter-forensics** — CSS routes by `block_attributes` keyed on `block_slug` (block.json-derived), NEVER by `wraps_block`/`container_kind` (the column's own docstring: "NOT read by the walker, zero walker impact"); P2 needs NO DB change and the roster classifier re-derives `wraps_block` from InnerBlocks presence regardless, so nothing desyncs. (B) **spec-lawyer** — the rules do NOT mandate P1 (I over-stated composite-mirror FR-31-21.1, which forbids per-block CSS *hacks* that DIVERGE, not a clean block-private equivalent); the DONE-checklist explicitly names quote a "single-semantic-element" block; one real minor P2 cost = FR-31-21.2 auto-propagation. (C) **capabilities** — quote never used `ContainerWrapperControls` (hand-rolls its own panel), consumes only box+width (content-KIND), and block-private is more robust for 100% no-inline (owns its output, immune to shared-wrapper churn). **PRINCIPLE (avoids R-31-9 carve-out):** content-KIND composites whose only wrapper use is box+width MAY migrate block-private (like button/heading); section/layout-KIND composites (hero, cta-section, card-grid) KEEP the shared wrapper (genuine grid/section machinery). Applies to quote NOW + info-box/testimonial/team-member/product-faq-item in Task 3. (A clarifying note on Spec 31 FR-31-21.1 is owed — "mirror capabilities" permits an equivalent block-private impl for thin content-KIND composites.)
- **quote — 100% no-inline + box-object LANDED block-private (`reports/visual-diff/quote-2026-07-09.md`).** `<blockquote>` is the root (no `SGS_Container_Wrapper`, no wrapper div, class-uid anchor-safe); all supports skip-serialised; all CSS scoped; 22 flat attrs → objects (base padding/margin→`style.spacing.*`, tiers→`paddingTablet/Mobile`/`marginTablet/Mobile`, `borderWidth` object, base radius→`style.border.radius`). LANDED asymmetric page 1356: zero inline full subtree @375/768/1440; padding landed all-4-distinct across ALL tiers (3/6/9/12 · 7/14/21/28 · 11/22/33/44), radius 24/0/6/12, border-width 1/2/3/4 (margin L/R emitted correctly in the scoped rule — live-CSS-confirmed — but computed-overridden by page content-column auto-centring, a page-layout behaviour not a block defect).
- **media — 100% no-inline LANDED block-private (`reports/visual-diff/media-2026-07-09.md`).** Bigger than the prompt implied: ALL inline (object-fit/position, aspect-ratio, opacity, box-shadow, native border, figure align-margins, caption) moved to scoped; border-radius migrated 5 custom flat attrs → WP-native `style.border.radius` base + `borderRadiusTablet/Mobile` objects. ## 2026-07-09 — D292: box-object merge + no-inline styling pilot on sgs/container (core PROVEN LIVE)

**D292 — the universal no-inline styling architecture, designed + council-hardened + piloted on `sgs/container` (branch main `764ab2e6`; container CORE proven live page 8).** Supersedes D291's "add a canonical base attr" framing with the researched, standard-WP mechanism: **KEEP the WP-native styling supports (for their editor controls) but flip them from auto-inline to SCOPED serialisation** — `block.json` declares `__experimentalSkipSerialization` + the shared wrapper serialises the block's `style` object via the stable core `wp_style_engine_get_styles($style, ['selector'=>'#uid'])` into its own scoped `<style>` (exactly how WP core outputs `layout` support). `/library-docs` + `/research-check` confirmed this is standard WP, correcting D291's FS-A "drop supports + grow attr family" direction (heavier + loses native controls). **Box-object merge (Bean-approved):** per-side/corner box props (padding/margin/borderWidth 4-side; borderRadius 4-corner) merge into ONE named OBJECT attr (`{top,right,bottom,left}`/`{topLeft,…}` = WP `BoxControlValue` shape) via WP `BoxControl`, replacing 24 flat per-side attrs. **Collision guard (Bean's concern):** merge fires only on attrs carrying the DB `block_attributes.box_family` column (seeded via `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES`, absence = never merged) — NEVER a name-regex (which would sweep the 10 keep-scalar single-side/shapeDivider families); enforced by a plant-tested AST gate `check-box-family-guard.py`. **3-rater cross-model `/qc-council`** corrected 3 overstatements (guard = convention+AST-gate not "by construction"; 61%-via-helpers = static count; HARD-fails a per-key collision or dict/scalar mix, `raise`/STOP-27). Phase 0 committed `96a97bb0`; full pilot `764ab2e6`. **LANDED page 8 (container CORE):** A1 zero inline (10 containers), A2 base paints (56/64px scoped), A5 no regression (67%/100%), A6 guard live. ## 2026-07-09 — D291: Spec 32 component styling token contract + button reference impl; inline-CSS root cause proven; qc-council validates FS-A

**D291 — the button styling re-architecture (branch main; button reference LANDED + Bean-confirmed working live) + a spec + a validated programme for the universal fix.** Bean reported the D283 "preset-as-seed" button emitted 2 class-layers + broke hover + defaulted every clone to primary. **Built (Spec 32, `.claude/specs/32-COMPONENT-STYLING-TOKEN-CONTRACT.md`, NEW):** the button now uses a semantic BEM class (`.sgs-button--{preset}`) that SETS six `--sgs-btn-*` CSS vars from per-client `--wp--custom--button-presets--{preset}--{role}` tokens (WP auto-generates them from the theme-snapshot `settings.custom.buttonPresets`) with framework theme-token fallbacks; base `.sgs-button` CONSUMES the vars; **hover is a stylesheet `:hover` rule** (cascade: inline override var > preset token > fallback). render.php emits clean HTML (no inline colour), colour overrides as CSS-custom-property VALUES only, non-responsive decls to the id-scoped `<style>`; the nested `sgs-button__label` span removed; converter emits the class + strips the WP colour channel for preset buttons; a NEW `scripts/extract-button-presets.py` populates the snapshot buttonPresets from the draft (pipeline collects, not hand-authored). This RESTORES + generalises the pre-D283 Decision-24 design (`.is-style` + `--wp--custom--button-presets` vars) that D283 wrongly replaced with inline attrs. **Hover/preset-colours/structure Bean-confirmed working live** (hero/brand/gift). **RC2 fix:** `button/block.json` `inheritStyle` enum gained `"custom"` — WP was coercing the converter's (correct) `inheritStyle:"custom"` against the 3-value enum → default `"primary"`, forcing naked links ("Find out more") to primary buttons. **ROOT CAUSE PROVEN (the residual inline defect Bean caught):** cloned buttons still carry inline `padding-*`/`margin-*` from **WordPress-native block-supports serialization** — block.json declares `supports.spacing/color`, the converter routes base CSS into WP-native `style.spacing.*`/`style.color.*`, and `get_block_wrapper_attributes()` serialises those INLINE (core behaviour). Spec 31 §46/§58 says the engine must route each property to the correct BLOCK ATTRIBUTE (the designed `css_router.py` D1 "typed-attr lift" — disconnected 2026-05-27, ABSENT in the modular engine); the only root-CSS path is `root_supports.lift_root_supports_to_style` → `style.*`. **Two threads named (Bean):** (1) block/theme token architecture (Spec 32); (2) pipeline direct-attribute routing (Spec 31 D1). This is the SAME thread as D289/D290's L4 per-area routing (route CSS → the correct canonical attr). **qc-council (3 raters, high certainty):** FS-A (route base CSS → the block's canonical typed attrs → scoped external CSS) is the correct shape but MUST be fallback-safe (gate on `block_attrs()` membership; fall back to `style.*`; never route-and-drop), class+token (not scoped `#uid` for base — editor parity), precedence-ordered vs `lift_styling_content`, and reuse `_serialise_for_schema`. FS-B (Style Engine) + FS-C (render_block post-filter) REJECTED (double-emission / cosmetic). Detection script GO; deterministic auto-fix NO-GO (per-block judgement). **Bean's canonical-base-attr reframe (verified):** `sgs/container` has `paddingTopTablet/Mobile` but NO base `paddingTop` — the tiers presuppose a base that only exists as WP-native inline; `helpers-responsive.php` is ALREADY built for base+tier on one scoped selector with correct max-width cascade (unset tier inherits up). So the fix = add the canonical base attr the tiers imply + a naming standard, not invent a family. **Programme + opening sequence:** `.claude/plans/2026-07-09-styling-two-thread-programme.md` (Bean-directed session opening: read setup + db_lookup + DB columns → map delta to FS-A → Spec 31/32 doc gaps → truth-docs + sgs-wp-engine foundational-piece). NOT deployed: RC2 batches with the Thread-2 build (needs LiteSpeed purge to verify — Hostinger serves a server-side page cache the deploy flow doesn't purge). Gotchas: enum coerces invalid → default at render; WP-native `supports.{spacing,color,border}` ALWAYS inline via get_block_wrapper_attributes; Hostinger LiteSpeed page cache.

## 2026-07-06 — D286: sgs/media converge two styling systems to native attrs + add CSS height (fill)

**D286 — media block converge (`9a4f6ca1` + inline height fold-in, pushed, LANDED page 8).** `sgs/media` had TWO non-interoperating styling systems (native attrs written by the converter + read by render.php, NO editor controls; vs the shared image-controls extension writing `sgs*` attrs — different names/breakpoints/selectors). Full audit → 10 defects fixed: `is_numeric` guard dropped unit-embedded max-w/h (D1); border-radius 3-way miss — converter writes native `style.border.radius`, render read custom `borderRadius`, naked img got no native style (D2, STOP-44); no client controls (D4); naked-mode selector + wrapper-style divergence (D6); breakpoints 599→767 (D3); dead ext controls (D5); forced object-fit (D7); vestigial attrs (D8/D9). PLUS the CSS `height` (fill) was DROPPED (no destination attr) — added `height`/`heightTablet`/`heightMobile` string attrs; resolver auto-routes css `height` via `property_suffixes` height→Height + a `sgs-update --stage 1` reseed (R-31-1, data-only, no converter code change). render.php now: accepts unit-embedded strings, resolves border-radius per-corner→custom→native + emits inline on the img in BOTH modes, `:where()` overridable object-fit; new Media Styling + Caption/Link inspector panels + editable alt; media OPTED OUT of the shared image-controls extension (`block.json`, other blocks untouched); `__experimentalBorder.radius:false` (single radius channel). ## 2026-07-04 — D270: feature-grid renders through the shared container grid engine (was forced auto-flex)

**D270 — feature-grid renders through the shared container grid engine (was forced auto-flex 3-across; draft wants 4). Bean-diagnosed, proven on the live node (STOP-43).** (Commit messages say "D269" — a concurrent collision with the sgs/media D269 below; canonical = D270.) feature-grid showed 3 columns on desktop where the Mama's draft declares `repeat(4,1fr)` (≥600px). Root cause proven by dumping the LIVE CSS (NOT inferred — Bean challenged my first inference [that the converter must declare fixed-columns] and was right): the shared `SGS_Container_Wrapper` ALREADY emitted `.sgs-container-<uid>{grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr)}` + mobile `1fr 1fr` — the grid WAS transferred correctly — but feature-grid's OWN render.php printed a higher-specificity `#uid.sgs-feature-grid{grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(240px,1fr))}` auto-flex override that beat it (`#id.class` 1,1,0 > `.class` 0,1,0). A sibling `sgs/container` on the SAME page already rendered 4-col cleanly via the wrapper — proof the engine works and feature-grid was the SOLE divergence (composite-mirror violation, R-31-9). ## 2026-07-02 — D259: min-width/max-width cross-device tier fix (P-MINWIDTH-CROSSDEVICE-TIER) — the CSS-transfer breakpoint match rebuilt as a device-tier CASCADE; Spec 31 FR-31-5.2 defined + implemented.

**D259 — the live CSS-transfer path silently DROPPED `min-width:600` (trust-bar 4-col → rendered 2-col; same root cause as products/gift/ingredients, D256). Fixed universally in the shared collector. NOT pushed. 320 tests (+9) + cheat-gate (0 NEW, 73 baselined) green; convert.py byte-identical (D-MODULAR). LANDED verify page 8 pending.**

- **Root cause (proven vs the real draft `mamas-trust-bar-real.html`):** `collect_css_decls_for_element` (`converter/services/styling_helpers.py`) matched each `@media` rule by SUBSTRING against a fixed marker table (`_BREAKPOINT_RULES`, db_lookup.py) and, on no match, fell through WITHOUT writing/logging — `min-width:600` (∉ the 5 markers) was silently discarded. The draft's `__inner` is `1fr 1fr` base + `@media(min-width:600px){repeat(4,1fr)}`; the 4-col override vanished → base kept the 2-col mobile value → rendered 2-col everywhere.
- **The real shape = a mobile-first→desktop-base INVERSION, not just "un-drop" (Bean-chosen scope: universal shared collector, not a grid-only carve-out).** SGS blocks are desktop-base (the unsuffixed attr IS Desktop; `tier_suffix._BASE_TIER`), but mockups are mobile-first (base CSS = mobile). Half-fixing (Desktop→base only) would break mobile (render 4-col on phones).
- **Fix = device-tier CASCADE (Spec 31 §13.4 FR-31-5.2, newly DEFINED — it was referenced at §3 line 260 but never specified):** `collect_css_decls_for_element` computes the effective value per tier by sampling the CSS cascade at interior widths (Desktop 1440 / Tablet 800 / Mobile 375; `db_lookup.device_tier_samples`), then maps Desktop→base, Tablet/Mobile→suffixed (override only where ≠ base). `min-width:X` populates every tier whose sample ≥ X; `max-width:X` every tier ≤ X — ONE symmetric calculation, both directions. Kept the 2-tuple return (no ripple across the ~10 callers); only the SEMANTICS of base_decls (now desktop-effective) changed. `grid.py` needs no edit — Desktop folds into base, so the resolver's existing tier→attr mapping lands it.
- **F-ii residual (D228 lock):** a non-device threshold (∉ {767,768,1023,1024}, e.g. 600/640) has a sub-tier band the 3-tier model can't hold — surfaced via a non-silent `sgs.converter.styling` log (never snapped, never silently dropped). Raw-band passthrough-CSS rendering is a tracked follow-up; the covered tiers land in full.
- **Verify:** 9 new regression tests (`test_minwidth_cross_device_tier.py`) prove the inversion on the real trust-bar draft + the symmetric max-width direction + F-ii residual logging + `_media_condition_applies_at` boundaries; 320 total green; cheat-gate clean (new 768/1024 constants live in db_lookup, outside `check_parallel_bp`'s convert.py-only integer scan). **LANDED on page 8 is the closing gate (STOP-21/37; Bean eye, R-31-13) — trust-bar + products + gift + ingredients at 1440 vs draft — pending.**

## 2026-07-02 (LATER) — D258: array-item content lift COMPLETED for the 5 gap-blocks (the D257 known gap) — declared role + BEM-segment disambiguation + flat-item self-extraction; Spec 31 FR-31-2.1a/2.5a; array_item_schema +role. Name-heuristic seeder trialled + REJECTED.

**D258 — closes the D257 slot-vocabulary gap the right way. Not pushed (builds on the held D257 set). 311 tests (+5) + cheat-gate (0 NEW, 73 baselined) green; convert.py byte-identical (D-MODULAR). LANDED still pending (Task 1).**

- **Root of the gap (proven, corrects the D257 note):** the 5 blocks' content fields dropped because their camelCase field NAMES don't resolve to a slot AND same-role fields (pricing-table's 5 `text-content` fields) can't be told apart by role alone. The handoff's list was also incomplete (DB-verified): `card-grid.title/subtitle`, `pricing-table.name/description`, `trust-bar.url` also dropped; `card-grid.badge` did NOT (it resolves).
- **Fix = DECLARED role + BEM-segment match, NOT global aliases (Bean; Spec 31 FR-31-2.1a):** each dropping field declares its extraction `role` in `block.json items.properties.<field>.role` (`icon-slug`/`url-href`/`text-content`), seeded into a new `array_item_schema.role` column by the existing Stage-1 seeder (no parallel table). The resolver (`array_content.py`) prefers the declared role; `_lift_item` gained **L1b BEM-element-segment matching** (child `__cta` ↔ fields `ctaText`/`ctaUrl`, longest token wins; one element serves two fields by different roles) + **L1c flat-item self-extraction** (a social-icon `<a>` carries platform+url on ITSELF) + a **root-inclusion fix** in `_find_item_nodes` (items that are DIRECT children of the root — icon-list/card-grid/social-icons — were never detected). All 5 blocks now lift with zero gaps (resolver-verified; these blocks are absent from page 8, so resolver tests are their floor per §7b).
- **Name-heuristic seeder REJECTED (Bean-led):** trialled auto-deriving attr→element in `assign-canonical.py` by peeling the property suffix + taking the last camelCase segment. REVERTED — it mis-guesses the element (`titleColour`'s real element is `__name`, not the formula `__heading`) and over-resolves booleans (`showIcon`→icon). Ownership is stated in the block's code (render.php applies it, edit.js groups it, style.css selects it) and must be READ/declared, never name-parsed (FR-31-2.1a). The stale `fingerprints.json`/`tools/recogniser` builder is NOT the go-forward channel (`ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` is).
- **Spec 31 (D258):** FR-31-2.1a (ownership from code/declaration, not name) + FR-31-2.5a (array RECOGNITION scores candidate repeating groups against the item-field role signature — identity-based, like the other stages).
- **Tracked follow-ups (separate tracks):** (1) migrate 67 `fingerprints.json` selectors → `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` + drop the fingerprints load from assign-canonical; (2) FR-31-2.5a recognition-scoring in `_find_item_nodes` (detection works today via root-inclusion; scoring is robustness); (3) per-item CSS via `lift_styling_content` (per-item styling is uniform/block-level for these 5); (4) LANDED trust-bar on page 8 (STOP-21/37).

## 2026-07-02 (LATE) — D257: DB-recognition array field-lift + role-fallback replaces the hand-declared arrayItemSchema (R-31-9 violation); items.properties data model seeded to the DB; client-copy cheats removed.

**D257 — the array/repeater lift (Spec 31 §3.B4 / FR-31-2.5) rebuilt DB-driven. 7 commits on `main` (`c7fda7db`→`f892d585`), NOT pushed. 306 tests + cheat-gate + F5/F6 green; convert.py byte-identical (D-MODULAR).**

- **Mechanism (Bean's design, `c7fda7db`):** `converter/resolvers/array_content.py` rewritten — **structural item detection** (largest repeating same-BEM-token sibling group, §2.4 — no hand-declared `item_selector`) + a **2-layer field match**: L1 canonical-slot NAME match; L2 **role-fallback** — a draft child whose element name doesn't match a field name but whose content ROLE does fills that field (a `__text` child, role `text-content`, fills the `label` field, also `text-content`; verified on the real trust-bar draft). Replaces the hand-declared `arrayItemSchema`→`array_item_fields` selectors, which Spec 31 §3.B.0.1 names an R-31-9 violation.
- **Item field NAMES DB-driven (`f892d585`, Bean-requested):** new `array_item_schema` table seeded from `block.json attributes.<attr>.items.properties` (the block's data model) by `sgs-update-v2.py`; `db_lookup.array_item_field_names()` reads it; the resolver reads the DB, not `block.json` at convert-time. Old `array_item_fields` seeder retired → prune (`4d500bf6`).
- **8 array blocks de-hardcoded (`45869bfa`):** +`items.properties`, −`arrayItemSchema`. KNOWN GAP: 5 blocks' content fields (`icon-list.iconName/iconSource`, `social-icons.platform`, `card-grid.badge`, `pricing-table.cta*/ribbon/priceYearly`) drop — field names not yet in the slot vocabulary → next session (Task 2), following §13.3 FR-31-2.1; blocked on the STOP-24 `slots.aliases`-not-reseed-surviving hole.
- **Cheats removed:** client copy in `trust-bar.items.default`/example + `product-card` example (framework-neutrality — was FAKING the "trust-bar works" read); polygon-star raw-SVG preserved to `iconSvg` (`f0f0c8ac`). The F5 `no_slug_literal` gate caught 3 per-slot/role literal carve-outs (`slot=='icon'`/`'link'`, `role=='identity'`, `role in tuple`) — refactored DB-derived or into the un-gated shared `field_extractors` → **STOP-41** (the gate guards `role`/`slot`/`canonical_slot`, not just `block_slug`).
- **No design-gate for pipeline tasks (Bean directive):** Spec 31 is the settled authority — follow it in every detail; Rule 7 rewritten from "design-gate sensitive changes" to "follow the spec in every detail."

## 2026-06-29 — D249: CSS-resolver unification merged to main (311c120f) + FACT-CHECKED before any further build (the merge's coverage claims were unverified)

**D249 — Task 1 fact-check of the 2026-06-29 unification merge (`311c120f`, branch unify-v2 → main; HEAD now `8018ac15`). The prior session merged the Option-A seam + 5 CSS resolvers but ran out of context and produced confident-but-unverified "covers N routes / no-cheating" claims (worst: a 9-routes audit that hand-waved Bean's "17"). Every load-bearing claim re-verified by me at file:line + DB (STOP-30); two cross-model cheat/route subagents corroborated.**

- **HEADLINE (Finding A, verified):** the engine is TWO disconnected, INERT subsystems, not the unified §3 dispatch. `process_element` (CSS spine, `converter/orchestrator.py`) has ZERO production callers; `build_block_markup` (content emit, `extraction.py:392`) has ZERO production callers AND never calls `process_element`. So wrapper/box/grid CSS (L1–L4) has no path to a real clone — every resolver is WRITTEN, never LANDED. The frozen `convert.py` remains the live conductor (D-MODULAR). The unification + interior-walker wiring is the NEXT build (the keystone), not done.

## 2026-06-27 — D246: D245's separate content-extraction engine SUPERSEDED — content + CSS are ONE dispatch (Spec 31 §1); modularise the working `_lift_scalar_*` functions, do NOT rebuild content

**D246 — Bean correction (4-point brain-dump, 2026-06-27): the D245 content-extraction build is the WRONG architecture and is SUPERSEDED. Reading the FULL Spec 31 holistically (not grep) confirmed it: §1 "Architectural principle #1 — ONE lift path" explicitly lists the working content functions `_lift_scalar_attrs_by_selector` (scalar content) + `_lift_scalar_media_from_img` (scalar media) as part of the SINGLE DB-driven dispatch alongside the CSS lift functions. Content + CSS share ONE routing/pipeline — CSS just adds the L1–L4 layers + more DB data. The rebuild's job (§12.0 "split the converter into per-resolver files") is to MODULARISE the existing working functions into that one dispatch, NOT to recreate content with new logic + new DB columns.**

**What D245 did wrong:** built a SEPARATE, parallel content system — `converter/services/extraction.py` (`extract_content`/`run_mechanism_a`/`run_mechanism_b`), new `db_lookup` accessors (`content_attrs_with_selector`/`content_role_for_slot`/`primary_content_attr`), `payload.py`/`content_select.py`, bespoke media object-shaping + a migration — recreating the proven `_lift_scalar_attrs_by_selector`/`_lift_scalar_media_from_img` (content was already ~working draft→clone in convert.py per Bean) instead of modularising them into the unified `(block, layer, property, tier) → resolver` dispatch table next to `outer_box`/`grid`.

**Why the prior framing misled me:** the qc-council "NO-GO — Spec 31 §3 has no content mechanism" was right about §3's *text* but I concluded "defer to a v2 / cross-ref Spec 22" — WRONG. The correct conclusion: §3 must be rewritten as the UNIFIED content+CSS routing (§1 already mandates one dispatch), and content resolvers are the modularised working functions IN the same dispatch. The sweep's "needs-seed/array/polymorphic-media gaps" largely reflect my from-scratch engine reimplementing (worse) what the working functions + existing DB data (`derived_selector`/`canonical_slot`/`standalone_block`/`parent_block`/`accepts_allowed_blocks`) already handle. STOP-22 ("never read convert.py") protected against the BROKEN CSS-side assumptions; the WORKING content side is exactly what §12.0 says to modularise — reading those two functions to port them faithfully is now sanctioned.

**Corrected direction (next session):** (1) read the two working content functions in full; (2) modularise them into resolvers in the ONE dispatch table (content + CSS unified); (3) rewrite Spec 31 §3 as the unified content+CSS routing algorithm; (4) the Axis-3 child-routing amendment (D-pending, parent_block/accepts_allowed_blocks) folds into that unified §3, not a separate child-shape mechanism. D245 commits kept as history (the recognition Stage 2 / D244 is unaffected + correct; only the separate-content engine is superseded). Memory: `do-not-recreate-working-functionality-modularise-it`. D-CEILING now D246.

- **#3 CSS-shorthand: NOT a real gate bug.** `css_router._parse_declarations` keeps `padding`/`margin` WHOLE (verbatim), matching `declare_input` — both sides of the gate's join agree. The council assumed the gate measured convert.py's decomposition, but the gate measures css_router. Dismissed.
- **#5 inline styles: already fail-safe.** Inline declarations surface as UNACCOUNTED (loud), never silently dropped, and no draft fixture has any (SGS-BEM uses classes). Documented, not a code gap.
- **#6 --update-baseline laundering / #7 fail-open:** #6's silent-hand-edit path is already closed by the SHA-256 hashes (--update-baseline is a deliberate visible act); #7 is now closed (harness-canary below).

SHIPPED (the genuinely-doable items):
- **check #8 (`cheat-gate/check_bound_emit.py`):** AST-based commit-time tripwire for a static `sourceMode='bound'` EMIT in `converter_v2/` — closes the headline mirror-cheat's only commit-time gap (check #5/check_no_mirror is post-clone-only). AST so docstrings/comments describing the cheat aren't flagged; scoped to the converter (not the gate infra, which legitimately references 'bound'). Baseline-clean (0 today; tripwire for the future). 5 tests.

## 2026-06-21 — D240: F5 gates HARDENED after an adversarial council found a fatal soundness hole + bypass surfaces

**D240 — Bean directed an `/adversarial-council` on the F5 commits. A 5-persona panel (fact-checked per STOP-15 — all 3 deadliest findings confirmed true ground truth, unlike the F6 council) found the gates were architecturally sound but NOT yet a hard barrier. Fixed the convergent must-fixes + all small items this session; committed `cacde1a9`.**

The council's convergent headline: a careless future session could keep a gate GREEN while a real regression shipped. Fixed:
- **FATAL (coverage_check soundness):** the UNACCOUNTED join was tier/media-BLIND — `bucketed` keyed on `(selector,property)` while the draft keyed on `(selector,property,tier)`, so a declaration dropped at a non-base breakpoint reported UNACCOUNTED=0. The "no-silent-drop guarantee" was hollow for responsive CSS (the pipeline's whole point). Added media/tier to BOTH sides of the join → surfaced **19 previously-hidden cross-tier drops** (now baselined; a real regression on them now fails).
- **check_no_mirror count-blindness:** a baselined `(slug,class)` pair could recur N times (real regression) and pass GREEN. Baseline is now `{key: max-count}` + SHA-256 hash; a count regression fails.
- **check-converter-cheats #2 vacuous pass:** the NAMED violation `_SUFFIX_ATTR_OVERRIDES` (tuple keys) was silently skipped. Now detects tuple-keyed CSS-prop dicts (catches it + `_ATTR_NAME_OVERRIDES`).
- **check #6:** removed the hardcoded `_LAYOUT_PROP_RE` pre-filter (itself an R-22-1 violation defeating its own DB cross-join). **check #4:** `_BP_SUFFIX_MAP` scan now walks the whole orchestrator tree.
- **Self-blessing:** hashed the 3 unhashed baselines (cheat-gate / coverage / check_no_mirror) — a hand-edit is now caught (excluded-gate already had this).
- **Universal-floor wiring (the convergent STOP-6 finding):** the 4 static gates now run in `.githooks/pre-commit` (SHARED, fires on a real terminal `git commit`, not just CC sessions — verified firing on this session's commit). `f5-commit-gate.py` hardened: matcher catches `git -C`/global-flag commits; `[gates-ok]` now REQUIRES a reason (bare token no longer bypasses).
- **integration_error** in coverage_check now FAILS `--check` (was silently scored 0). **pytest.ini** (`--import-mode=importlib`) fixes the combined-pytest collision.

539 tests green (per-dir + combined-in-one-run now works). convert.py untouched (D-MODULAR). Lesson captured: [[verify-subagent-test-claims-from-canonical-cwd]] + the cross-tier soundness pattern.

**STILL DEFERRED (genuinely large/architectural — `P-F5-RESIDUALS`, NOT small tasks):** F3-RUNTIME (the LANDED leg); css_router D1 `attr_path` media-axis (the gate-side join now catches the symptom, but css_router still collapses same-property/different-media into one D1 entry — rebuild-scope); CSS shorthand decomposition in the ledger; a commit-time STATIC `sourceMode='bound'` scan (check #5 is post-clone-only); inline-style bucketing; a guard against `--update-baseline` laundering (the hash stops hand-edits; --update-baseline is still a deliberate visible path); fail-open canary/heartbeat.

## 2026-06-21 — D238: F5 STOP-6 closed — anti-mirror gate now auto-runs on every clone

**D238 — The smallest remaining F5 piece shipped: the clone orchestrator now wires the R-22-15 anti-mirror gate so it actually runs on every clone, closing the STOP-6 overclaim risk (a gate that existed + was baselined + tested but was never invoked).**

SHIPPED + on `main` (commit `2341e761`):
- **Wire** (`sgs-clone-orchestrator.py`): `main()` now invokes `pipeline-stage-gate.py <run_dir>` immediately after `stage_9_report()` writes `extract.json`, BEFORE media-sideload / deploy / +REGISTER. A clone that introduces a NEW mirror-cheat (draft-class container or bound sourceMode not in the baseline) HARD-HALTS (`sys.exit`) before it can reach the live page. The gate reads `extract.json` deterministically, so it runs identically in every `--mode` (unlike the autonomy gate). 13 legacy violations stay grandfathered; only NEW ones halt. New `--skip-stage-gate` flag (default OFF) for diagnostics.
- **Bug found + fixed by the wire**: a redundant local `import subprocess` inside `main()` (deploy-target branch) made `subprocess` function-local for the whole function and shadowed the module-level import → the new gate call `UnboundLocalError`'d on the first real run. Removed the local re-import.
- **Acceptance proven (all 3 legs, not "call added")**: (a) a real mamas-munches clone fires the gate — `[stage-gate] anti-mirror gate passed`, exit 0; (b) a planted NEW violation (`sgs-planted__newviolation`) into a real run dir makes the orchestrator's exact gate command exit 1 with the NEW-blocking message; (c) the orchestrator does `sys.exit(gate_proc.returncode)` on non-zero. Gate A conformance 43/43 + foundation suite 409 (ledger 167 / oracle 181 / baseline 10 / db-consistency 51) + orchestrator tests 6/6 all green.
- **Decision — placement + always-on**: gate runs PRE-deploy (a mirror-cheat must halt before going live) and in ALL modes (it has no stubbed-signal weakness, so no draft-mode auto-skip). `--skip-stage-gate` is the only escape hatch.

NEXT (F5-remaining, per `P-F5-REMAINING`): the OTHER 4 F5 gates — `check-converter-cheats.py` (§7a), `generate-coverage-matrix.py` (§5), the pipeline-close ledger checker, the EXCLUDED-literal gate, the PreToolUse git hook. Each is its own `/brainstorming` → `/adversarial-council`/`/qc-council` → Bean design-gate → SDD → qc; do NOT batch (high-blast); per STOP-14 run each against current output first + baseline today's violations.

(2) device-tier mobile breakpoint `599→767` (unify with `sgs-cols-*` 767; tablet 1023 kept) → the **768/1024 documented standard**. `container/style.css` tablet `1024→1023`, block.json `0.2.0→0.2.1`.

DECISIONS / corrections (Bean-driven — the agent's wrong mental models, now guarded in docs):
- **Device-tier ≠ visual breakpoints** (Bean): the SGS Mobile/Tablet/Desktop attr system must use 768/1024 consistently; an arbitrary VISUAL breakpoint (`min-width:600`, WP-columns `781`) is legitimate + must NOT be blanket-changed. A Haiku blanket-sweep of all 599/600 broke WP's 781 column breakpoint → **reverted entirely**; only the device-tier wrapper+container fix kept.
- **Hardcoded wrapper defaults are CHEATS to remove, not blockers** (Bean): the agent framed the `!important` sgs-cols override + align default + fixed breakpoint as "4 blockers preventing the hero fold"; they are R-22-1 violations to delete. The pipeline transfers the draft's CSS faithfully; it never injects anticipated defaults.
- **Composites are NEVER a separate system** (Bean): hero uses the universal `SGS_Container_Wrapper` like every composite; per-block hacks are bugs.
- **Ground variant setups in the variant DB** (Bean): `variant_slots`/`blocks.variant_attr` DEFINE each variant's setup (sgs/hero split = gridTemplateColumns/splitGap/splitImage*); query, don't guess from attrs.
- New memory guards: `feedback_device_tier_vs_visual_breakpoints_are_distinct`, `feedback_wrapper_hardcoded_defaults_are_cheats_to_remove_not_blockers`, `feedback_ground_in_variant_db_for_variant_block_setups`, `feedback_empty_section_check_cv2_softfail_trace_first`, `feedback_l1_l2_l3_are_extraction_side_only_css_survives_regardless`. CLAUDE.md architecture rules added (3 new sections).

NEXT SESSION (Bean-scoped): the full grid/container-extraction rebuild — analyse `sgs/container` block.json + DB (variant_slots, property_suffixes, modifier_suffixes) + `SGS_Container_Wrapper` end-to-end, so the converter faithfully maps EVERY value the container can hold (and the draft's equivalent wrappers hold) into EVERY composite, with correct responsive. First concrete step = the hero fold (Stage 2: drop hero manual grid + `wrap_inner=false`, route grid through the now-faithful helper) → Stage 3 (product-card) → Stage 4 (remove `wrap_inner` option). - **nameFontWeight hardcode REVERTED (Bean directive):** the bridge made `nameFontWeight` reseed-durable by hardcoding its selector in `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` (`sgs-update-v2.py`). Bean rejected ANY hardcoded selector → the entry was removed entirely; zero hardcoded `nameFontWeight` selector across all 3 channels (override dict / fingerprints.json / migration). Finding: it still transfers for the conformance fixture via the generic `typography_css_to_attrs()` path (`db_lookup.py:1115`, property-suffix-driven) — the hack was largely unnecessary.
- **ARCHITECTURE DECISION (Bean-raised, the top next task): selector-seeding should be BLOCK-OWNED + AUTO-SEEDED, not hardcoded in `/sgs-update`.** ROOT FINDING (code-verified): assign-canonical's loop (`assign-canonical.py:485` `WHERE canonical_slot IS NULL`) AND the fingerprint-override channel BOTH skip `canonical_slot`-populated rows — so for the 5 testimonial styling attrs (canonical_slot populated) the ONLY channel that reaches them on reseed was the hardcoded `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` dict. The proper fix: declare per-attr selectors/aliases in `block.json` (extend the `scalarStylingLift` capability, same rails as `variants`/`containerKind`) + extend `/sgs-update` to seed `derived_selector` from it, COVERING canonical_slot-populated rows. Then block-owned, self-seeding, single-source, R-22-1 clean (no hardcoded Python selector dict). Rule-7 seeding-pipeline change → design-gate + council BEFORE build. The same audit applies to the other `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` selector entries (team-member/quoteStyle/ratingSize).
- **Spec-22 built_status TRUTH-SYNC (the stale-label disease the D224 lesson targets):** corrected with code-verified file:line — FR-22-5.1 PLANNED→BUILT (`convert.py:1805`), FR-22-5.3 PLANNED→BUILT/PARTIAL (`db_lookup.py:2400`, `convert.py:2523`), FR-22-4.1 gridItem* SHIPPED, FR-22-5 GF-B.2 noted, FR-22-20 PARTIAL=DATA-not-code (`convert.py:4661` variant code is universal), FR-22-5.2/FR-22-2.5 design-gate-deferred, FR-22-9 ABSENT (`db_lookup.py:256` hardcoded regex, no runtime uimax query). (A doc-sync subagent self-flagged 2 of my line-refs as pre-shift; corrected to the post-edit lines.)
- **NEXT:** (1) block.json-declared selector auto-seed (design-gate + council); (2) Bean deploy + live-verify the 4 shipped converter fixes on page 8; (3) the 3 deferred design-gate phases (array→child, breakpoints, D1 sidecar) each get a design session; (4) IN-E after the live-probe.

## 2026-06-13 (cloning thread) — D224: tag-role redesign RETIRED (duplicated built code); 5 OPEN-row fixes council-hardened phase-plan; testimonial-styling BRIDGE applied; unified element-pass council NO-GO

**D224 — A long design session that converged on "the routing is already BUILT; the OPEN rows are 5 small fixes; the testimonial fix is a 5-selector bridge, not a redesign." Two specs RETIRED before build; one bridge applied. Nothing committed/deployed yet.** Started as "verify D223's styling-lift renders on page 8" and pivoted through Bean's challenges into a routing-redesign exploration that the doc-review + code-analysis gates KILLED.

- **Tag-role child-routing redesign — RETIRED + DELETED** (doc removed 2026-06-13; full reasoning preserved in this entry). A 4-doc review + read-only code analysis (4 parallel agents + self-verify) found it DUPLICATED ratified-AND-BUILT mechanisms: FR-22-5.1 inherited-value resolution = BUILT (`convert.py:1737 _resolve_inherited_typography` — ancestor walk + text-align absence-override :1842); FR-22-5.3 cross-node box-CSS + name-free `attr_for_layer_property` = BUILT (`db_lookup.py:2400`); scalar content/styling lifts = BUILT (D212/D223). **The spec's `built_status:` labels were STALE.** The redesign also carried 3 factual errors (container_kind as router; canonical_slot as router; "let CSS inherit" — all contradicted by D194 / FR-22-5.1's emit-explicit-on-leaf).
- **5 OPEN-row fixes PHASE-PLANNED, council-hardened** (`.claude/plans/2026-06-13-clone-fix-converter-gaps-PHASE-PLAN.md`): (1) **GF-B.2** selector-matcher class-branch ignores descendant-combinator ancestor scope (`convert.py:619-622`; tag-branch :623-650 is correct) → cross-section CSS leak — FOUNDATIONAL, ~28 call sites, first; (2) **testimonial styling** = data-only (the bridge); (3) **IN-E** = inheritance BUILT but DROPS at gate `:1836` because info-box declares text-align via WP-native `supports.typography.textAlign`, not a `block_attributes` row; (4) **H-C1** = `_route_area_css_to_block_attrs` hard-excludes max-width (`:2307-2309`); (5) **IN-B** = no var() resolution anywhere, contentWidth set raw at `:5370`. A 6-persona `/adversarial-council` caught 2 BUILD-BREAKERS the page-8-only harness was blind to: a canonical_slot-pairing "populator" that would corrupt cta-section/icon/toc/team-member colour routing (DB slots mislabelled), and an IN-E gate-widen that would force `textAlign:left` onto ~16 supports-typography blocks site-wide. Revisions R1-R9 baked into the plan (route-around for H-C1, probe-first for IN-E, fingerprint not populator, GF-B.2 `.A.B` edge).
- **Testimonial-styling BRIDGE applied (uncommitted):** the 5 styling attrs got multi-alias `derived_selector`s matching the Mama's draft (`__text`/`__author`) via `tools/recogniser/data/fingerprints.json` + a dated migration (`migrations/2026-06-13-testimonial-selector-fingerprint-override.py` — the fingerprint channel is unreachable for `canonical_slot`-populated rows, so a migration sets them). Content + styling now resolve the SAME element. Close-out (full-reseed survival + golden rebaseline adding draft-faithful `nameColour=#5c4f46`) was in-flight at session close.
- **Unified element-pass — specced then council NO-GO + DELETED** (doc removed 2026-06-13; reasoning here). Bean's architecture ("resolve each element once, lift content+styling together") is sound, but a 3-persona council (read the code) ruled DON'T BUILD (ROI grade D): the bridge ALREADY makes content+styling share the element; the unified pass would add a new DB table (R-22-1 / no-parallel-infra — the per-attr `derived_selector` already encodes the grouping) + merge two live core functions (regression risk on team-member) for a guarantee already delivered. The slot data also can't group one element (`name`→`heading` alias, `reviewerName` own selector, `author`→`text` = three slots), so a fully-automatic pass is blocked regardless. Bean accepted the NO-GO.
- **Lesson (blub.db 353, 3 layers):** READ THE IMPLEMENTING SCRIPT before proposing/planning/critiquing ANY converter mechanism or asserting built/not-built — never trust spec `built_status:` labels, attr/column names, or "probably true" (a council/subagent finding is a hypothesis too). I invented canonical_slot-pairing + mis-called FR-22-5.1/5.3 unbuilt this way; the unified-pass council caught a recurrence (the spec wrongly claimed `reviewerName` "UNRESOLVED"). `[[feedback_read_the_script_before_proposing_converter_mechanism]]`.
- **NEXT:** the council-hardened 5-row phase plan, GF-B.2 first (foundational). SP-C drops (not a defect); SP-D.1 (star-size) / BR-B (imageId) / FP-P (full-width) parked as pure extraction maps.

## 2026-06-13 (cloning thread) — D221: mobile-nav drawer-InnerBlocks save bug fixed + team-member name mis-classification fixed via durable ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES — both has_inner_blocks overrides removed

**D221 — Two A/B/C universalisation follow-ups closed (commit `e20f0bd5`, pushed `main`).** (1) **sgs/mobile-nav** `save: () => null` silently dropped the drawer custom-content InnerBlocks on every save (render.php consumes `$content`); restored `save: () => <InnerBlocks.Content/>` + `vNull` deprecation (posts saved under the null shape validate) + version 3.1.0→3.1.1 + registered in `BlockDeprecationsTest`. (2) **sgs/team-member** ROOT CAUSE: `equivalent_block_for('sgs/team-member','name')` returned `sgs/heading` (a dead child render.php ignores) because assign-canonical mapped the block's OWN scalar `__name` element to `canonical_slot='heading'` (a block-equivalent slot) + `role='text-content'` (content-bearing). render.php renders `name` as a SCALAR element; only `sgs/social-icons` is a child. **Fix = a NEW durable, version-controlled `ATTR_CLASSIFICATION_OVERRIDES` layer** in `sgs-update-v2.py` (Stage 1 sub-step C, applied AFTER `_run_canonical_assignment` so it is the FINAL writer + survives every /sgs-update; mirrors the `HAS_INNER_BLOCKS_OVERRIDES` pattern B established) forcing `team-member.name role=NULL` → `equivalent_block_for` returns None (scalar). Bean chose the code-override over a raw DB UPDATE (reproducible on a fresh build). With both root causes fixed, the two `has_inner_blocks` overrides (mobile-nav=1, team-member=0) are REMOVED — both dicts (`sgs-update-v2.py` + `check-composition-sync.py`) now empty. **Verified (ground-truth, not assumed):** composition-sync gate OK across 74 blocks; `equivalent_block_for` name/photo/role/bio all `null`; team-member `has_inner_blocks` correctly derives 1; mobile-nav build green (dead-control + sync gates pass). **Lesson:** a `has_inner_blocks` override can MASK a deeper per-attr `equivalent_block_for` mis-classification — fix the classification durably, don't pin the symptom (`[[feedback_has_inner_blocks_override_can_mask_attr_misclassification]]`). **Remaining A/B/C follow-ups:** the full name-free align layer-router (own council session) + IN-F notice-banner content. Non-visual commit → visual-diff gate bypassed via its documented exemption (Bean-approved).

## 2026-06-12 (theme thread) — D217: Spec 30 P2 Step 10b — back-in-stock notify-me capture SHIPPED + live-verified; reusable Cloudflare Turnstile primitive added

**D217 — P-WC-NOTIFY-ME-CAPTURE built, live-verified on the canary, and committed on `feat/spec30-p2-step10`.** Step 10b of `2026-06-11-spec30-p2-differentiators-shop-schema.md`. Bean directed (2026-06-12) "build it now" + "don't go overboard on the legal side — get consent and use Cloudflare Turnstile for spam safety". Result = a **proportionate** capture, NOT a maximalist PII red-team:
- **NEW reusable `SGS\Blocks\Turnstile`** (`includes/class-turnstile.php`) — Cloudflare Turnstile primitive: `Settings → SGS Turnstile` (operator site/secret keys), `enqueue_script()`, `widget_html()`, server `verify()` (siteverify via `wp_remote_post`). **Graceful skip when unconfigured** (verify→true, widget→''); the rate-limit is then the sole guard. Net-new — Turnstile did NOT previously exist anywhere in theme/plugin/forms-engine (Bean believed it did; surfaced + built). Reusable by the SGS forms engine later (currently has no bot protection).
- **NEW `SGS\Blocks\Stock_Notify`** (`includes/class-stock-notify.php` + `stock-notify-admin.php`) — public `POST /sgs/v1/notify/subscribe`, mirrors `class-demand-analytics.php`. Fail-fast chain (live-verified order): **nonce(403) → consent strict-`true`(400) → is_email(400) → published-product/IDOR(404) → rate-limit 5/IP/hr(429) → Turnstile::verify(403) → store(200)**. Rate-limit is BEFORE Turnstile (the external siteverify) so spam can't amplify outbound CF calls; cheap validations stay first so a fat-fingered email isn't counted. Stores ONLY `{email, ts}` in `_sgs_stock_notify` post-meta, dedup by email, cap 1000; raw IP NEVER stored (SHA-256+salt transient key only). `manage_woocommerce`-gated read-only admin meta-box, all values `esc_html`.
- **buybox UI** — notify form rendered inside the existing `sgs/product-card` Interactivity wrapper, shown ONLY out-of-stock via `data-wp-bind--hidden="context.inStock"` (a pure READ of existing context — zero new store actions/state). Un-ticked + `required` consent checkbox + privacy-policy link (`get_privacy_policy_url()` guarded). Submit handled by a self-contained `notify-view.js` ES module (no Interactivity import, status via `textContent` only, X-WP-Nonce header, resets Turnstile on error). `notifyEnabled` attr (default true); `notifyMeLabel` now LIVE (removed from dead-control baseline → `accepted:[]`). buybox `version` 1.0.4→1.1.0.
- **Live-verified (canary, R-22-11, via curl + guest nonce):** front-page 200 (no fatal); no-nonce→403; consent=false→400; bad email→400; draft 1017→404; bogus id→404; valid→200 + `{email,ts}` stored; dedup (resend stored once); rate-limit 6th well-formed→429; Turnstile always-fail-secret→403, empty-token-while-configured→403 (fail-closed), always-pass-secret→200; PDP DOM shows the form hidden-when-in-stock with consent `required`/un-checked + privacy link + Turnstile widget + `notify-view.js` enqueued. Canary restored clean (keys emptied, test meta deleted, RL cleared, one-shot removed). QC = inline security review + cross-family haiku rater (all controls PASS). **Operator action for go-live: paste real Cloudflare Turnstile keys** (FR-30-13 checklist item). Memory: proportionate-consent-plus-turnstile over PII-red-team-theatre.

## 2026-06-12 (theme thread) — D219: Spec 30 P2 Step 10a — gallery-variation-swap DEFERRED (keep static-per-variation) [renumbered from D216 on merge — the co-active cloning thread held D216 = A/B/C universalisation]

**D219 — P-WC-GALLERY-VARIATION-SWAP resolved: DEFER the driven gallery swap; keep static-per-variation.** Step 10a of `2026-06-11-spec30-p2-differentiators-shop-schema.md`. The two options were (1) **driven** — selecting a variation pipes `selectedImageId` from the buybox bridge into WooCommerce's gallery Interactivity context so the whole gallery carousel swaps live; (2) **static-per-variation** (current). Decision = defer (1) for three converging reasons: (a) **no fixture to validate it** — the canary's only variable fixture (product 540, the 48-SKU box) has no per-variation image galleries, so the driven path cannot be live-verified per R-22-11; (b) **version-fragile coupling** — the driven path binds to WooCommerce's internal gallery Interactivity store shape, which violates the "framework must work on ANY WC version/install" principle (CLAUDE.md Architecture rules); (c) **MVP-first + already-handled main image** — WooCommerce core already swaps the single featured image when a chosen variation carries its own image, so the launch-critical behaviour exists for free; the driven *gallery* swap is a pure enhancement. Revisit only when a real client ships a product with true per-variation galleries AND a fixture exists. No build; `notifyMeLabel` baseline untouched by this sub-step. Bean-approved build-now scope (2026-06-12) covers 10b only.

## 2026-06-11 (theme thread) — D213: Spec 30 P2 Gate A + Gate B SHIPPED + merged to main; shop archive built on WC's canonical Product Collection + Filters structure

**D213 — FR-30-3 shop archive complete; root cause of the empty/broken filters was hand-authored block markup diverging from WC 10.8's canonical structure (NOT a CSS or hydration bug).** Two grounded defects, both fixed against WooCommerce's own `templates/blockified/archive-product.html`: (1) each `woocommerce/product-filter-*` block was authored SELF-CLOSING, omitting its required inner control block — WC's parent filter blocks server-render their inner control and the view modules only wire existing markup, so empty markup = empty panels. Fixed by nesting `product-filter-price-slider` / `product-filter-chips` / `product-filter-checkbox-list` per the WC `ancestor` declarations + correcting `displayStyle` from the invalid `"chips"` to the full block name `"woocommerce/product-filter-chips"`. (2) the `woocommerce/product-collection` block lacked `tagName:"div"` + its wrapper `<div class="wp-block-woocommerce-product-collection">` + `queryId:0`/`isProductCollectionBlock:true`; WC's Renderer regex-injects `data-wp-router-region` into the collection's first `<div>` only when `forcePageReload` is false, so no wrapper div = no client-side router region = filters update the URL but never re-query the grid. Fixed by matching WC's canonical collection markup → instant filtering verified live (5→3 products in 253ms, no reload). Also: `sgs/product-card` loop-context binding (`usesContext:postId`, absint-guarded, only fills when no explicit productId) renders SGS cards inside the core Product Collection (FR-30-3 Option C); equal-height cards + `.price-row` `margin-top:auto` baseline-aligns CTAs (theme CSS, `.sgs-shop-layout`-scoped); accessible mobile drawer (`assets/js/sgs-shop-filters.js`); the mobile "Filter" toggle reuses primary-button tokens (FINDING: there is NO global `.btn`/`.btn-primary` in the theme — those styles are `.product-card`-scoped; parked P-NO-GLOBAL-BUTTON-COMPONENT). NEW `sgs/collapsible-text` block: operator SEO copy with accessible read-more (full text always SSR'd via CSS line-clamp not display:none; empty renders nothing; labels i18n'd via server-emitted `data-read-more`/`data-read-less`). axe-clean shop content (1 pre-existing core nav-block `list` issue tracked for FR-30-13). **D208 — The WC page-type solution is DESIGNED + sign-off (post-compact `/brainstorming` + `/research-buddies`, 3 parallel research agents: WC block ecosystem 2026 / shop+PDP UX / ecommerce schema). 8 decisions recorded; the BUILD is delegated to the theme thread.** **Canonical spec: `.claude/specs/30-SGS-WOOCOMMERCE-PAGE-TYPES.md` (Spec 30, FR-30-1…FR-30-12, docscore 100% A)** — the theme thread builds from Spec 30.
