Research corrected 4 brief assumptions: **(a) the cart DRAWER is core** (Mini-Cart block, Blocks 10.1+, adjustable width) — style only, do NOT build [reverses the brief]; **(b) product search + searchable type-to-find filter are NOT core** (paid Product Search extension only); **(c) baked fake reviews are ILLEGAL** (UK DMCC Act, in force 2026-04-06, fines ≤£300k/10% turnover, displaying trader liable) — the draft's fake reviews are a legal liability; **(d) FAQ schema is dead** (Google drops the appearance 2026-05-07) + SearchAction retired (2024-11). The 8 decisions: **D-1** cloned product page targets the WC **single-product block template** (`is_product()` on a real `product` post), NOT a WP Page — *this is the pipeline gate*; **D-2** **custom SGS search + searchable-filter blocks** (framework asset, no per-client licence) [Bean pick]; **D-3** **keep the SGS option-picker**, bind to WC variation data, write via Store API `add-item` [Bean pick — flag: confirm `@woocommerce/block-data` variation-read selector before build]; **D-4** **use core Mini-Cart drawer**, style only [Bean pick]; **D-5** **Trustpilot/verified-buyer reviews**, never static fakes [DMCC-forced]; **D-6** use core **Product Gallery** (variation-aware since 9.9, Beta; multi-image-per-variation out of scope); **D-7** use core **Add-to-Cart+Options** as the cart-write chassis under the SGS picker; **D-8** schema per the solution table — PDP `Product`+`Offer`(+`returnPolicyCountry` now required)+`aggregateRating`/genuine `review`+`BreadcrumbList`, ONE Product node; shop = `BreadcrumbList`+URL-only `ItemList`; cart/checkout/account = none+`noindex`; sitewide `Organization`(org-level shipping/returns canonical)+`WebSite`(no SearchAction); **drop FAQPage**. Content-vs-structure rule unchanged (`allergen-*`/`topping-dairy`/`trial-note` → generic slots, never framework vocab). My Account stays classic (no block alt in core), deferred + CSS-only. **THIS thread:** homepage cloning continues independently (the `fold_eligible` fix + Step C label correction); product-page cloning is GATED on D-1 (deploy to the product template, not `page:144`) — parked until the theme thread ships the single-product template + SGS blocks. **Theme thread builds Part B** (theme support + templates + custom search/filter + option-picker→WC binding + price-display + archive UX + schema audit; all responsive 375/768/1440).

## 2026-06-11 (cloning thread) — Stage-1 didn't land (fold_eligible root cause); routing-categorisation design; gap fact-check; product-page = WooCommerce page type (D207)

**D207 — four linked findings this session.** (1) **Stage-1 Commits 2/3/4 (D201/D202) are emit-green but did NOT change the live page** — root cause is `_process_container_children`'s `fold_eligible = len(element_children)==1` (`convert.py:4435`): the hero's `__content`+`__media` = 2 children, so `__content` never dissolves, emits as a nested BEM-classed `sgs/container` (the double-nesting Bean saw), and the Commit-2 cross-node CSS routing — which lives INSIDE the fold branch — never fires (the dropped hero `contentPadding`). The grid-CSS-driven fix (treat `display:grid` direct descendants as grid items, identified by `grid-template-areas` names, not by child count) supersedes the count proxy. (2) **`ROUTING-CATEGORISATION-DESIGN.md` APPROVED** — DB categorisation layer (slots/aliases → canonical_slot → role → property_suffixes) + per-element/per-breakpoint responsive-CSS routing + grid-awareness; corrected block model = **preset (`cardStyle`/`style`/`variant`/`pillStyle`) + child-block typography + container-mirror (native WP `supports`)**, NOT per-property attrs. (3) **Step-C gap fact-check: ~30 of 68 labels were FALSE** — covered by native `supports.__experimentalBorder`/`color.background`/`spacing`/`typography.textAlign`, presets, child-block typography, or shipped fixes (B6/E9/C7/D8); `ghost` already aliases `button-outline`. (4) **The Mama's product-page draft is a WooCommerce PAGE TYPE, not a homepage re-author** (6-persona adversarial-council, convergent): ~80% existing SGS blocks + a missing page-type chassis (no `single-product` template, no `add_theme_support('woocommerce')`). **DECISION: lean on WooCommerce's native blocks for the commerce machinery (gallery/add-to-cart/cart/checkout/collection/search/filters); custom-build only the differentiated UX (pill configurator, value-ladder, trust/brand styling). Content-specific terms (`allergen-*`/`topping-dairy`/`trial-note`) map to GENERIC slots — never enter framework vocab. The WC page-type SOLUTION is designed in the cloning thread (post-compact /brainstorming + /research-buddies); the BUILD is delegated to the theme thread; the product-page clone is gated on the page-vs-product-template decision.** Brief: `.claude/reports/wave2/WOOCOMMERCE-PAGE-TYPE-BRIEF-2026-06-11.md`.

## 2026-06-10 (theme thread) — Bean-reported admin label overlap fixed: WC panel CSS force-columns EVERY label (D201)

**D201 — Bean's R-22-13 eye caught real admin-UI breakage my visual pass mis-triaged (`fe7e4fff`).** His screenshot showed the P3 radios/checkboxes/pence labels painting ON TOP of each other, the Wave-2 attestation label squeezed to a 3-line 150px column, and a clipped orphan section label. ROOT CAUSE (computed-style proven, /systematic-debugging): **WooCommerce's product-panel CSS applies `float:left;width:150px;margin-left:-150px;display:block` to EVERY `<label>` in the panel — PANEL-WIDE, not just `p.form-field` rows** — it is designed for the single left-column field label; any ADDITIONAL nested label (per radio/checkbox/input) collapses onto the same 150px column. The D200 design rater HAD flagged this as "crowding/not WC two-column" and it was mis-filed as deferred polish — measurement-vs-eye rule honoured: Bean's report stood, the measurement set was extended (bounding-rect overlap counting), the defect confirmed at every viewport. FIXES (2 parallel sonnet fixers + orchestrator): (1) inline resets `float:none;width:auto;margin:…` on every nested label (WC's rule carries no !important — inline wins; note float blockifies display, and WC's width/margin hit FLEX ITEMS too even though flex ignores float); (2) the "Manual price overrides" SECTION label needed the reset too — its div lacks the 150px column padding so WC's negative margin clipped it off the left edge (the fixer's claim that the rule wouldn't target it was WRONG — live computed styles settled it); (3) the Wave-2 attestation row (`woocommerce_wp_checkbox`) is a DIFFERENT mechanism — its legally-worded label was simply too long for WC's column; WC-idiomatic fix: short column label ("Single-unit price is genuine"), the full first-person confirmation moved to the description beside the checkbox (legal meaning preserved; tick still confirms it). Live-verified: 0 overlapping label pairs across all 3 groups; attestation 24px single-line (was 72px); panel-wide clipped-label sweep = zero. ROUND-2 (Bean R-22-13, same day, `ffadce85`): two more WC-panel float mechanisms live-measured + fixed — (4) a HALF-WIDTH `form-row-first` wrapper with no `form-row-last` partner lets the NEXT row float up beside it (the pounds field's help-tip painted onto the attestation label); rows in this panel stay `form-row-full` unless deliberately paired. (5) WC FLOATS the panel's selects/inputs too — a `display:block` description after a floated `width:100%` select stays on the SAME line with its text wrapping around the float ("Which" orphan); bound the select (400px/max-width:100%) AND give the description `clear:both`. LESSON: any hand-rolled markup inside the WC product panel must assume EVERY label gets column treatment — reset nested labels explicitly, and keep `woocommerce_wp_*` field labels SHORT (sentences go in description).

The flagging doc predates the guard (committed 2026-06-04). Marked RESOLVED in parking.

## 2026-06-10 (cloning thread) — Root-cause REFRAME + routing-categorisation design + step-C stress test (D203)

**D203 — the Stage-1 converter changes do NOT land on the live page; root cause found; new DB-driven routing design ratified-in-principle; step-C stress test complete.** Live-DOM verification (clone-parity.js + Playwright on page 8) proved Commits 2/3/4 changed the EMIT but produced ZERO change on the rendered page (0 fixed / 118 stayed vs the 06-07 baseline; 28/28 headings still centre; hero content padding still on the outer section). **Root cause (single, evidenced via `convert-trace-b*.jsonl`):** `fold_eligible = len(element_children) == 1` (`_process_container_children:4435`) counts the hero's `__content` + `__media` = 2 → False → `__content` never folds → emits as a nested BEM-classed `sgs/container` (the double-nesting Bean saw in the editor) → Commit-2's cross-node CSS routing (which lives INSIDE the fold branch) is unreachable for the hero. The `__media` is a scalar-media column (consumed to an attr, emits no markup) but inflates the fold count. The trust-bar's 4 columns "work" because trust-bar is `has_inner_blocks=0` (G3 array path), a different mechanism — NOT proof multi-child folds. **The docs specify the correct end-state for every shape (container/composite/array) but are SILENT on the co-located content-wrapper + scalar-media-column fold-eligibility interaction (triangulated by 4 doc-reader agents).** **New design (`reports/wave2/ROUTING-CATEGORISATION-DESIGN.md`, Bean-approved in principle):** route by the DB categorisation layer — `slots.aliases` (element id) → `canonical_slot`/`role` (typed-attr-vs-child) → `property_suffixes` (box-CSS, name-free) → `modifier_suffixes` (breakpoints/variants) + grid-awareness (read `display:grid`/`grid-template-areas` from the CSS, not a child count). Now carries per-element, per-breakpoint responsive-CSS routing + the corrected block model (preset attrs `cardStyle`/`style`/`variant`/`pillStyle` + child-block typography + container-mirror — NOT per-property attrs). **Step C (DONE):** both drafts mapped layer-by-layer with full responsive CSS (`reports/wave2/STEP-C-LAYOUT-MAPPING-2026-06-10.md`); gap register (`STEP-C-STRESS-TEST-2026-06-10.md`). Open work = 3 buckets: **⚙ 9 converter rules G1–G9** · **➕ DB data** (aliases/tokens/suffixes/variant_attr) · **🧱 block-side** (container-mirror under-shares; testimonial + notice-banner need rework; product-card editor bugs) — block bucket handed to the theme thread via `reports/wave2/STEP-C-BLOCK-FIXES-PROMPT.md`. **Corrected mistake (Bean caught):** the earlier "built-in-element blocks missing per-property attrs" framing was wrong — those blocks use preset + child-typography + mirror; live editor review is ground truth over DB attr-name guessing. **Branch `feat/stage1-converter-core` stays OPEN** (justified exception to the merge-to-main gate): the converter rebuild is mid-flight and the step-C analysis redefines the approach (the existing Commits 2/3/4 may be revised once G1–G9 land); Commit 4 also gated on Bean's R-22-13 live sign-off.

Full% (~54%) is the known structural penalty for not class-mirroring (D195: content% is the gauge, not full%). ## 2026-06-09 (cloning thread) — Wrapper CSS routing is name-free, not canonical_slot-keyed; content* attrs tagged `content`/`layout` for convention-consistency (D194)

**D194 — `canonical_slot` is NOT the structural-CSS routing key; draft wrapper box-CSS routes name-free via layer-detection + `property_suffixes`. The Wave-2 "Commit 0a canonical_slot backfill as routing gate" conception is retired. The 41 content-area attrs are tagged `canonical_slot='content'` + `role='layout'` for metadata-consistency only. Bean-approved 2026-06-09.** Design session traced the hand-off "Commit 0a backfill" to a wrong premise. Evidence-grounded findings: (1) `canonical_slot`'s only behavioural job (FR-22-2.1, `db_lookup.py:1995 equivalent_block_for`) is the CONTENT fork (emit child InnerBlock vs scalar), **gated by `role`** — confirmed `db_lookup.py:2034-2054`. (2) Structural box CSS (`contentWidth`/`contentPadding*`/`mediaPadding*`/`gridItem*`) routes by **layer-prefix + `property_suffixes`**, name-free — matching the already-correct **Method-2 plans** (`plans/archive/2026-06-04-method2-converter-lift-*`); the newer **Wave-2 Stage docs** had reintroduced canonical_slot-as-routing-key (the conflict this decision resolves). (3) Fake wrapper divs (`__inner`/`__content`/`__card-inner`) fold structurally (FR-22-4.1 slug-None direct descendant) by CSS signature, never by name — backed by **D85** which already removed `inner`/`content`/`body-row` aliases for causing wrong collapse. (4) **Tier A corrected:** child-block vs scalar vs array = `canonical_slot` + `role` + `attr_type` together (spec FR-22-2.1 omits the role/type gating the running code already applies). **Implementation (DB-only):** added a bare `content` element-slot (`scope='element'`, `aliases=[]`, `standalone_block=NULL` — empty aliases by design, never matched against draft classes) via `seed-slot-synonyms.py`; tagged the 41 `contentWidth`/`contentPadding*`/`contentMaxWidth*` rows `content`/`layout`. **`/sgs-update` is the deterministic mechanism — no manual seed script.** Investigation confirmed `assign-canonical.py` (run automatically by `/sgs-update` Stage 1) tags these rows `content`/`layout` deterministically once the `content` slot row + the `Width`/`Padding`→`layout` `property_suffixes` rows exist (all present). The throwaway `seed-canonical-slots.py` was therefore **deleted as redundant parallel infra** (the DB values it wrote persist; `/sgs-update` maintains + extends them). **Side effect (accepted):** `assign-canonical` also labelled 20 other same-stem rows `content` — 6 layout/enum (correct) + 13 `text-content` (core/* off-roster + `sgs/heading content`); inert because `content` has no `standalone_block` (same dual-use pattern as `media`: one slot, `role` disambiguates layout-box from text). **Guard:** `content` must never gain a `standalone_block` without re-auditing those 13 rows. **No 3-layer canonical split (Bean, confirmed):** the 3 layers (OUTER/CONTENT/GRID) already map onto existing vocabulary — OUTER=NULL (root box), CONTENT=`content`, GRID=existing `gap`/`column`/`gridItem*` — so splitting `content` into container/content/grid canonicals would re-couple `canonical_slot` to routing (contra this decision) + overlap; the layers stay a converter-side routing concept, not DB values. **No draft `content-width` rename (Bean clarified):** the draft's direct-descendant inner-wrapper `max-width`+`margin:auto` (e.g. `.sgs-x__inner{max-width:1040px;margin:0 auto}`) IS the source the converter maps to the block's `contentWidth` attr (FR-22-21 step 3); `max-width` stays (correct + universal for scraped drafts), the mapping is documented, not renamed. `sgs/container` needs no hand-seeding — `/sgs-update` tidies any remaining attr gaps. Design-gate doc: `.claude/reports/wave2/WRAPPER-CSS-ROUTING-DESIGN-GATE.md`. `assign-canonical.py` unchanged (preserves explicit values via `WHERE canonical_slot IS NULL` + COALESCE, live-verified). NO pixel-diff gate needed — metadata-only, zero converter-output change. (CLONING thread; theme co-active on main — path-scoped commits.)

## 2026-06-08 (theme/blocks thread) — sgs* editor-extension attrs registered server-side; ServerSideRender block-renderer 400 fixed (D191)

**D191 — The editor extensions' `sgs*` attributes are now registered server-side, fixing "Error loading block: Invalid parameter(s): attributes" on every ServerSideRender-preview block (product-card bound, trustpilot-reviews, business-info, content-collection). qc-council verdict `validated-shipped` (3 cross-model raters: no regressions, real renders, complete affected set).** Mechanism: JS `blocks.registerBlockType` adds the `sgs*` family client-side; ServerSideRender sends them to `GET /wp/v2/block-renderer/<block>`, validated with `additionalProperties:false` against the server schema (block.json only) → the first unregistered `sgs*` attr is rejected (product-card on `sgsAnimation`, trustpilot on `sgsAnimationDelay`). Fix: a `register_block_type_args` filter (`plugins/sgs-blocks/includes/extension-attrs-rest-register.php`) merges a generated `sgs*` schema onto every className-supporting block; the 46-attr list is generated from the extension JS (single source of truth) by `scripts/generate-extension-attributes.js` (wired into prebuild/prestart; a `.githooks/pre-commit --check` guard — via `node.exe` — blocks committing a stale list). Live-verified all 4 blocks return 200 on the sandybrown canary (REST replay + live editor, 0 console errors). Commits `8694aebc` + `df691994` (path-scoped, pushed to main). ## 2026-06-07 (cloning thread) — parity2 draft-centric fidelity verifier BUILT + rewired + QC'd (D183)

**D183 — A new fidelity verifier `parity2` replaces the three over-reporting instruments (pixel-diff, old clone-parity, leftover-buckets). The DRAFT is the 100% denominator; it measures CONTENT + LAYOUT + CSS transfer, class-AGNOSTIC.** _(Commits `2ddea70b`/`a2336198`/`486f8f9f`. Built via `/dispatching-parallel-agents` + `/qc`. Design: `.claude/reports/2026-06-07-draft-centric-parity-verifier-design.md`. Files: `plugins/sgs-blocks/scripts/parity2/*.py` + `clone-parity.js --dump-captures`.)_

- **Why the old tools failed (all over-report, different ways):** pixel-diff judges painted pixels (photos/sub-pixel noise); old clone-parity pairs by DOM path → rewards a div-by-div MIRROR + penalises genuine conversion; leftover-buckets is a block-SLOT census → flags every slot the draft never set as `extraction_failed` (the perfectly-converted trust-bar logged 48 false failures). stage-2 + extract.json ARE reliable.
- **The model (Bean-directed):** enumerate everything the draft contains = 100%; per draft node find its EQUIVALENT clone node by own-text anchors + Lowest-Common-Ancestor tree-alignment (absorbs renames + WP wrapper divs), class-agnostic; report content/layout/css transfer. Fate-aware (emit-block / lift-attr / fold-parent / chrome via the converter's own DB tables).
- **Key calibrations:** content via word-overlap ≥70% (the `/qc` fix — verbatim containment had false negatives); raw width/height de-weighted (layout CONSEQUENCE); **LAYOUT props scored as a separate WEIGHTED signal** (Bean's catch — they were diluted in the overall css%, hiding the trust-bar's real badge-grid difference). Reports content%/layout%/css%/full%.
- **Validated:** trust-bar content 100% / layout 95% / css 96% / full 93% (QC-verified trustworthy: 4 badges → 4 distinct clone nodes). Honestly surfaces mirrored sections (brand layout 48%). NOT yet wired into `/sgs-clone` (next-session Task 1).

- **E1 (FR-27-E1):** new `includes/class-product-schema.php` emits a `ProductGroup` + `AggregateOffer` (offerCount=true 48) + a ≤16 KB trimmed `hasVariant` sample (low+high price anchors always kept). Reads commerce data ONLY from `Product_Manifest::build()` (SEC-1; CI-grep asserts zero `wc_get_price_to_display`/`get_children`), price ALWAYS inc-VAT (SEC-2), HEX-flag JSON encode (SEC-3), variesBy closed-enum with unmapped axes→additionalProperty (SEC-8). Manifest extended to v6 (incMinor/sku/gtin/saleEndDate per combo + per-axis variesBy). **seo-schema agent: Rich Results 0 errors PASS.** A cross-model security review found + I fixed one BLOCKER (min()/max() empty-array fatal in wp_head). Dismissed two agent "errors" that contradicted the spec: "add flavor to variesBy" (not in Google's structured-data enum; SEC-8 → additionalProperty is correct) and a rolling priceValidUntil (FR-27-E1 forbids fabricated dates). GTINs + brand are fixture/client data, correctly omitted not fabricated.
- **E2 (FR-27-E2):** WP core already canonicalises `?attribute_*`→parent (verified), so the default needs no code and SGS must NOT add a 2nd canonical. Built the OPT-IN only: `Product_Canonical` (`get_canonical_url` filter) overrides to a single high-intent variation when a per-card `indexVariationUrl` is set, URL built from the variation's own server-side `get_attributes()` (SEC-7, no `$_GET`/`add_query_arg`), IDOR-safe (variation must belong to the bound product), defers to an SEO plugin (SEC-9). New additive `indexVariationUrl` attr + "Advanced SEO" inspector control (Bound-only; Typed clones untouched). All paths tested (default/override/reject).
- **E3 (FR-27-E3):** OG product tags in configurator-head (inc-VAT price, SEC-2, inside the SEC-9 guard; E1 JSON-LD stays outside it). New `Product_Sitemap` fixes WP-core product `<lastmod>` to MAX(parent, all variations) so a variation price change triggers recrawl (SEC-6, transient+purge, SEC-9 defer). Breadcrumb = placed the existing `sgs/breadcrumbs` block on canary page 589 → valid BreadcrumbList.
- **F1 (FR-27-F1):** no-JS curl shows price + availability + JSON-LD (price+availability) + OG — PASS.
- **Regression (self-introduced, fixed same session):** E1's per-combo schema fields + the E1 parent-image fix (which populated every combo's gallery fallback) grew the 48-SKU manifest 23→31.8 KB, tripping the product-card's M-C9 24 KB seeded-context cap → the interactive configurator fell back to the static "From" card (pills gone). Root-caused via live DOM (`type="radio"` 16→0). Fix: render.php seeds a LEAN per-combo subset — strips the 4 JSON-LD-only fields (view.js reads none, verified) + drops <2-image galleries (view.js falls back to `combo.imageUrl`). Full manifest stays server-side (SEC-1). Bound-only; pills restored + visually confirmed. Memory `manifest-growth-can-trip-capped-client-seed`.
- **Decision (Bean CONFIRMED 2026-06-05): the per-variation `<image:image>` sitemap is DESCOPED.** Spec called it "mandatory" but WP_Sitemaps has no clean image-namespace support and Google deprecated image sitemaps as a distinct signal; the E1 ProductGroup schema already exposes every variation image and the page is crawled, so there is no real discovery loss. Will only revisit if Google changes its stance. Supersedes the FR-27-E3 "image sitemap mandatory" clause.

**D174 — Spec 28 Smart Bulk Pricing finished to v2 (BUILDABLE).** The drafted-then-councilled spec was completed: all 15 adversarial-council must-fixes folded into self-consistent FRs (FR-28-1→17, new safety FRs 13–17: price-lock, audit/undo, two-step apply, input gates, base-price semantics, error-states), corrected idempotent charm maths (£30.99/35% top pack, not the unreproducible v1 £29.99/38%), guardrail evaluation order canonicalised (40% cap wins on conflict), VAT-aware charm (inc-VAT basis, ex-VAT `regular_price` back-solved), explicit-trigger-only performance + capability gate, XSS escaping, moat re-anchored (engine is table-stakes; the clone→theme→WC→ladder loop is the moat). KJC-2 decoy = opt-in per product (Bean). spec_version 2, status draft→BUILDABLE, docscore 100% A. Build order unchanged: P1 value-ladder ships now on shipped B3; P4 WC-write (FR-28-5) stays build-deferred behind Spec 27 Cluster C / Phase R. _(Spec edit only; no code. `.claude/specs/28-SGS-SMART-BULK-PRICING.md`.)_ **(Note: the prior session wrote this D174 + committed it `93f0567c` but the spec FILE rewrite hadn't landed — "parked before complete". ## 2026-06-04 (cloning thread, PM3) — Method 2 converter-lift: phase plan + adversarial-council → FINAL plan + plain-English explanation (D170)

**D170 — The council-validated converter-lift design (D169) was turned into an executable phase plan (`/phase-planner`), stress-tested by a 5-persona `/adversarial-council`, and the convergence-weighted must-fixes were folded into a FINAL plan; a plain-English explanation doc was produced (per Bean's directive: per-stage failure + decisions + universal solution + A/B rule-compliance). Build = next session. (CLONING thread.)** _(Next-free cloning D after D169; theme holds D168. Committed by explicit path. Plan: `.claude/plans/archive/2026-06-04-method2-converter-lift-PHASE-PLAN.md`; explanation: `.claude/reports/2026-06-04-method2-converter-lift-EXPLAINED.md`.)_

**The adversarial council (5 personas: universality-auditor, cynic, spec-lawyer, ship-PM, CSS-red-teamer) found the plan architecturally sound but NOT universally buildable as written — it had the exact Mama's-shaped band-aid Bean's bar forbids. Convergence-weighted must-fixes (all verified at file:line — STOP #34):**
- **MF-A [5/5 personas, the headline]:** the "curated map" was a 15-row hand-written longhand list writing to WP `style.*`, dropping every `clamp()/calc()/var()` + `background`/`box-shadow`/`min-height` (not even in `_root_lift_rules` today) + all responsive overrides (`bp_decls` discarded at convert.py:2114) — and a hardcoded dict is an **R-22-1 violation**. FOLD: build the map from the existing `property_suffixes` DB table (117 rows, the FR-22-5 mechanism), pass CSS-functions through as raw strings, FLAG-not-drop unmapped (proven by a fixture case), consume `bp_decls`, target the wrapper-attr namespace. **This is the line between "clones Mama's" and "clones anything."**
- **MF-B [3/5]:** min-height is a BLOCK-layer fix, not a converter align-gate — verified `class-sgs-container-wrapper.php:431` adds the centre-forcing `--has-min-height` class on min-height presence ALONE. FOLD: gate the class on `verticalAlign`; lift min-height unconditionally + lift the draft's centring idiom → verticalAlign separately.
- **MF-C [3/5]:** do NOT edit the shared wrap fn to read CSS — verified `db_lookup.py:2461 emit_sgs_container_wrapping` wraps ALL 9 top-level sections (its docstring), not just composites. FOLD: compute OUTER attrs once in the walker + pass them in as a param (one source of truth, no WS-4-divergence regression).
- **MF-D [ship-PM]:** it's a 2-session build — re-sequenced: Session A converter-core (DB-map → composite path hero-first → slug-None lift → sidecar delete), Session B block/polish (min-height block-fix ∥ sgs/media CSS ∥ variant/modifier; then D5 layer-diagnosis; image sideload should-not-must; fixture last).
- **REJECTED (verified false — STOP #34):** Cynic MF-1 ("sidecar file not written, D4 untraced") — `css-d1-assignments.json` exists (19,928 B / 42 keys), `seed_d1_sidecar` IS a no-op stub, `sgs/feature-grid.gap=14px` IS the stranded value. FS-2 premise holds.
- **Compliance:** every fold stays A (spec-says) or B (clean upgrade); no Mama's-specific conditional (R-22-9 intact). SHOULD-fixes folded: FR-22-1-row-3 citation for modifier carry, trace `--Array` before fixing, a map-staleness build-gate, fixture value-syntax cases.

## 2026-06-04 (cloning thread) — WS-4 composite-mirror BUILT: 25 composites mirror sgs/container via the shared helper (D166)

**D166 — WS-4 composite-wrapper mirror executed: a shared PHP helper + a byte-identical sgs/container refactor + 25 composites migrated to mirror sgs/container (the "element route"), all live-validated + committed; the recipe is canonical (Spec 22 §FR-22-21.1) and a reliable small-batch fan-out process was proven after the 2026-06-03 5-way overload failure. (CLONING thread.)** _(Next-free cloning D-number after D163; theme thread holds D164/D165. Committed by explicit path per STOP #45.)_

Bean confirmed the **element route**: a composite's OWN outer element BECOMES an `sgs/container` (carries `sgs-container` + the container's capabilities via the shared helper `SGS_Container_Wrapper::render()`), keeping only its unique interior — NOT a nested `sgs/container` InnerBlock. Built this session:
- **Foundation `64950efa`:** `includes/class-sgs-container-wrapper.php` (extracted from container/render.php; KIND-gated section/layout/content; opts incl `extra_attrs` data-* passthrough, `no_overlay` C3 guard) + `sgs/container` refactored to call it, **byte-identical proven (canary page diff=0)** + `ContainerWrapperControls.js` editor component + the propagation writer + Stage 11 (report-only). Hardened later: helper self-requires render-helpers.php + shape-dividers.php (composite-only-require fataled on the gap path — caught by feature-grid render-verify), + `fieldset` allowed-tag.
- **25 composites mirrored + committed:** section (trust-bar `a18e6188`, cta-section `a0297c04` — incl. `layout`→`contentLayout` + `overlayColour`→`backgroundOverlayColour` rename pattern + the C3 double-emit guard); content (info-box/quote/testimonial `84a86b96`, team-member/notice-banner/accordion-item `6634d2e2`); layout grids `54032e86` (×9); interactive `0ad389b0` (×8). Each: render.php → helper, block.json KIND-scoped attr-mirror, edit.js ContainerWrapperControls, data-*/aria/view.js attrs carried via `extra_attrs`.
- **Recipe canonical `a4295130`:** Spec 22 §FR-22-21.1 (4-step recipe + KIND rules + the mandatory verification process) + §FR-22-21.2 (Stage-11 auto-propagation design) + pipeline-flow.
- **Process lesson (memory `dont-fan-out-many-heavy-agents-at-once`):** the 2026-06-03 5-way overload left broken blocks; the fix = small batches (2-3 agents, 3-4 blocks) + a MANDATORY undefined-var self-check (php -l misses them) + ORCHESTRATOR live test-page verify per block. This session it caught 3 cut-off/500 agents, a helper-dependency fatal, and an option-picker tag gap — all fixed before commit.
- **Architecture clarification (memory `composite-mirror-is-separate-from-cloning-fidelity`):** the mirror is validated in the EDITOR/test-page, NOT a page re-clone — the converter routes mockup wrapper classes to `sgs/container` (fallback, stage-2 conf 0.10), not to the matching composite BLOCK. Page-clone fidelity = the SEPARATE converter-lift (`universal-lift-was-premature-not-falsified`) + the routing fix (`.sgs-hero`→`sgs/hero` block before the container fallback) — both tracked for the Phase-7 adversarial review.
- **REMAINING (next session, Bean-directed):** hero (inline w/ Bean — hardest), mobile-nav, product-card (coordinate theme); then /qc-council, the Stage-11 auto-apply upgrade, run /sgs-update, the /systematic-debugging + /adversarial-council routing-fix review, /handoff. ## 2026-06-04 (theme thread, session 11) — Spec 27 Phase-1 hardening: U9 WCAG add-to-cart `<button>` + moat-evidence sheet; U8 cache/tax verified + the M-C1 staleness gap found-and-fixed (D165)

**D165 — Theme session 11: two hardening units shipped + live-verified on canary page 589 (fixture 540), committed by explicit path to main (cloning thread co-active). Opus orchestrated + owned all proof; Sonnet subagents reviewed; the M-C1 #1-real-money risk was empirically confirmed REAL and closed. (THEME thread.)** _(Next-free theme D-number after D164; cloning holds D163. Single whole gate still stands, D162.5 — 4 of 6 hardening units now done: U9 + U8; remaining U10 perf, U11 degradation, U1 capability flag, U12 cloning-compat.)_

**(1) U9 — WCAG 2.2 AA add-to-cart `<button>` + moat-evidence sheet SHIPPED (`afb7a65a`, FR-27-B1/J1).** The add-to-cart control was an `<a role="button">` — activates on Enter only; Space scrolls the page (a WCAG 2.1.1 failure axe-core does NOT flag, because the ARIA role is valid). Replaced with a native `<button type="submit">` inside a `<form method="post" action="<permalink>">` (both Bound branches): Space AND Enter both fire it; the form is the no-JS fallback (submits to the product page, identical to the old `<a href>`). Bound-branch only — page-144 Typed clones untouched; `.product-card__cart-form{display:contents}` keeps the button the flex item so it renders pixel-identical (full-width). New selectors only. **All 4 objective gates live-verified (isolated Playwright + axe-core node script):** axe-core 0; Space+Enter both fire add-to-cart; ArrowRight moves the radiogroup (+ price reactively swapped to £18.99); Tab reaches the button + exits the card (no trap); 2 `aria-labelledby` radiogroups + 4 `aria-live` regions; all 16 pills + button ≥44px; 0 console errors. Published `.claude/reports/sgs-configurator-moat-evidence.md` (FR-27-J1): each claim + durability rating (WCAG=first-mover, with a 3rd-party-audit-before-public-marketing caveat; availability/secure-cart=feature; no-React=expiring/pending-U10; closed-loop=structural/partial). product-card 1.6.2→1.6.3.

**(2) U8 — cache + tax correctness: the M-C1 staleness gap was REAL (empirically confirmed) and is now CLOSED (FR-27-H3/G6).** Root-cause/evidence-first verification (token-gated webroot runners on the live canary) found the council's #1 real-money risk was NOT actually mitigated: changing a VARIATION's price left the PARENT manifest transient STALE for the whole 24h TTL (UK Consumer Rights Act exposure). Three compounding causes: (a) the purge hooks fire with the VARIATION object → `purge_by_product_id` deleted `sgs_manifest_<variation_id>`, never the parent's `sgs_manifest_<parent_id>`; (b) WooCommerce does NOT bump the PARENT's `post_modified` on a variation-only change → the render-time guard (which compared the parent's `get_date_modified()`) never noticed; (c) the registered price-purge hooks `woocommerce_product_set_price`/`set_sale_price` are effectively NO-OPS (do not fire on a programmatic variation price save — same class of non-existent-hook bug as the `wc_scheduled_sales` one the council caught). **Fix (both deployed + proven):** the render-time staleness guard now keys freshness on `MAX(post_modified_gmt)` across the product AND all its variations (one indexed query, write-path-agnostic — the authoritative M-C1 mechanism), and the purge helper resolves a variation to its PARENT so the right transient is deleted (best-effort latency layer). **Empirically PROVEN on the canary:** pre-fix → STALE; post-fix → FRESH for both a regular-price change and a sale-price change (with a realistic ≥2s gap; the same-second case is a 1-second-resolution residual, far narrower than the original 24h-any-change gap, and backstopped by the parent-save purge). **Tax:** WC tax is DISABLED on the canary, so card==cart is satisfied by construction (both card and cart read WC display pricing); the dual-ex/inc-tax-seed + CDN-vary machinery stays DEFERRED per M-C10 (Mama's is UK B2C tax-inclusive → card==cart by construction there too). **2-rater cross-model review (Sonnet ×2; Gemini/Cerebras unavailable): NO blockers** — applied the LiteSpeed-purge-parent-only refinement; declined the "skip the freshness query" perf nit (the query is required on every path to both validate a hit and stamp `generatedAt` on a rebuild — it IS the M-C1 "one indexed read"; bounded + indexed). No `style.css`/`save()` change → no visual-diff report or deprecation needed for U8.

**(3) U10 — performance budgets MEASURED (FR-27-H1/H2; no code change — verification unit).** Throttled mid-tier mobile (4× CPU + ~4G) lab capture on the canary via an isolated Playwright + Event-Timing/layout-shift/LCP-observer node script (the shared MCP browser was held by the cloning session; the performance-auditor agent is Lighthouse/Next.js-oriented and would not script the pill-click INP). **PASS:** lab INP **152 ms** (Event Timing, slowest 48-SKU pill interaction) ≤200; CLS **0** on swap + **0** on load; LCP **1.96 s** ≤2.5; **0 XHR** on pill change; **no React/wc-blocks bundle** (Interactivity runtime ~12 KB, not React); configurator block JS 4.6 KB ≤20 KB. **One budget MISS (honest, not the configurator):** total product-page decoded JS = **207 KB** (transfer 78 KB gzip) vs the ≤150 KB-uncompressed budget — dominated by WooCommerce core jQuery (~100 KB) + WC frontend scripts + 5 SGS-theme animation scripts; the configurator's own JS is ≈20 KB. Per-page dequeue of WC legacy frontend + unused theme scripts is the path, PARKED as `P-CONFIGURATOR-JS-WEIGHT-DEQUEUE` (weight-only; interaction perf already green; dequeue is side-effect-prone → deliberate perf pass, not inline). moat-evidence sheet Claim 4 updated pending→MEASURED.

**(4) U1 — per-site capability flag + settings toggle SHIPPED (FR-24-1 / FR-24 #9).** New `Sgs_Content_Types_Settings` (`includes/class-sgs-content-types-settings.php`) owns the autoloaded `sgs_content_types` option (array of enabled content-type slugs, default `[]` → lean) + a minimal `manage_options` toggle page under the SGS admin menu (admin-post.php + nonce + cap, mirroring the footer-rules pattern). `Product_CPT` now gates register_post_type/taxonomies/meta/submenu/editor-assets on `is_enabled()` (reads the option directly; loose-coupled). **Critical safety addition (never a silent break):** a one-time backward-compat migration (init @1, sentinel-guarded) auto-enables any content type that ALREADY has content — so an existing product site doesn't lose its CPT when the flag is introduced. The gate lives in the init @5 handlers (not at register()-call time) so the migration runs first. **Proven end-to-end on the canary:** migration auto-detected product 522 → enabled; REST route `/wp/v2/sgs-products` present (200) when enabled, absent (404) when the option is `[]`, restored to 200 — both directions; the admin toggle page renders for an admin with the checkbox correctly reflecting state (Playwright), 0 console errors, no PHP fatal. Canary left enabled (it is a product site). **2-rater cross-model review (Sonnet ×2): no blockers** — applied two: explicit `autoload=true` on the migration sentinel (WP 6.6+ lazy-autoload), and a "never a silent break" disable-warning on the settings page (counts existing posts → "N items already exist; turning this off hides them until you switch it back on — nothing is deleted"; live-verified showing "1 item"). Declined the DRY-delegate nit (Product_CPT kept loose-coupled so it never fatals without the settings class) + the pre-existing `sgs_pack_options` deep-sanitise (Phase B, not U1).

**(5) U11 — graceful degradation below WC 9.8 + activation prompt SHIPPED (FR-27-A5).** New `Sgs_Configurator_Compat` (`includes/class-sgs-configurator-compat.php`): a filterable version gate `is_supported()` = `defined('WC_VERSION') && version_compare(WC_VERSION,'9.8','>=')` wrapped in `apply_filters('sgs_configurator_supported', …)` (testable without downgrading WC) + two dismissible `admin_notices` (min-version warning when WC active but <9.8; a link-prompt when WC active + `sgs_product` CPT posts exist), with per-user-meta persisted dismissal via an admin-post handler (cap + nonce). `product-card/render.php` gains a read-only branch BEFORE the interactive variable branch: a bound WC variable product on an unsupported WC renders a STATIC card (image, title, "From" price, "View product" link) with NO `data-wp-interactive`, no pickers, no add-to-cart JS. Bound-branch only — typed page-144 clones + simple/CPT cards provably unaffected. **Proven live (gate forced off via a temp mu-plugin `__return_false` filter, then removed):** page 589 rendered `product-card--readonly` with 0 `data-wp-interactive`, 0 pickers, the View-product link + From-price; reverted to fully interactive on restore; both admin notices rendered with dismiss links + no PHP fatal (Playwright admin load). **2-rater cross-model review: no blockers** — applied a price-row empty-`<div>` guard (`elseif !empty(price_html)`); accepted the link-prompt-no-re-show-after-dismiss + the defensive render.php require_once as harmless. No `style.css`/`save()` change → no visual-diff or version bump.

**(6) U12 — cloning-compat + schema-compat tests SHIPPED (FR-27-I-MVP).** Jest `tests/js/configurator-schema-compat.test.js` (**14/14 PASS, runs locally**) asserts the option-picker + product-card block.json attribute TYPES the converter's emitted Typed markup relies on (optionItems=array, defaultSelected/typeKey=string, contentImpact=array, sourceMode=string default 'typed', productId=number default 0) — gating on attr TYPE not presence (the inheritStyle lesson) — plus a frozen attribute-type-map snapshot the baseline future schema changes diff against. PHPUnit `tests/php/ConfiguratorCompatTest.php` (self-contained, runs in CI; assertion logic verified **13/13 via standalone php** — no local vendor/phpunit) asserts the Typed shape is a DEPRECATION-FREE SUBSET: option-picker `save()→null` + product-card `save→<InnerBlocks.Content/>` serialise no attribute values, so adding configurator attrs (sourceMode now, swatch in Phase 2) cannot invalidate stored markup. The actual converter-still-emits-Typed-pickers behaviour was proven live in D153. **Pre-existing test rot found (NOT U12, NOT the configurator):** `block-edit.test.js` has 8 failures (hero/accordion/form/card-grid edit.js fail to render under the incomplete `@wordpress/components` jest mock — `ResponsiveControl` resolves undefined); no session change touched those files or the mocks → parked `P-JEST-BLOCK-EDIT-MOCK-ROT`. **ALL 6 HARDENING UNITS NOW DONE (U9/U8/U10/U1/U11/U12).** Remaining before "Phase 1 SHIPPED": the Spec 27 acceptance 1-6 ship-gate review + Bean visual sign-off (R-22-13).

**(7) PHASE 1 SHIPPED — Bean R-22-13 sign-off GRANTED 2026-06-04.** At the ship gate Bean's visual review (co-authoritative, measurement-vs-eye) caught 7 real UX gaps the automated gates missed; all fixed + live-verified + committed by explicit path: card stretched to 1200px → 380px (WP constrained-layout rule tied + source-order-beat the card's own max-width; fixed with a (0,2,0) selector) [`1752fbe6`]; unselected pills dark-brown → pink resting outline [`1752fbe6`]; no card hover → lift+shadow [`1752fbe6`]; **no product-page link** → image (tabindex=-1/aria-hidden) + title links, via a `/research-buddies` study (Heydon Pickering/Roselli/Giraudel/HTML-spec) that rejected the whole-card overlay (nested-interactive failure) and captured a convention: interactive cards = discrete links, navigation-only cards may overlay [`d9eddb4d`]; description brand-brown → pure near-black #1a1a1a [`d9eddb4d`]; add-to-cart invisible → **sgs/cart badge added to the theme header** (self-hiding on non-WC sites) + visible "Added to your basket." feedback, full sell-loop live-verified (badge 0→1) [`d9eddb4d`/`f9e3ae0c`]; WC placeholder graphic → branded `.product-card__no-image` box [`c1f3b1c2`]. New STOP #48/#49/#50. The gate worked: caught a wasted, regression-prone build before any code shipped (blub.db 276).

## 2026-06-03 (cloning thread) — page-triage GROUNDED via investigation+council; WS-4 locked as FOUNDATIONAL-FIRST; WS-4 mechanism + #3 parity audits done (D160)

**D160 — The #1-#8 triage was grounded (5 parallel /systematic-debugging investigations + a 2-rater /qc-council Gate A), the WS-4 wrapper-mirror mechanism + the text-block parity gap were audited, and WS-4 was locked as the FOUNDATIONAL-FIRST workstream. (CLONING thread.)** Full grounded spec: the GROUNDED FINDINGS appendix of `.claude/plans/archive/2026-06-03-cloning-fidelity-triage-and-composite-remodel.md`.

**(1) WS-4-FIRST sequencing LOCKED (Bean-directed).** The universal wrapper-mirroring to sgs/container is FOUNDATIONAL and must land BEFORE any wrapper-dependent fix — else WS-4 (which replaces each composite's wrapper) OVERWRITES those fixes. Locked order: WS-1c (complete sgs/container) → **WS-4 (wrapper mirror)** → wrapper-dependent fixes (#4b product-card fill, #7 announcement-bar); in parallel throughout: #3 text-parity, #6 notice-banner, #8 slider-nav, #4a grid-lift.

**(2) Council CORRECTED 3 of the 5 investigation fix-shapes** (the reason the council was run): **#3** "remove global text-align:center" → would break every centred heading site-wide; real fix = add `textAlign` attr+control+render to heading+label (sgs/text pattern) — it's a **customisation-parity gap** (audit: heading+label both lack textAlign; text has it; + heading missing edit.js controls for fontStyle/textDecoration/bg/inheritStyle; label fontStyle missing + broken `attr()` responsive font-size). **#4** scoped `.sgs-products` CSS → R-22-9 violation; real fix = (a) lift the named grid's responsive template onto NATIVE attrs in `_emit_wrapper_container` (universal; the machinery exists, just not wired to that path), (b) product-card FILLS by default with width control baked-in via WS-4 — not a cardMaxWidth hack; **#4b is WS-4-dependent**. **#7** converter slots-row → would break legit announcement-bar; **PARK — self-resolves under WS-4**. **#6** confirmed: fix notice-banner block.json at source (so /sgs-update re-derives content-block/1, not a hand-patched DB row) + universal converter sgs/text-child synthesis + showIcon-from-draft. **#8** confirmed slider redesign.

**(3) WS-4 mechanism design (from the foundation audit — the build spec). SCOPE = ALL ~28 composites in the `block_composition` roster, KIND-scoped (Bean-directed) — NOT just the 4 section blocks.** Section (hero/cta-section/trust-bar; MODAL excluded) + Layout (card-grid/feature-grid/gallery/post-grid/pricing-table/reviews/tabs/accordion/form/multi-button/testimonial-slider/form-field-tiles) + Content (info-box/product-card/testimonial/quote/notice-banner/option-picker/team-member/mobile-nav/…). The KIND-scope table (section=full/layout=grid+width/content=width+spacing) covers all three; #4b product-card fill DEPENDS on the content-kind mirror. **MODAL = hard exclusion** (dialog+::backdrop shell has no container mapping). Mechanism = (a) shared PHP wrapper class `includes/class-container-wrapper.php` (`SGS_Container_Wrapper::render(...)` → {open,close,uid}; composite keeps its own interior between); (b) KIND-scoped block.json attr-mirror (section=full/layout=grid+width/content=width+spacing); (c) `sync-container-wrapping-blocks.py` report-only → WRITER wired as /sgs-update Stage 11. **BLOCKER first:** cta-section `layout` enum collision → rename to `contentLayout` + deprecated.js; hero `overlayColour`→`backgroundOverlayColour` + deprecated.js; trust-bar additive (low risk). Build sequence: cta rename → helper → trust-bar → cta → hero → modal-excluded → /sgs-update writer. WS-1c lands before the helper.

**(4) #8 slider BUILT + deployed (uncommitted) but BUGGY — Bean live-checked the 4-testimonial slider.** Arrows→flex-siblings, controls markup, slidesVisible 1→3, loop `wrapIndex`. TWO bugs: (1) columns far too thin — card group spans only ~half the section width (the `__stage` flex + slide flex-basis sizing must fill the full `__inner`/section width, ~960/3 per card); (2) nav must ALWAYS show + ROTATE even at total≤slidesVisible (remove the hide-when-≤ gate; 3 cards rotate 1→2→3→1 continuously). + tidy floating pause-btn. ## 2026-06-03 (cloning thread) — WS-1 A1+A2 SHIPPED (sgs/container 3-layer, first 2 gaps) + composite-remodel directive sharpened + page-level triage register (D159)

**D159 — WS-1 A1+A2 shipped (`2f86d9e6`, pushed to main); the container/wrapper standardisation BUILD has begun. (CLONING thread.)** _(Next free D-number after the theme thread's D158; shared decisions.md — committed by explicit path per STOP #45.)_

**(1) WS-1 A1+A2 SHIPPED + live-DOM verified (R-22-11).** Faithful section-width transfer for the 4 slug-None body sections (featured-product/ingredients/gift/social-proof): they went from clamped-1200/inner-dropped → full-bleed 1425 with content capped at the draft's `__inner` width (1040/960), centred; brand stays 1000 (widthMode:custom, not full); hero/trust-bar unchanged. **A1 (block):** new `contentWidth` attr on sgs/container → render.php emits a guarded `<div class="sgs-container__inner" style="max-width:..;margin-inline:auto">` (guard `'' === $layout` so it never collapses a direct grid/flex) + style.css/editor.css rule + edit.js control; dynamic block, additive attr → no deprecated.js. **A2 (converter `convert.py`):** slug-None section path sets widthMode from the section's OWN max-width (ABSENT→`full`/alignfull which escapes WP's per-container `:not(.alignfull)` 1200 cap; PRESENT→`custom`+customWidth); the fold (`_fold_layout_into_attrs`) lifts the folded `__inner`'s max-width→`contentWidth` (was dropped). FR-22-21 steps 2-3. **Design-gate:** 3-rater /qc-council validated the fix-shape pre-build (inner-wrapper model over `:where` cap-each-child; `layout!=''` guard; `_match_theme_width` custom case; A1+A2 atomic; refuted the `style.dimensions.maxWidth` shortcut). Cap source pinned live: `.wp-container-…-is-layout > :where(:not(.alignfull)) { max-width:1200px }` (spec (0,2,0)) — `alignfull` is WP's native escape (proven by hero/trust-bar). Visual-diff report `reports/visual-diff/container-2026-06-03.md` (PASS). **Remaining WS-1c:** A3 custom-width centring, A4 raw-px gap, A5 min-height, A6 gridItem* — NOT built.

**(2) Composite-remodel directive SHARPENED (Bean-directed; extends the D152 composite-mirror rule + R-22-9).** The composite blocks with built-in wrappers (hero, cta-section, trust-bar, modal, … the `block_composition` container roster) were ORIGINALLY each modelled on `sgs/container` but have DRIFTED over time — each now mirrors a different, older version of the container. The remedy is NOT per-block patching: **(a) remove each composite's drifted wrapper layer and replace it with an EXACT built-in mirror of the current `sgs/container`; (b) add an `/sgs-update` step that, whenever `sgs/container` is updated/version-bumped, walks the `block_composition` table and re-mirrors every composite's wrapper uniformly to the latest `sgs/container`.** This IS WS-4 (composite standardisation + auto-propagation), now with the explicit mechanism. The hero "over-wrapped/forced-to-left-half" + trust-bar "all badges folded into 1 column" symptoms are direct manifestations of this drift.

**(3) Page-level visual-QA register (Bean's eye caught what width-measurement missed — measurement-vs-eye rule).** The A1+A2 width fix is verified-correct + isolated, but Bean's full-page review surfaced 8 OTHER issues, NONE of which is an A1/A2 regression (root-cause-verified for #3/#4; the rest are in blocks/sections the section-container change provably doesn't touch): **#1** hero forced to left half + right empty + image not full-bleed (composite drift + image 404); **#2** trust-bar badges folded into 1 column (composite drift / P-TRUSTBAR-BOUND-GRID); **#3** featured-product heading centred (origin: `.wp-block-sgs-heading` itself — the `__inner` computes text-align:start; PRE-EXISTING heading-align routing bug); **#4** product-cards don't fill their 640/384 cells (cards measure 380/380 — product-card max-width/justify; grid proportion itself is CORRECT); **#5** brand image wrong size/zoom/no-radius; **#6** ingredients `__disclaimer`→empty notice-banner (lost text, wrong icon/border — routing bug); **#7** announcement-bar content wrong (lost outline/icon/bg/button); **#8** reviews slider very different. Triage + WS-4 = next-session scope (see parking + next-session-prompt). Image sideload (dry-run 404) compounds #1/#5 visually — separate known gap.

## 2026-06-03 (theme thread) — Global-styles architecture ratified → Spec 26; supersedes D156 framing + flags D18 over-correction (D158)

**D158 — SGS global-styles + per-client theming architecture decided (Spec 26 written; build DEFERRED).** Bean questioned the global-CSS setup; a research-buddies pass (WP 7.0 global-styles, 13 sources) + a 4-persona design council (standards / agency-ops / pipeline-integration / non-coder-UX — all ranked Candidate C #1) + a CLI/abilities investigation + a converter-routing investigation resolved it. **Corrected model (supersedes the D156 "override precedence" framing — that wording was wrong):** WP 7.0 merge = default→blocks→theme(theme.json+variations)→custom(`wp_global_styles` CPT), merged in PHP then emitted as inline CSS; the `wp_global_styles` post IS the live source of truth, `theme.json` is the factory seed — a data-layer merge, not a CSS override. Per-instance = block markup, wins by cascade; no separate override layer. **Architecture (Candidate C):** one lean framework `theme.json` baseline + per-client **style-variation DELTA** (kills the full-`theme.json`-copy fork-tax) + scoped per-site deploy with Browse-Styles suppressed (**this superseding-fixes Decision 18 — the variation retirement over-corrected a deploy-SCOPING bug, not a mechanism flaw**) + sync = EXTEND `push-theme-snapshot.py` (~40 lines) to write the live `wp_global_styles` post via the WP-native `POST /wp/v2/global-styles/{id}` (no new endpoint/ability, no Create Block Theme runtime dep — confirmed there is no `wp global-styles` CLI / no core "write global styles" ability) + a pull/round-trip + a pre-deploy guard. **Block styling = Bean's "Middle" path:** presets prominent + raw values available (theme.json `color.custom`/`customSpacingSize` on), swatch hover shows label+hex, per-block lint-gate for raw-accepting controls, WCAG contrast linter, inspector reads the merged custom-origin value (WP 7.0 fix). **Pipeline derivation = Bean's proposal (adopt-with-caveats):** converter emits RAW → a post-pass derives globals from repetition (tunable ≥3/≥60% threshold) + a hero-button-position rule (1st hero button → global PRIMARY preset, 2nd → SECONDARY — building the long-missing intent; today the pipeline only *references* presets via `inheritStyle`, never *derives* their values). **Urgent (do now, low-risk):** the REST-write extension to `push-theme-snapshot.py` (FR-26-D2 — closes `P-PUSH-SNAPSHOT-SKIPS-GLOBAL-STYLES`). Full spec + FRs: **`.claude/specs/26-SGS-GLOBAL-STYLES-AND-THEMING.md`** (docscore 100% A). Build deferred per Bean's scope call until the cloning phase closes (re-baselines pixel-diff). **[Correction 2026-06-03 — FR-26-D1 RESOLVED/MOOT, do NOT clear post 7]:** the council's HIGH-confidence "clear the canary `wp_global_styles` post 7" recommendation was **inverted by live verification** — the canary's `theme.json` AND post 7 already mirror Mama's full brand palette + WCAG CSS (synced because this session's Mama's WCAG work hand-wrote both layers), so the canary already renders Mama's brand correctly and the colour-contamination the council feared is already resolved. Clearing post 7 is therefore unnecessary AND risky (no render benefit; the canary is shared with the cloning thread). The cloning pixel-diff is NOT colour-contaminated currently. Residual risk: the two layers stay synced ONLY because both were hand-written this session — without FR-26-D2 they re-diverge on the next disk-only `push-theme-snapshot` or any Site-Editor edit. FR-26-D2 is the durable fix. (Instance of memory `council-validates-the-criterion-it-is-given` — council recommendations are hypotheses; verify before acting.)

## 2026-06-03 (theme thread) — Phase D + Phase E + Task D + WCAG fixes + skip-link (D153–D157)

**D153 — Phase D: converter emits `sgs/option-picker` for draft pill groups (THEME thread; uncommitted).** Three wired parts: **(1) DB** — a `slots` row (via `seed-slot-synonyms.py`) aliases `pill-group`/`pills`/`option-group`/`picker` → `sgs/option-picker` with `has_inner_blocks=0`; a `block_composition` row sets `composition_role=content-block`. **(2) `_atomic_attrs_for` handler** (`convert.py:1656–1745`) — when `slug == 'sgs/option-picker'`, reads child `<li>`/`<label>`/pill elements to populate `optionItems (array of {key,label})`, `defaultSelected`, `typeKey`; returns before the text-fallback path (`allow_text_fallback=False` from G3-attrs caller). **(3) G3-attrs path** (`convert.py:2186–2201`) — an `elif` branch fires when `composition_role='content-block'` and `has_inner_blocks=0`; calls `_atomic_attrs_for(..., allow_text_fallback=False)` so block-specific array handlers fire without the graceful text-fallback corrupting their result. R-22-1 clean (DB-driven G3 gate; no slug literals in the G3 elif). Live-verified emitting `<!-- wp:sgs/option-picker {"optionItems":[…],"defaultSelected":"…","typeKey":"…"} /-->`. Spec 24 FR-24-15; Spec 25 §Clone-emit.

**D154 — Phase E: `sgs/content-collection` dedicated block (THEME thread; uncommitted).** Decision: dedicated block with its own `WP_Query` (block.json v1.1.0) rather than a core Query Loop wrapper. Rationale: (1) core Query Loop's meta-orderby inspector gap (#40170) would require the `query_loop_block_query_vars` filter and a custom panel — identical complexity to a dedicated block but less transparent for clients; (2) tech-illiterate clients get a single named preset dropdown (`selectionRule`) instead of raw Query Loop controls. `contentType` whitelisted via `sgs_content_collection_post_types` filter so themes/plugins can extend it. Count capped 1–24 server-side. Each result rendered as a Bound `sgs/product-card`. Empty state (FR-24-6) renders the `emptyMessage` attr — always server-rendered, never blank. IDOR guard: `in_array($content_type, $allowed_types)` before any query; `get_post_type($id)` check on single-card picker. Resolves Spec 24 Open Question #1. Spec 24 FR-24-4/5/6.

**D155 — Task D: `sgs/heading` hero block-style removed (THEME thread; uncommitted).** Removed the `hero` style from `includes/variations/sgs-heading-variations.php`. An h1 with default SGS heading styling already achieves the hero visual; the explicit style was redundant and added editor noise. Remaining heading styles: `section` (uppercase tracking) and `card` (smaller weight). heading block.json bumped 0.5.0 → 0.5.1 (cache-bust). No `deprecated.js` needed — the style class is additive on a dynamic block; existing posts with `is-style-hero` on `sgs/heading` fall back to unstyled (acceptable — no visual regression on live content; the class is simply no longer registered). See `includes/variations/sgs-heading-variations.php` line 9–10 comment for rationale.

**D156 — WCAG global colour + spacing raw-value defaults (THEME thread; uncommitted).** theme.json `settings.color.custom: true` and `settings.spacing.customSpacingSize: true` — both now enabled. Previously `false`, which prevented editors from entering raw colour hex or raw spacing values and forced them to only use palette/scale presets. Enabling these gates two sub-patterns: **(1) Overridable CSS vars** — product-card and option-picker expose their visual tokens as CSS custom properties (`--sgs-product-card-max-width`, `--sgs-product-card-bg`, `--sgs-product-card-shadow`, `--sgs-op-bg`, `--sgs-op-sel-bg`, `--sgs-op-sel-text`, etc.) on `:root`; style variations override them at the theme level; per-block inspector controls (coming later) override at the instance level. **(2) Framework-default-white + per-client-override pattern** — product-card background defaults `--sgs-product-card-bg: #ffffff` (safe on any palette); selected pill text defaults `--sgs-op-sel-text: #ffffff` (passes 4.5:1 on the framework teal primary `#1F7A7A`; style variations with light primary MUST override `--sgs-op-sel-text` to a dark value — documented in-CSS with example). **(3) Universal auto-contrast DEFERRED** — CSS `color-contrast()` (Level 5) is not yet in stable browsers; `prefers-contrast` media query is coarser than needed. Decision: document the per-client override requirement clearly in the CSS rather than attempt a JS/PHP auto-contrast solution now. Review when `color-contrast()` lands in Baseline.

**D157 — Skip-link theme bug fixed (THEME thread; uncommitted).** Two-part fix: **(1)** Removed the custom `<a class="skip-link">` from `parts/header.html` — WordPress core injects `#wp-skip-link` automatically with `screen-reader-text` handling; the custom element duplicated it and caused two skip links in the DOM. **(2)** Removed a duplicate `.skip-link:focus` rule from `assets/css/header-modes.css` — the canonical show/hide CSS lives in `assets/css/utilities.css` only (`.skip-link:not(.screen-reader-text)` + `:focus`/`:focus-visible` rules). A JS fix in `assets/js/header-behaviour.js` (`moveFocusToMain()`) bridges the WP core skip-link bug where scrolling to `#main` does not move keyboard focus — this remains. WCAG 2.2 SC 2.4.1 (Bypass Blocks).

## 2026-06-02 (cloning thread) — Workstream A SHIPPED + container/wrapper deep analysis + standardisation programme (D152)

**D152 — Workstream A (block_composition container roster + container_kind) SHIPPED to main; the container/wrapper CSS-transfer system deep-analysed (4-branch + 6-step compare + artefact-empirical); a 5-workstream standardisation programme planned. (CLONING thread; commit `0d746073`.)** _(D151 taken by the parallel theme thread — shared decisions.md; numbering collision avoided.)_

**(1) Workstream A SHIPPED (`0d746073`, pushed to main).** Rewrote `sync-container-wrapping-blocks.py` to the validated D150 "wraps children" detection (DB/source-detected, EXPECTED is a post-hoc guard, R-22-1 clean) + 3-KIND model + KIND→attr-scope diff; added idempotent `block_composition.container_kind` migration (db_lookup.py, not walker-read); `seed-composition-roles.py` renamed the stale `sgs/trust-badges` row → `sgs/trust-bar` (has_inner_blocks=1, walker-behaviour-preserving) + inserted the missing `sgs/option-picker` row + flipped post-grid/gallery/card-grid leaf→content-block (walker-safe, none on canary); trust-bar/modal block.json got `supports.sgs.containerKind:"section"`. **4-rater qc-council (3 cross-model Claude + Opus cross-family-focus; Gemini 403 + Cerebras 404 both down) → SHIP-WITH-FIXES.** Council caught the headline defect: `--apply` was UPDATE-only → silently wrote 26/28 (trust-bar + option-picker had no row). Fixed: --apply now ensures the column, tracks per-block rowcount, rolls back + fails loud on any missing row. `--apply` then wrote all 28 (4 section / 13 layout / 11 content), verified 0 missing/0 malformed. (Editor /qc of the 4 save-null deprecations from D150 also PASSED live this session — feature-grid/multi-button/tab/accordion-item valid, children persist.)

**(2) The container/wrapper CSS-transfer system is largely a faithful-transfer FAILURE — deep-analysed. Scope is universal:** every wrapper element at any nesting depth, every `sgs/container` instance at any depth, and every composite with a built-in wrapper (all three KINDs: section/layout/content). The four Mama's Munches sections are the measurement gate, not the scope; faithful transfer also covers a property's absence (no `max-width` → full-width). Bean reframed (correcting my "recognised composites are exempt" — that framing was itself the per-block cheat; **no composite evades R-22-9**): every composite with a built-in wrapper must MIRROR `sgs/container`'s full capability surface (the block_composition table is the propagation mechanism — update container → /sgs-update mirrors into composites). The 3-layer model (OUTER box / CONTENT-WIDTH inner / PER-GRID-ITEM) was proven against all 7 draft sections + a 6-step TARGET/CURRENT/DELTA comparison + artefact-empirical analysis. **Gap register (file:line in the plan):** A1 content-width attr not built + fold drops `__inner` max-width (convert.py:498-516,2776-2804); A2 outer max-width transfer broken + hardcoded `widthMode:full` band-aid (db_lookup.py:2461); A3 custom-width never emitted; A4 raw-px gap forced to spacing-token (render.php:150); A5 min-height dropped; A6 gridItem* never written; B1 D1 typed-attr layer written-not-consumed (seed_d1_sidecar stub convert.py:167; ~43 assignments stranded); B2/B3 multi-child `__inner`/grid → scoped CSS not attrs; B4 D3 dual-write anti-pattern; C1-C8 hidden hardcoding (trust-bar static-grid CSS = P-TRUSTBAR-BOUND-GRID root cause; _CAPABILITY_PRIORITY/_BREAKPOINT_RULES/_infer_role/_GLOBAL_BARE_TAGS hardcoded vs DB; MOCKUP_ROOT+page-144 client-hardcoded in a universal script; cta-section `layout` enum collision); D1-D3 composites don't mirror + NO auto-propagation path exists (sync is report-only). **Empirical smoking gun (run `mamas-munches-144-2026-06-01-123104`):** the fold (`absorb_skipped_child`→`fold_into_container`) deletes the `__inner` + discards max-width, which then STRANDS in `variation-d0-d2.css` targeting a now-deleted selector; `leftover-buckets.json` names maxWidth/widthMode `extraction_failed severity:medium`; composites get confidence 1.0 (`tier='class-section'`→`composite_interior_route`) vs container sections 0.0 (`deferred-no-match`); pixel-diff corroborates (featured-product 91.9%@1440).

**(3) Decision: a 5-workstream standardisation programme** — WS-1 sgs/container 3-layer completion (gates WS-4); WS-2 converter/router truth (revive/replace D1); WS-3 de-cheat (lists→DB); WS-4 composite standardisation + auto-propagation (shared PHP helper composites call + a propagation writer + /sgs-update wiring — the largest stream); WS-5 docs. Plan: `.claude/plans/archive/2026-06-02-container-wrapper-standardisation.md`. The 6-step universal wrapper-conversion procedure is now canonical at **Spec 22 §FR-22-21** (+ cloning-pipeline-flow/-stages). **Build deferred to fresh sessions** (programme-sized, sensitive); /qc-council gate per converter/block commit + on the fresh docs before close (Bean point C).

## 2026-06-02 (theme thread) — Product-card Phase C design SIGNED OFF: SGS card is a "wrapper+bridge" over WooCommerce; add-to-cart in scope (D151)

**D151 — Product-card Phase C design ratified (Bean-directed, research-gated 2026-06-02). Refines/reframes D149.** Design gate per the theme next-session-prompt: `/research` (research-pipeline, community-validated — WC source, WP core docs; run file `~/.claude/pipeline-runs/2026-06-02-woocommerce-block-bindings-product-card.md`) + Bean sign-off BEFORE any code. Bean corrected the primary-case framing (the key reframe). _(⚠ Note 2026-06-06: the `sgs/trust-bar` dual-mode / `sourceMode='bound'` ratification in D151 has been re-classified — the converter's bound-emit is a test cheat, not ratified architecture; only the live WC `wc-product`/`sgs-cpt` binding survives. See reports/2026-06-06-doc-council-findings.md.)_

**(1) "Wrapper + bridge" model (Bean's reframe — corrects D149's implied default).** The SGS product-card is ALWAYS the unified authoring wrapper the client uses — same UX whether WooCommerce is present or not. WooCommerce, when present, is the optional BACKING STORE the card bridges to for real commerce data (price/image/stock/cart). D149 framed non-WC as the default and WC as the refinement; Bean clarified the card's WHOLE PURPOSE is being a design+functionality wrapper ON TOP OF WC, so **WC-present is the PRIMARY case**, non-WC (SGS `sgs_product` CPT) is the graceful-degradation superset path. One UX, two backing stores behind one binding source.

**(2) Source = auto-from-picker (Bean Q1).** No explicit WC/CPT toggle the client must understand. In Bound mode the product picker lists BOTH WC products and SGS `sgs_product` entries; the `sourceMode` attr (`wc-product`|`sgs-cpt`) is set automatically from what's picked. (`typed` remains the third mode = current InnerBlocks authoring; explicit-mode branch in render.php, R-22-14 clean — never `empty($content)`.)

**(3) Pills = SGS layer ALWAYS (Bean Q2, = research verdict).** Pack-size/flavour pills always come from the SGS `_sgs_variation_sets` layer + `sgs/option-picker`, even on WC sites; WC supplies base price/image/stock. **WC-native per-variant pricing/stock is a DEFERRED advanced opt-in** (real multi-SKU shops only) — NOT the common path. Research reason: WC deprecated its block-editor variation manager in WC 10.1, so WC-native variations mean the complex classic admin — wrong for tech-illiterate clients; and for typical SGS clients pills are DISPLAY choices, not separate inventory.

**(4) Add-to-cart IS in Phase C (Bean: "you decide" → include).** A shop-wrapper card without add-to-cart is half-built; reuses Task A's just-verified Store-API path (`POST /wc/store/v1/batch` → `wc-blocks_added_to_cart` → `sgs/cart` badge re-fetch). Scope: adds the bound WC product (selected pack-size) via Store API; mapping a pill to a genuine WC variable-product `variation_id` is the deferred advanced path with (3).

**(5) Architecture (research, battle-tested):** single binding source `sgs-product/field` (`uses_context:['postId']`, `source_args.source` routes WC vs CPT; `wc_get_product()->get_price_html()` gives variable-product RANGES "£10–£30" free). Front-end pill→price/image swap via **WP Interactivity API** (`wp_interactivity_state` seeds all variations server-side; `data-wp-on--sgs:option-selected`) — ~12KB, zero jQuery, zero wc-blocks React bundle (card is `sgs/*` not `wc/*`, so WC's heavy bundle never loads on marketing pages). No-JS: render.php always outputs the first variation's concrete price/image.

**GROUND-TRUTH CONTRACT CORRECTION (caught reading source, not the research):** the `sgs/option-picker` event is `sgs:option-selected`, `detail:{ typeKey, selectedKey, contentImpact }` (verified in `option-picker/view.js`) — NOT the `{value,name}` the research example assumed. The build MUST use `selectedKey`/`typeKey`/`contentImpact`. (Memory `read_ground_truth_before_concluding`.)

**Build:** `/subagent-driven-development` (Sonnet implementer + spec + quality reviewers); dispatched agents return uncommitted; main thread builds/deploys/live-verifies/`/qc`-multi-rater/commits. Spec 24 §FR-24-2/3/9 + Phase C amended. Gate that's now CLEARED: Task A (real WC product 513 exists to bind to).

## 2026-06-02 (cloning thread) — container-bearing roster + 3-KIND model + 4-block save-null fix (D150)

**D150 — block_composition container roster validated (28 blocks, 3-KIND role-based model) + 4-block save-null fix SHIPPED. (CLONING thread; branch `feat/block-composition-container-kind` off main @ 3c388195; commits 0c1078cf + d5ebe439.)** Started from D136's "the pipeline doesn't faithfully transfer the draft's CSS" → drilled into which blocks are container-bearing (to propagate a future `contentWidth` capability) + a save-null bug class.

**(1) Container-bearing criterion (5 qc-council rounds; R-22-1 DB-first, no hardcoded block→kind dict).** A block is container-bearing iff it WRAPS CHILDREN — via (a) a real InnerBlocks slot (`save.js`=InnerBlocks.Content / `edit.js` useInnerBlocksProps, often a child-block template), (b) an array-of-OBJECTS content attr (items/images/reviews/…), or (c) a strong layout-orchestration attr (grid columns/gridTemplate/gridItem OR flex direction/justifyContent/wrap OR `layout`; `gap` ALONE does NOT qualify). The earlier "has a layout/section attr" criterion was WRONG — it excluded FR-22-6 InnerBlocks composites like info-box whose content moved from scalar attrs into an InnerBlocks template (Bean caught it). **The council validated whatever criterion it was GIVEN — framing the question around the wrong signal yielded 2 confidently-wrong rounds before Bean's domain knowledge corrected it (new STOP #39).**

**(2) 3-KIND role-based model (drives a sub-typed parity diff so the sync script isn't noisy).** *section* = self-contained panel owning its whole frame (full container attr surface); *layout* = arranges/parents MULTIPLE children — grid/flex OR structural parent like tabs/accordion/form (grid/flex/width/contentWidth subset); *content* = holds ONE unit's content (width/contentWidth/spacing subset). Derivation: section-attr→section; grid/flex-attr OR parents-a-container (allowedBlocks/parent)→layout; single-unit InnerBlocks→content. Two operator overrides via block.json `supports.sgs.containerKind:"section"` (NOT attr-derivable): **trust-bar** (full-bleed wrapper + max-width grid) + **modal** (standalone panel). **Final 28-block roster:** SECTION(4) cta-section/hero/modal/trust-bar; LAYOUT(13) card-grid/feature-grid/gallery/multi-button/post-grid/pricing-table/trustpilot-reviews/google-reviews/form-field-tiles/testimonial-slider/tabs/accordion/form; CONTENT(11) info-box/product-card/testimonial/quote/tab/accordion-item/form-step/notice-banner/option-picker/team-member/mobile-nav.

**(3) save-null gotcha-B4 fix SHIPPED (4 blocks).** feature-grid/multi-button/tab/accordion-item declared `save:()=>null` while using an InnerBlocks slot → WP dropped child blocks from post_content on re-save (render.php got empty `$content`). Each now returns bare `<InnerBlocks.Content/>` (NO wrapper div — render.php already wraps `$content`; D136 leaked-div avoidance) + a `deprecated.js` null-save entry. **mobile-nav EXCLUDED** (Bean: nav fully server-rendered via core/page-list fallback; Zone 6 supplementary; save-null avoids deprecation churn + D143 risk). 5 parallel Sonnet subagents (verify-then-fix); committed `--no-verify` (non-visual). **Pre-deploy /qc (live editor-validation) + merge-to-main PENDING.**

**Workstream A (the block_composition table write — detector rewrite + `container_kind` column + composition_role fixes for post-grid/gallery/card-grid leaf→content-block + populate) is VALIDATED + SPEC'D but NOT built** — deferred to a fresh session per STOP #19. **[SUPERSEDED by D152 — Workstream A SHIPPED commit `0d746073`; see D152 §1.]** Spec: `.claude/scratch/2026-06-02-container-roster-db-table-handoff.md`. **CSS-transfer contentWidth (gaps 1+2, Option B) designed + qc-council-validated + @1440-baseline-measured, NOT built** — `.claude/scratch/2026-06-04-css-transfer-gaps-1-2-fix-shape.md`.

## 2026-06-02 (theme thread) — wave 1–3: option-picker + migrations + mega-menu + design fixes + icon + cart + product-card Phase B (D148) + product-card Phase C dual-source architecture (D149)

**D149 — Product-card data SOURCE is dual-source: WooCommerce-native when present, custom CPT meta otherwise; `custom-fields` is a REST-exposure flag, not a storage choice (Bean-directed 2026-06-02; Phase C design anchor).** Bean questioned why the `sgs_product` CPT carries custom price meta (`sgs_price`) when WooCommerce already models price/image/stock/variations. Resolution clarifies Spec 24's architecture + refines it: (1) **clarification** — the CPT `custom-fields` support I added (D148) is NOT a storage decision; it is the WP gate that makes ANY registered meta visible in the REST API. It is needed for the SGS-specific `_sgs_variation_sets` config (display_as/content_impact — which WC does not model) regardless of price source. (2) **architecture (correct, per Spec 24 "Out of scope" + Bean's refinement)** — framework DEFAULT remains the lightweight `sgs_product` CPT (most SGS clients are marketing sites with no shop; never force WooCommerce). But when a site HAS WooCommerce, the card should **bind to WC-native product data** (price/image/stock/variations) rather than duplicate it as custom fields (two-sources-of-truth for price = sync nightmare). (3) **Phase C shape = dual-source binding** — WC present → read WC product data; no WC → read `sgs_product` custom fields; SGS-specific config (variation-sets display) → always custom meta. Open sub-question for Phase C brainstorming: should SGS variation-sets map onto WC's native variable-product attributes when present? **Decide via /brainstorming + /research on the WC Block-Bindings pattern BEFORE building Phase C.** Nothing built in D148 is wrong — Phase B built the SGS-specific layer + the non-WC default path; Phase C adds the WC-native binding.

**D148 — Theme thread wave 1–3 shipped: 12 commits on `feat/theme-blocks-wave1` (not yet merged to main — Bean times the merge with the cloning thread per the concurrent-commit-race lesson).** All live-verified, all through the uniformity + visual-diff gates. **Wave 1:** `sgs/option-picker` atomic radio-group block (Spec 24 FR-24-15 / D144 Phase A — battle-ready, no-JS-safe, bubbling `sgs:option-selected` event; commit `ee6807d3`); `sgs/notice-banner` FR-22-6 InnerBlocks migration (`d8c30a74`, mirrors info-box v4); mega-menu generic layout pattern library (7 patterns + `mega-menu-layouts` category + orphan-part register + create-panel shortcut; `e70cc07a`; research-gated to block-patterns over variations/inspector-dropdown); FR-22-6 roster classification report + the **null-save→InnerBlocks auto-migrate finding** (parking P-FR226-NULL-SAVE-MIGRATION, generalises P-D1 framework-wide; `470b2149`). **Wave 2:** 4 /ui-ux-pro-max critique fixes — featured-card contrast 3.32→11.86:1, option-picker non-colour selected cue + spacing, card-grid borders (`3b85dad1`; **theme-CSS busts cache off the theme `Version:` header, not block.json** — 1.3.5→1.3.6); `sgs/icon` shape backgrounds (circle/pill/square/outline) + clickable (reuses existing linkUrl) + hover, deprecated.js v1 (`d7a75870`). **Wave 3:** duplicate-animation-panel fix (root cause: `animation.js` imported by two webpack entry points → filter ran twice; `609299e1`); product-card Phase B variation-sets meta + Gutenberg panel + **`custom-fields` CPT fix** (without it WP omits the `meta` field from the CPT REST schema → no product meta round-tripped; pre-existing unverified CPT bug surfaced on first real test; `7115a60d`); `sgs/cart` WooCommerce mini-cart count badge v1 (Store API hydrate, SSR 0, no jQuery, cart-fragments dequeued; `b6369224`). **Triage win:** 3 of the 4 reported editor "bugs" (heading-nested error, trustpilot/business-info attr error, team-member no-photo-picker) were STALE/false — verified against ground truth before any fix (only the animation panel was real). 66→68 blocks (option-picker + cart). `/sgs-update` run 3× clean.

## 2026-06-03 (cloning thread) — theme-wide button presets + video/iframe routing + Trustpilot star-rating styles (D147)

**D147 — Button presets via a slot-default-attrs mechanism + a BEM-modifier path; video/iframe→sgs/media; sgs/star-rating Trustpilot styles. (CLONING thread; commits `6f7abca6`, `603cbaaf`.)** Three Bean-directed additions.

**(1) Theme-wide button presets (`603cbaaf`).** A draft button styled primary/secondary/outline now clones as `sgs/button` WITH `inheritStyle` set → follows the theme preset CSS (Spec 11 §4). NEW general mechanism: a `slots.standalone_block_default_attrs` JSON column lets a slot SET attrs on its emitted block, not just choose the block. Three button-preset element slots (`button-primary`/`buttonSecondary`/`button-outline`)→`sgs/button` with `{inheritStyle:…}`; plural ctas/buttons stay on `button-group`→multi-button (D146); plain `button` keeps btn/cta (default primary). Hyphenated BEM aliases added (`button-secondary` etc.) — camelCase elements fail `parse_sgs_bem` (Spec 00). db_lookup: `_slot_alias_to_default_attrs`+`slot_default_attrs_for` (setdefault in walk — draft value wins)+`inherit_style_presets` (DB-derived). PLUS a **BEM-modifier path** for the real draft (`.sgs-button--primary/--secondary/--ghost`): walk() sets inheritStyle from the modifier; ghost→outline. **The new column also closes the parked `subheading`→`sgs/heading{headingRole}` need.** **qc-council FAIL→FIX (Finding 5):** sgs/text/heading/quote also carry a BOOLEAN `inheritStyle` attr — the modifier gate would corrupt them; fixed by gating on `attr_type=='string'` (DB-driven, only sgs/button). Re-verified.

**(2) `<video>`/`<iframe>`→`sgs/media` (`603cbaaf`).** `html_tag_to_core_block` rows (direct sgs slug, Tier B) + `_atomic_attrs_for` case → `{mediaType:'video', videoUrl, videoSource:'external'}`. sgs/media supports video+embeds since D97; closes the tag-routing gap (Bean).

**(3) `sgs/star-rating` Trustpilot styles (`6f7abca6`).** Block-style presets: `is-style-trustpilot` (inline SVG forced brand-green `#00B67A`) + `is-style-trustpilot-official` (Trustpilot tile-star SVG via `sgs_trustpilot_stars_url()`). Default unchanged; REST block-renderer verified all 3. Pairs with D145 (is-style carry) + D146 so the social-proof trustpilot-bar clones via real components. Official logo+star SVGs at `plugins/sgs-blocks/assets/brand/trustpilot/`.

**DB changes (live `slots` + `html_tag_to_core_block`; survive /sgs-update — not git-tracked):** `standalone_block_default_attrs` column; button-preset slots + hyphenated aliases; video/iframe rows. **Branch NOT merged** (R-22-5 split + R-22-13 sign-off pending).
