## 2026-06-01 (cloning thread) — sgs/button replaces core/button (D146) + is-style carry & tag-authoritative leaf routing (D145)

**D146 — `sgs/button` replaces `core/button` everywhere + WP-mirror `sgs/multi-button` grouping (Spec 11 / P-9 complete; CLONING thread; commit `270cd995`).** _[Documented from the commit during the 2026-06-01 doc-sweep — cloning thread to ratify.]_ Implements Spec 11's "replaces all uses of core/button" + that spec's internal item P-9 (**NB:** distinct from parking.md slug `P-9` = Bucket-2 blocks, which stays OPEN — naming collision, benign). Three parts: **(1)** `sgs/button` block.json declares `replaces: core/button`; the converter's `atomic_tag_map` reverse-walks `blocks.replaces` so bare `<a>`/`<button>` → `sgs/button` (was core/button); `/sgs-update` reconciles `blocks.replaces` from block.json. **(2) DB slots:** the plural group terms `ctas`/`buttons` moved off the singular `button` slot onto a new `button-group` slot → `sgs/multi-button` (aliases ctas/buttons/cta-group/button-group); a draft CTA-group wrapper (`.sgs-hero__ctas`) → multi-button; singular `.sgs-button`/`__cta` still → sgs/button. **(3)** `convert.py` `_group_loose_buttons` post-pass wraps every run of loose `sgs/button` siblings (incl. a run of 1) in `sgs/multi-button` at the two children-assembly points; gated so a multi-button parent never double-wraps; group slug DB-derived (R-22-1, no literal); regex matches sgs/button not multi-button → idempotent. R-22-1/3/9 clean.

**D145 — Converter carries `is-style-*` block styles onto cloned blocks + content-leaf ladder made tag-authoritative (CLONING thread; commit `b93a3b51`).** _[Documented from the commit during the 2026-06-01 doc-sweep — cloning thread to ratify.]_ Enables a Trustpilot-style review bar (and any styled block) to clone fully. **(1) is-style preservation:** a draft can request a registered block STYLE on a recognised block (e.g. `<div class="sgs-x__stars is-style-trustpilot" data-sgs-rating="5">` → `sgs/star-rating` with the Trustpilot-green preset). `walk()` now carries any `is-style-*` class from the source node onto the emitted block's className (resolved-block path + top-level wrap); rating lifts via the existing `lift_behavioural_attrs` `data-sgs-*` path. **(2) content-leaf ladder reordered to tag-authoritative:** the node's OWN tag (`atomic_tag_map`) routes FIRST + ungated (img→sgs/media{src,alt}, p→text, h*→heading, a→core/button, blockquote→sgs/quote), THEN text-capable BEM segment, THEN sgs/text — fixes an sgs-classed `<img>` (the Trustpilot logo) that previously mis-routed to sgs/text instead of sgs/media. Unit-verified: logo `<img>`→sgs/media; stars div→sgs/star-rating{rating,className:is-style-trustpilot}; CTA span→sgs/text; prior committed-D regressions unchanged. Cross-model qc-council PASS (1 intentional nit: `<a>` text-label → core/button by tag-authority — correct for SGS-BEM drafts, not a regression). R-22-1/3/9 clean. Builds on D141's §FR-22-4.1 content-leaf step.

## 2026-06-01 (theme thread) — Mobile-nav full-fix (D143) + product-card 6 decisions ratified (D144)

**D144 — Product-card / `sgs/option-picker` design ratified (Bean's 6 decisions) — Spec 24 §FR-24-11..17 promoted from stub to canonical; BUILD still deferred (Task 2).** Bean answered the 6 open decisions in `.claude/reports/2026-06-01-product-card-option-picker-design.md`; all accepted, two upgrade the design. **(1) Per-type display mode [enhances rec]** — each variation type gets a display mode: **pills** (interactive), **static text-summary** ("Available in 3 flavours: Banana, Strawberry, Chocolate" — a selling point, no interaction), or **hidden**; PLUS a card-level "price only" switch that turns ALL pickers off → card shows just "From £x". Maps onto the existing `display_as` field in `_sgs_variation_sets` (add `static-list` value) + a card toggle. Bean's "pills that change image/text not price" already fits `content_impact` (a flavour pill swaps photo+description, leaves price). **(2) SKU matrix deferred [=rec]** — two price-affecting types → Phase-1 editor warning (first type wins); `_sgs_sku_matrix` is Phase 2. **(3) Pill style [=rec + enhance]** — filled in card / outlined global default; PLUS three visual states: resting / hover+focus ("considering") / selected ("active") — pure CSS on the radio-group. **(4) Clone emit [Bean: OPPOSITE of rec — corrected 2026-06-01]** — emit `sgs/option-picker` DIRECTLY from the clone (update TRUTH-SPEC + slot_synonyms/slots so the converter outputs the picker block for a pill group). Bean's directive: build the option-picker ASAP and get it BATTLE-READY, then wire it into the pipeline — NOT a manual post-clone swap. This pulls Phase D (Typed authoring) + pipeline-emit forward; the picker must be robust enough to be the converter's emit target. **(5) Source toggle [Bean: both]** — the Typed/Bound source toggle appears in BOTH toolbar AND inspector (one attr, two controls). **(6) Variation-sets editor [=rec]** — Gutenberg panel, not classic meta box. ## 2026-06-01 (cloning thread) — Editor "invalid content"/"cannot be previewed" root-caused to 2 issues + 5 fixes; all live-verified (D141)

**D141 — The editor errors are TWO distinct issues in two layers; fixed + LIVE-DOM VERIFIED (editor `core/block-editor` store: 0 invalid blocks, 0 console errors, post-fix). Root-caused from the runtime, not assumed.** Bean reported the prior reclone was NOT clean. Playwright editor investigation (logged in via `.claude/secrets/sandybrown.env`) read the runtime: **(1) 10 invalid `sgs/container`** — console `Block validation failed … Expected end of content, instead saw Chars` — all **text-only leaf elements** wrapped as containers (a container's `save()=<InnerBlocks.Content/>` rejects raw text); **(2) `sgs/media` "cannot be previewed"** — console `ReferenceError: imageId is not defined at edit (media/index.js)` — a pure block bug (edit.js used `imageId` but never destructured it). **Bean's methodological challenge ("are you sure? wouldn't correctly-routed blocks face the same issue since most have the prefix?") was CORRECT and sharpened the diagnosis:** resolution is ELEMENT-based, the `sgs-<section>__` prefix is irrelevant — correctly-routed elements resolve because their BEM *element* is in the slot map; the broken ones have a compound element where only a *segment* is a known slot. **5 fixes:** (a) **media `imageId`** — added to the edit.js destructure (built+deployed+editor-verified). (b) **compound prefix-strip** (db_lookup `_resolve_slug_from_bem_tuple` Path 2b — `card-tag`→`tag`→sgs/label; both-segments gate; cross-model qc-council PASS) + **`disclaimer` slot added fresh** → sgs/notice-banner. (c) **§FR-22-4.1 content-leaf step (NEW spec amendment)** — a slug-None sgs-classed node with NO block-resolvable element children is a CONTENT LEAF → emits a content block (content-gated segment-resolution → atomic-tag-swap → sgs/text default; `_node_is_text_leaf`/`_is_text_capable_block`/`_route_text_leaf` in convert.py), NEVER a container; gate = target has a primary `text`/`content` string attr (so a literal-text leaf never lands in media/star-rating/responsive-logo). Mirror of the leaf-misresolution guard. 2-rater cross-model qc-council PASS (2 docstring nits fixed). (d) **2B badge repoint** — `badge` slot `standalone_block` NULLed (badge = trust-bar grid-item = container, Bean), `pill` alias moved to `label` row to preserve pack-size pill→label (STOP #23 — no pill regression). (e) **C chrome-skip extension** — top-level `<header>`/`<footer>`/`<nav>` now skipped from page body when their BEM block segment is itself chrome (`sgs-header`/`sgs-footer`/`sgs-nav`), while a content block wearing a semantic tag (`<header class="sgs-hero">`) still resolves. **Live editor verification (run `mamas-munches-homepage-2026-06-01-170153`, deployed page 144):** `invalid_by_name={}`; top-level = core/html + 7 body sections (NO header/footer block); 3 media valid; 0 console errors (was 23); trace shows chrome_skip×2 (header+footer) + text_leaf×5 (price-note×2 + trustpilot-logo/stars/text → sgs/text). **Deferred design items (Bean 5/6):** trustpilot-stars/logo route to sgs/text for now — later use the real Trustpilot logo image + add the draft star style as a `sgs/star-rating` visual variation, then edit the draft. **Cart-block research (research-check):** `sgs/cart` mini-cart on WooCommerce Store API + WP Interactivity API (NOT cart-fragments / core mini-cart); leanest v1 = count badge + link; theme-thread prompt at `.claude/scratch/2026-06-03-prompt-sgs-cart-and-icon-enhancements.md`. **DB changes (live `slots` table, survive /sgs-update — not git-tracked):** `disclaimer`→sgs/notice-banner added; `badge` standalone_block NULLed + `pill` moved to label row.

## 2026-06-02 (theme thread) — Task 1: shared visual IconPicker (D137)

**D137 — Shared visual IconPicker built + live-verified on sgs/icon + sgs/icon-list (SGS THEME thread Task 1).** Replaced the type-the-name icon UX (1,917 Lucide names typed from memory; icon-list's 8-slug `@wordpress/icons` dropdown) with a reusable `plugins/sgs-blocks/src/components/IconPicker/` modal: search box + keyboard-navigable radiogroup grid (roving tabindex, arrow/Home/End, role=radio + aria-checked, 44px targets, WCAG 2.2 AA) across 4 tabs — Lucide (1,917) / Emoji (1,914) / WordPress (49) / Dashicons (curated). **Architecture (research-grounded — research-check 2026-06-02; memory `2026-06-03-gutenberg-icon-picker-architecture` + blub.db):** do NOT inline SVGs into the editor bundle (WP core hit exactly that bundle-bloat wall in core/icon, gutenberg#75715). Instead `scripts/generate-icons.js` (prebuild) emits static JSON datasets to `assets/icons/` — `lucide-icons.json` (952KB, the SVG map) + `lucide-tags.json` (search aliases) + `emoji.json` (from new build-time devDep `unicode-emoji-json`) + `wp-icons.json` (parsed from the canonical `includes/wp-icons.php` so the editor preview is byte-identical to the frontend). Datasets are fetched on demand per editor session (module-cached promise), never bundled, never on the frontend. The block stores only `{iconSource, iconName}`; render.php resolves the SVG server-side (single source of truth preserved — R-22-1 spirit: generated from the same source, not a hand-dup). PHP localizes the asset URLs to `window.sgsBlocksData.iconAssets` via a `wp-blocks` `'before'` inline script (filemtime cache-bust). **icon-list:** per-item picker + a default-icon picker; render.php made source-aware (4 sources) with backwards-compat for legacy `{icon:slug}` items (legacy→Lucide map) + conditional Dashicons enqueue; dynamic `save:null` so attribute-shape change needs no deprecation. **Live-verified (R-22-11, Playwright on canary 144 logged-in editor):** picker trigger renders in inspector → modal 4 tabs → Lucide grid loads on FIRST open (300 cells, real SVGs) + Emoji (300) → search filters by name+tags → click sets the block attrs + closes modal; zero own console errors (the 39 page errors are pre-existing cloned-content: see below). **Bug caught + fixed during live verify:** first-open Lucide load stuck on "Loading…" while Emoji + 2nd-visit Lucide worked → root cause a React useEffect cleanup race stranding a separate `loading` flag on the first source loaded → fixed by DERIVING loading from data-presence (no separate flag). **Pre-existing bugs surfaced (Task 8 scope, NOT this work):** `sgs/media` edit.js throws `ReferenceError: imageId is not defined` (editor crash = the "media cannot be previewed" symptom); `sgs/container` block-validation failures on the cloned page (cloning-thread converter issue). **Remaining Task 1 family:** notice-banner picker wiring is Task 4 (+ per-type defaults + corner-radius).

## 2026-06-02 (session 3, cont.) — CSS-transfer fidelity audit + static-div editor-error fix (D136)

**D136 — The cloning pipeline does NOT faithfully transfer the draft's CSS — 4 systemic gaps found by a draft-vs-clone computed-style audit; principle locked + static-div editor bug fixed.** Bean reframed the section-width problem as the pipeline's CORE job: "this is literally just about transferring the CSS values that exist in the draft into the clone." A Playwright draft-vs-deployed-clone computed-style diff (@1440px, mockup served on localhost since `file://` is Playwright-blocked) proved 4 transfer failures: (1) **framework IMPOSES `max-width:1200`** on full-bleed sections (featured-product/ingredients/gift/social-proof) — the draft has no section max-width (Bean's deliberate blank rule); the WP page template constrains any non-`alignfull` child to wideSize. Recommended fix = **theme-CSS keyed on structural position**: `.entry-content > .wp-block-sgs-container { max-width:none }` (top-level sections full-bleed by POSITION; composite-nested + explicit-max-width containers unaffected) — answers Bean's "why can't the template tell a section from an inner wrapper" (it can, via `>`). (2) **pipeline DROPS the `__inner` content wrappers** (ingredients/gift/social-proof `__inner`, max-width:960) — the FR-22-4.1 fold collapses them → content constraint lost. (3) **framework PAINTS a hero gradient** (`linear-gradient(135°,#C56A7A→#E68A95)`) the draft (solid pink) never had — the `#C76C7C` from the global measurement-vs-eye rule. (4) **`grid-template-columns` not transferred** (trust-bar__inner draft 266×4 → clone uneven 143/132/111/160; brand draft 122/782 → clone 450/450). **Two converter band-aids REJECTED** by Bean (detect-max-width→set-widthMode, gated on is_class_section_block then on a regex) — the fix belongs in the transfer layer / theme-CSS, never a walker conditional (memory `feedback_pipeline_transfers_draft_css_not_converter_detection_hacks`, STOP #33). **Also fixed (committed) the static-div editor bug:** `emit_sgs_container_wrapping` wrapped children in a static `<div class="wp-block-sgs-container">` + inline `<style>`, but sgs/container `save()` is `<InnerBlocks.Content/>` → WP validation rejected it → "unexpected/invalid content" on every cloned container in the editor (+ an extra nesting level breaking grid-on-section, likely feeding gap 4). Fix mirrors the already-correct `_emit_section_container`: emit children directly, no div, no duplicate inline style (CSS is in variation_buf). The committed `widthMode:'full'` width fix (e27ff591) is a PARTIAL band-aid covering only slug-resolved sections — to be superseded by the faithful-transfer fix. **NEXT (cloning thread):** the 4 transfer gaps, the priority. Audit + reframing captured in `.claude/next-session-prompt.md` + `.claude/scratch/2026-06-02-brain-dump-variant-routing-and-issues.md`.

## 2026-06-02 (session 3) — FR-22-20 universal variant detection BUILT + emit-proven + qc-council bug fixed (D134) + rollout-scope finding (D135)

**D135 — Rollout finding: slot-fingerprint detection (FR-22-20) fits ONLY content-distinct, modifier-less variants; the stylistic/behavioural MAJORITY need a complementary modifier-class→enum path (a spec amendment, NOT a slot-`variants` sweep).** Investigating Commit 6 ("generalise to the other ~24 variant blocks", per D133) surfaced that the slot-fingerprint mechanism does NOT generalise as D133 assumed. Evidence (block.json audit): **gallery** (layout: grid/masonry/carousel) shares `mediaItems`/`images` across all layouts; **heading** (variantStyle: default/hero/section/card) shares `content`; **divider** (line/dots/wave/shape) + **mobile-nav** (overlay/slide-left/slide-right/bottom-sheet) have NO content/object/array attrs at all. Their variants are purely stylistic/behavioural (same content, different CSS/animation) → **zero discriminating slots** → `detect_variant` always returns None → declaring `supports.sgs.variants` on them would silently never fire. The **hero is the exception**: its variants populate genuinely-different media attrs (backgroundImage vs splitImage vs backgroundVideo vs svgContent) AND the draft carries no `--variant` modifier class (`<section class="sgs-hero">`), so slot-fingerprint was the only available signal. Stylistic-variant drafts instead carry a BEM modifier class (`sgs-gallery--masonry`, `sgs-divider--wave`, `sgs-heading--hero`). The EXISTING modifier-class lift in `lift_behavioural_attrs` (db_lookup.py:2066-2109) does NOT cover this: it only fires for modifiers in `modifier_suffixes` kind='variant' (just Primary/Secondary/Tertiary) AND matches attr-NAME==modifier — it would never set `layout='masonry'` from `--masonry`. So the stylistic majority is handled by NEITHER mechanism. **Correct rollout = a complementary `detect_variant_from_modifier` path** (when the resolved block has a `variant_attr` and the draft node carries a BEM modifier matching a value in that attr's enum, set it) — a SECOND, universal detection mechanism that needs its own brainstorming/spec + a canary test target (Mama's has no gallery/divider with a modifier, so no live-DOM gate exists for it yet) before build (R-22-11). product-card's slot-`variants` mapping is additionally gated on its PARKED variation-sets design (D129, P-PRODUCT-CARD-FULL-DUAL-MODE). **Action:** the universal mechanism (hero) is SHIPPED + live-verified; the broad rollout is re-scoped as a focused next step needing the modifier-class mechanism (parking P-FR2220-VARIANT-DETECTION updated). Do NOT declare non-functional slot-`variants` on stylistic blocks (would give false coverage). Evidence-first per R-22-6/R-22-9/R-22-10; do-not-ram-new-mechanism per STOP #32.

**D134 — FR-22-20 universal variant detection BUILT (Commits 1-4 of 6) + emit-proven + LIVE-DOM VERIFIED; hero `$is_split` band-aid REVERTED.** Implemented Spec 22 §FR-22-20 / D133 on branch `feat/fr22-4-1-universal-wrapper` across 4 R-22-5 commits: (1) `1a48c602` DB schema — `blocks.variant_attr` column + `variant_slots` table (idempotent module-load migration in db_lookup.py mirroring `_migrate_property_suffixes_kind_override`); (2) `278b99ac` hero block.json declares `supports.sgs.variantAttr:"variant"` + `variants` map (standard→backgroundImage, split→splitImage/splitImageMobile/splitColumnRatio/splitGap, video→backgroundVideo/bgVideo, svg-animated→svgContent); (3) `5db969cf` /sgs-update Stage 1 populates `variant_attr` (write-on-drift) + `variant_slots` (DISCRIMINATING set-difference: a variant's slots minus the union of sibling variants' slots; live-verified 8 hero rows, all discriminating); (4) `55f42e1b` converter detector — db_lookup `variant_attr_for()` + `_variant_slots_map()` + `detect_variant()` + a convert.py emit-path enrichment after the `sourceMode` block (R-22-3: NOT a 4th walk branch; gated by `variant_attr_for`) + REVERT hero render.php `$is_split` back to `('split' === $variant)`. **detect_variant reads the draft's EXTRACTED attrs THIS run (`attrs` dict at emit), never stored attrs → closes the stale-data hole.** R-22-1 (DB-driven, no slug literals/dicts), R-22-9 (one mechanism for all 33 variant blocks). **3-rater cross-model qc-council (Sonnet rules + Haiku logic + Sonnet pipeline-trace, R-22-12)** triangulated ONE real bug: detect_variant used truthiness → dropped a legitimately-extracted numeric `0`/`False` (would flip detection on a 0-valued discriminator, violating R-22-9). FIXED via `_slot_extracted` (presence-of-meaningful-value: counts 0/False, excludes only None/''/empty-container — covers Rater A placeholder + Rater C empty-dict edges). Pipeline-trace rater READ convert.py + confirmed the hero reaches the enrichment with `splitImage` already lifted into `attrs` by `_route_composite_interior`; `attrs` flows unchanged into `emit_sgs_container_wrapping`. **EMIT-PROVEN** (production converter CLI on the Mama's hero section): hero now emits `sgs/hero{...,"variant":"split"}` (was: splitImage+splitImageMobile but NO variant attr) — single sgs/hero, no double-wrapper, images lifted scalar, art-direction CSS in variation buffer. ## 2026-06-01 (session 2) — Hero §FR-22-19 scalar-media BUILT + emit-proven; product-card/picker designed (D128-D129)

**D128 — §FR-22-19 scalar-media mechanism RESOLVED (DB-audit) + BUILT + emit-proven (NOT yet live-DOM-gated/committed).** Bean's "rework how the attribute slot decides block-vs-scalar" instinct landed correctly: the routing is a **role-column marker**, not an `attr_type` change (`attr_type` must keep `object`/`string` so the lift knows how to write the value). Mechanism (no new column): (1) new `roles` row `scalar-media` (styling-behaviour) → `equivalent_block_for()` returns NULL → walker emits no child; (2) direct DB UPDATE the affected attrs to `(canonical_slot='media', role='scalar-media')` — survives /sgs-update because assign-canonical only touches `canonical_slot IS NULL` rows (corrects the spec's earlier "block.json declaration" claim — canonical_slot/role are NOT block.json-driven); (3) walker preference rule `_route_composite_interior()` inside the `is_class_section_block` emit path (R-22-3 compliant, not a 4th branch): a composite interior column resolving to a slot the composite has a scalar-media attr for → lift the img(s) into the scalar attr (BEM `--mobile`/`--desktop` → base vs `+Mobile` sibling); else fold the column into bare `$content`. **DB-audit-verified roster: only 3 attr tags / 2 blocks** — hero.splitImage, hero.splitImageMobile, testimonial-slider.sideImage. **3-way discriminator (the universality boundary):** scalar-media (foreground + bespoke pipeline) vs FR-22-6 InnerBlocks migration (foreground + plain content, e.g. cta-section.headline/body) vs already-handled (CSS-routed backgrounds: hero standard/video/svg-animated variants; already-migrated info-box.image). **BUILT** (convert.py + db_lookup.py via implementer per a code-explorer map; DB UPDATE for the 2 hero rows). **EMIT-PROVEN** (walker run on the hero mockup section): hero emits `sgs/hero{splitImage,splitImageMobile}` + bare content InnerBlocks — double `.sgs-hero__content` GONE, imgs lifted with correct mobile/desktop. **REMAINING:** live-DOM gate (deploy + Playwright, R-22-11) + /qc-council the converter diff (R-22-12, NOT yet done) + commit. **GAPS:** testimonial-slider.sideImage NOT routed (tier='block' not 'class-section' → gate doesn't fire; DB row not updated) — broaden gate OR handle with social-proof. cta-section LATENT (gate fires, no scalar-media attr → all columns fold to InnerBlocks but its render.php renders headline/body scalar → would render empty; NOT on Mama's so no canary impact; needs FR-22-6 migration before any cta-section clone). Code uncommitted-then-checkpointed; live-DOM is the merge gate. **→ REMAINING closed — full integration shipped + live-DOM verified; see D130/D131.**

## 2026-05-31 — FR-22-4.1 Universal wrapper/container resolution (D118)

**D118 — §FR-22-4.1 "Universal wrapper/container resolution" added to Spec 22 as the canonical single rule for every sgs-classed wrapper the walker meets below a section root (Bean-directed 2026-05-31). Supersedes the patchwork: `walk_passthrough` drop-and-bubble for sgs-classed nodes, the depth-2 `_is_layout_bearing_wrapper` gate, and `_absorb_transparent_wrappers` (D52). Closes the FR-22-4 refinement mandate from D109.**

Four-step precedence (§FR-22-4.1):

1. **Block match wins** — BEM class resolves to a registered block → emit that block; it owns its CSS.
2. **Direct descendant + no block match → FOLD into parent container** — 1-child or non-layout shell: CSS folds as inner-CSS layer. Grid/flex direct child: container absorbs layout (`gridTemplateColumns`, `gap`, …); each resulting direct-item's positioning CSS folds as grid-item attrs on the container.
3. **Exception to #2 — direct descendant whose class matches a block → emit as that block** (it IS the grid item; handles its own CSS).
4. **Non-direct-descendant (nested below a folded wrapper) → its own sgs/container** (NEVER dropped); its descendants then recurse through #1–#3.

**What this supersedes:** the three patchwork mechanisms were each partial/overlapping implementations of the same principle — merge transparent direct-child shells, preserve genuine nested structures. §FR-22-4.1 unifies them into one coherent rule. `walk_passthrough`'s drop-and-bubble applied to non-sgs nodes only (FR-22-11) — its sgs-classed analogue is now §FR-22-4.1. The depth-2 `_is_layout_bearing_wrapper` gate (D117 G2) was the empirical discovery that led to this formalisation. `_absorb_transparent_wrappers` (D52 merge-side pre-pass) is folded in as rule #2's 1-child case.

**FR-22-11 scope clarification:** FR-22-11 governs nodes with NO sgs- classes (transparent non-SGS wrappers) — unchanged. §FR-22-4.1 governs nodes WITH sgs- classes that do not resolve to a registered block.

**Propagated to:** Spec 22 §FR-22-3 deferred-trigger note, §FR-22-11, §FR-22-17; Spec 00 §3.2; cloning-pipeline-flow.md Universal-path topology section; cloning-pipeline-stages.md Stage 4 annotation; TRUTH-SPEC.md trust-bar + featured-product worked examples; parking.md P-XS-3-TRIGGER-REFINEMENT + P-UNIFY-CONTAINER-ABSORPTION + P-CONVERTER-CONTENT-ROUTING-FIX + P-FR226-FIDELITY-AND-MERGE.

R-22 compliance: R-22-3 (remains FR-22-4 refinement, NOT a 4th walker branch), R-22-9 (universal — same rule for every wrapper, no per-class special-casing), R-22-11 (live-DOM verification gate), R-22-13 (Bean sign-off co-authoritative).

---

## 2026-05-31 (pm) — Converter content-routing: pipeline now RENDERS content + layout (D117)

**D117 — FR-22-2 leaf content-routing (G1) + FR-23-6 depth-2 grid-wrapper preservation (G2) shipped on `feat/fr22-6-content-render` (commit 1fcb0742). Mama's page 144 now renders its content AND side-by-side card layout — verified on the LIVE DOM, not pixel-diff.** Sequence: D116's container migrations were necessary-but-insufficient (content stayed empty). Root cause = the universal walker never ran FR-22-2 content-routing for leaf blocks.

- **G1 (leaf content-routing):** `walk()` lifts a leaf block's rich text into its content attr via `_atomic_attrs_for` + suppresses child recursion for leaves. ALSO fixed a latent bug: `_atomic_attrs_for`'s graceful fallback checked `info.get("type")` but `block_attrs()` returns the type under `attr_type` → the fallback NEVER fired (only explicit slug handlers worked). Result (live DOM): featured-product 0→510 chars, social-proof →621, trust-bar →98; all 7 content sections render. 4 regression tests (`tests/test_g1_leaf_lift.py`).
- **G2 (FR-23-6 depth-2 grid-wrapper preservation):** designed via a **3-rater council** (pipeline-forensics + code-path-tracer + live-CSS — all converged) reading the full Spec 20/21 log set + code. `_is_layout_bearing_wrapper` Trigger A preserves a slug-None wrapper as a neutral className-only `sgs/container` when **depth≥2 AND display:grid/flex AND ≥2 children resolve to real block slugs**. The depth gate (trace-confirmed: depth-1 `__inner`/`__content` wrappers over-fire + double-nest; depth-2 grid wrappers are the genuine layout rows) is the missing signal FR-23-6 always specified ("fire through `__inner` passthrough, targets at depth-2"). Result (live DOM + screenshot): featured-product + gift cards SIDE-BY-SIDE; header/trust-bar/brand back to 1 container (**duplicate nesting fixed**); brand −11.1; mean −0.66pp net win. Two earlier attempts (leaf-misresolution guard → hero regress; grid/flex-any-depth → over-fire) reverted per STOP #19 before this landed.
- **Methodology lesson (false-pixel-diff, BOTH directions):** an EMPTY section scores a false WIN on cropped pixel-diff (matches background); a REFLOWED-to-correct section (cards side-by-side) scores a false LOSS (differs from the stacked baseline crop). Pixel-diff mis-scores exactly the structural changes that matter. Live-DOM `textLen` + element-layout checks (Playwright) are the authoritative gate. Captured: memory `empty-section-false-pixel-diff-win`.
- **Status:** WIP on branch (renders correctly, NOT yet pixel-acceptance — images dry-run, `sgs/info-box` hybrid, exact styling). Merges to main when fidelity reaches the acceptance threshold. block_composition role corrections shipped via idempotent `seed-composition-roles.py` (testimonial+slider leaf→content-block, label→leaf).
- **Bean directives (parked):** (1) unify `_absorb_transparent_wrappers` (D52 merge-side) + the walker preservation into ONE structural container rule for all containers; (2) duplicate-nesting now fixed empirically by the depth gate.

Pre-existing since the WS-4 content-kind mirror (2026-06-04, commit 84a86b96). Fix: heading `edit.js` + `render.php` coerce numeric `level`→`h{n}` (permanent safety net + frontend parity); info-box + hero templates pass `'h3'`/`'h1'`. Live-verified 0 console errors. - **D186 — Icon-identity resolver (cloning converter) shipped.** New `converter_v2/icon_resolver.py` fingerprints each cloned `.sgs-trust-bar__badge` SVG/emoji → correct icon slug (reverse path-index + structural heuristics + emoji map), raw-SVG fallback (never a silent wrong icon). - **D187 — Stage 9 coverage-report schema fix.** `sgs-clone-orchestrator.py` renamed the bucket router's `totals`/`total_count` to `leftover_*` and dropped `gap_level_totals`, so the autonomy gate FAILED schema validation and ROLLED BACK every page deploy. Fix: emit the canonical contract keys (`totals`/`gap_level_totals`/`total_count`) alongside the `leftover_*` aliases. Verified: re-clone went `outcome=rolled-back` → `outcome=surface merge=success`. Commit `f93db924`.
- **D188 — Task-3 (converter Method-2) scope CORRECTED.** `sgs/container` is a LEGITIMATE, reusable, DB-driven conversion target for slug-None sections (Spec 22 permitted-exception-3 + Stage-2 confidence-matrix fallback by design); the fix is completing the UNIVERSAL DB-driven CSS-transfer onto the container's EDITABLE attributes (§FR-22-21), NOT forcing bespoke composites and NOT per-section. An earlier same-session overcorrection ("route to bespoke composites") was caught + reversed by Bean before any build; lesson captured (blub.db 329, `rule-critique-is-not-fix-shape-confirmation`). - **Icon-picker polish** (sgs/icon: browse-all beyond the 300-cap + category sidebar + wider modal) shipped `1450ade6` (editor-only).
- **D190 — parity2 containment fallback (Task 1) NOT shipped: its premise was falsified by the raw emit.** The next-session-prompt framed the testimonial/brand 0% scores as a GAUGE bug (parity2 mis-pairing text to a `<footer>`, "hiding real converter gains"). Reading the existing captures directly (not parity2's verdicts) showed the opposite: (1) the converter emitted the testimonials as a SLIDER with the quote text buried in `<div>` containers — **no clean text leaf exists** to pair to (every node carrying the quote has empty `ownText`), plus the `sgs-testimonial--Array` variant bug; (2) the brand headline likewise has no clean text leaf and the **attribution text is entirely absent** from the clone. So the 0%s are HONEST converter failures, not spurious mis-pairings. A word-overlap containment fallback (built + self-tested) correctly re-points the testimonial text off the footer onto the slide container, but (a) cannot recover any score (a container's CSS ≠ a text leaf's), and (b) NET -2 on the existing captures (44.4%→40.7%) because it removes two coincidental-CSS "passes" (section-heading__sub, product-card__description matched content-WRONG nodes at 0.00 word-overlap but similar CSS). Bean chose: revert the gauge change, pivot to the converter (Task 2) — the real lever. Reverted to clean HEAD; no commit. Method lesson: the handoff's framing is a HYPOTHESIS — verify against the raw emit before building (the primary-source rule, `.claude/reports/2026-06-07-converter-root-cause-and-primary-source-methodology.md`).

---

## 2026-06-08/09 — HC2 dead-control cleanup + build-time guard (D192)

- **D192 — Library-wide DEAD CONTROL purge + structural guard SHIPPED (commit `6922e541`, pushed; canary-verified).** An editor control whose attr is never consumed in render = a setting a client changes that does NOTHING (FR-22-6/native-supports migration debt). Audit (`.claude/reports/wave2/HC2-dead-control-library-audit.md`) found 34; the new guard surfaced ~39 more → ~73 handled (~60 removed, ~13 wired/confirmed-live). Full record: `.claude/reports/wave2/HC2-COMPLETION-2026-06-09.md`.
  - **Governing rule (locked):** a parent composite owns STRUCTURE (layout, wrapper, background, gap); the child text blocks (`sgs/heading`/`sgs/text`/`sgs/label`) own CONTENT + TYPOGRAPHY across ALL breakpoints. A parent control duplicating a child capability is BOTH a forbidden duplicate AND usually **dead by CSS specificity** — a parent scoped rule `.{uid} .sgs-hero__headline{color}` (0,2,0) cannot beat the child's inline style (1,0,0,0), so "wiring" it would ship a control that looks live but paints nothing. Removed hero's 22 typography attrs + all headline/sub-headline/label font-size groups; cta-section body + testimonial name font-size groups (child owns sizing); info-box colour/icon/legacy-link; testimonial(-slider) colours; form-field-file maxFiles + form-field-address lookupProvider (unbuilt); the shared dead `ContentSpacingPanel` innerPadding (product-card keeps a bespoke one); feature-grid columnsDesktop schema bug; ~20 orphans + 2 vestigial destructures. Wired where the parent IS the natural home: post-grid hover, google-reviews breakdown, mobile-nav social size, hero text-align + CTA gap.
  - **Guard `plugins/sgs-blocks/scripts/check-dead-controls.js`** (Rule-10 structural defence): fails `npm run build`/`start` (prebuild `--check`) on any new controlled-but-unrendered attr; DB-260 compliant (consumed/extension sets derived from source); empty baseline = zero tolerance. Two cross-block channels handled: responsive `{base}Tablet/Mobile` (consumed if base consumed + breakpoint token IN THE BLOCK'S OWN corpus) and `providesContext`→live-`usesContext`. Corpus is block-local + shared `includes/` ONLY — deliberately NOT broadened to all blocks (generic names `title`×91/`label`×74 would collide and re-open the bug class). Proven to fail on a reintroduced (incl. `sgs`-prefixed) dead control and pass clean across 69 blocks.
  - **Validation:** `/qc-council` overturned 2 of my calls (hero typography WIRE→REMOVE on the specificity proof; innerPadding WIRE→remove-panel) + tightened the guard rules. `/adversarial-council` (6 personas) graded the cleanup A−/A (converter-safe per the live trace; deprecations sound) but found 3 real guard false-negatives (rule (a) neutered by shared-corpus `@media` pollution; regex blind to `update('k',v)` + `RRangeControl attrDesktop=` controls; `sgs*` prefix bypass) + a commit-safety trap (untracked guard files) — ALL fixed + re-proven before commit. Commit was path-scoped (50 explicit paths; co-active Spec-28/cloning files excluded); `--no-verify` used (hook-sanctioned for non-visual change). `/sgs-update` pruned 86 orphan DB attrs to match the slimmed schemas.
  - **Scope note:** the guard is build-gated (runs on every `npm run build`/`start` = the deploy path); a CI/pre-commit/self-test backstop was considered and deliberately NOT pursued (no CI exists; over-engineering for now). No client inspector-notice added — the typography capability was always on the child block; the removed parent controls were dead, so there is no functional loss to bridge.
  - Memory: `dead-control-can-be-dead-by-specificity`. R-22 compliance: R-22-9 (universal — every block, no carve-out), R-22-11 (live-DOM canary verify), R-22-13 (Bean eye co-authoritative — screenshot delivered).

### D229 — Cloning CSS-transfer = CLEAN MODULAR STAGE-BY-STAGE REBUILD; Spec 31 v0.3 is the build blueprint (adversarial-council-corrected, Bean-locked 2026-06-17)

A full architecture+validation session (no code shipped — planning only) concluded the cloning CSS-transfer system is not soundly patchable and must be **rebuilt clean**. Evidence: a 22-finding persona audit (6 HIGH) across the 3 vital cross-stage mechanisms (M1 nested wrapper/grid layers · M2 child-block/atomic/CSS/variant classification fork · M3 complete no-exception CSS transfer) showed systemic holes in sgs/container + composites-with-scalar/child-elements + blocks-with-child-blocks; the trust-bar precedent proved spot-fixes don't generalise and *regress*. Deliverables (all on main, untracked→committed this handoff):
- **`specs/31-UNIVERSAL-CLONING-PIPELINE.md` v0.3** — THE build blueprint. §1-§11 = validated architecture (DB-driven name-free routing, 4-axis model, anti-cheat intent); **§12 = authoritative clean-modular-rebuild direction** (banner supersedes §1/§11 fix-in-place assumptions). qc-council-verified build-ready (all council must-fixes APPLIED; 2 stale-text reconciliations fixed: §6.7 Method-2 in-scope, §5 ledger-supersedes-matrix).
- **`reports/pipeline-routing-map-2026-06-17.html`** — exhaustive 24-stage decision graph (every branch/DB-call/terminal) + 3 cross-stage mechanism traces + the 22-gap register. Built from direct code extraction. THE structural map for the rebuild.
- **`reports/2026-06-17-adversarial-council-register-and-rebuild-direction.md`** — convergence-weighted must-fix register + Bean's locked decisions.
- **`reports/2026-06-17-cross-stage-reviewer-personas.md`** — persona roster for future audit subagents.
**Bean's 3 locked decisions:** (1) clean rebuild not spot-fixes (Mama's=100% is a METRIC of pipeline effectiveness, not the goal); (2) MODULAR file architecture — split the converter into per-resolver files behind one dispatch table + remake the orchestrator against the chart (the giant convert.py/orchestrator scripts hide functions/cheats/DB-calls from humans AND subagents — demonstrated this session when a rater overwrote the chart); (3) stage-by-stage = BUILD ORDER + per-stage universality test (don't start stage N+1 until stage N passes on the multi-shape fixture set).
**The Tier-1 FOUNDATION (built FIRST, the spine — §12.2):** (a) draft-DERIVED CSS Accounting Ledger — input = the draft's parsed declarations at Stage 0.7, NOT the converter's recognised set (the keystone; makes the ~15 no-suffix-row classes impossible to silently drop); (b) WRITTEN vs LANDED (LANDED = live computed-style = draft on a non-default fixture; the only "done"); (c) differential render-oracle (render draft vs render clone, pixel-diff) + 3 metamorphic relations; (d) closed DB-backed EXCLUDED set + gate; (e) the 3 missing gates built+ARMED first (check-converter-cheats.py + generate-coverage-matrix.py + pipeline-close ledger check; wire check_no_mirror.py --enforce + a PreToolUse git hook); (f) ledger = the build spine. §12.7 carries the foundation build order (F1-F6) + the gap-to-stage map. **D-CEILING now D229.** Method lesson (memory `subagents-must-not-write-shared-files`): a reviewing subagent overwrote the master pipeline-map HTML — subagent prompts must say "return data, never write shared files"; recovered from context.

### D230 — Exact-match width model: widthMode RETIRED → 3 independent layers (align / maxWidth / contentWidth); Bean-locked, council-gated, LANDED-verified 2026-06-18

A Bean-initiated **architectural design upgrade** (NOT part of the D229 Phase-F plan, but NOT a spot-fix either — Bean-clarified 2026-06-18: a spot-fix is a means-to-an-end score/section-chase that ignores pipeline-wide implications; this is a deliberate, universal 3-layer width-model upgrade considering overall implications, so it does NOT conflict with D229's no-spot-fix principle — it's an architectural primitive the clean rebuild builds ON) to make cloned section widths render EXACTLY like the draft. Designed via `/brainstorming` → `/adversarial-council` (6-persona, caught a fatal `maxWidth`-is-occupied premise error pre-build) → Bean design-gate (4 iterations) → SDD build (subagents implement, Opus orchestrates) → `/qc-council` (3-rater, caught a real responsive-specificity WRITTEN-not-LANDED bug pre-commit) → live computed-style verify on the canary. Design doc: `.claude/plans/2026-06-17-exact-match-width-model-design.md` (v0.4).

**The model (replaces the old `widthMode` outer-width system):**
- **`align`** (WP-native, `supports.align:['wide','full']`) = breakout (full-bleed/wide). Converter emits `align:"full"` for a full-bleed section (was `widthMode:"full"`).
- **`maxWidth`** (string literal) = OUTER box cap, exact draft value (decimals+unit preserved; the 5% theme-snap + `int()` truncation are GONE). Responsive `maxWidthTablet/Mobile` via the wrapper's 767/1023 device tiers (base deferred to a `.uid` rule when tiers exist, so `@media` wins — the specificity fix).
- **`contentWidth`** (token OR literal) = INNER band. Tokens RENAMED: `narrow`=content-size(~780), `default`=wide-size(~1200, the new default value), `full`=no cap. Base sanitiser unified onto `$sgs_css_length`. Converter emits `contentWidth:"full"` for a slug-None section with no detected band (fidelity — no imposed 1200 default).

**Retired:** `widthMode`/`widthModeMobile/Tablet/Desktop` + `customWidth`/`customWidthUnit` (theme NOT live → deleted outright, no deprecation). Editor controls now `UnitControl`-style (number+unit) like gap/font-size; breakout via WP's native align toolbar. `sgs/quote` bespoke customWidth control migrated to the shared control. 6 conformance goldens rebaselined (`widthMode:"full"`→`align:"full"` only — verified no other drift). **Deferred cosmetic sweep:** ~30 vestigial `widthMode` block.json declarations + 8 stale render.php doc-comments (harmless, declared-but-unread). **LANDED-verified:** all 7 live render cases correct on the canary (align breakout, maxWidth literal, contentWidth narrow/default/full/literal). WP best-practice confirmed via `/library-docs` (no native max-width support → custom attr is correct). **D-CEILING now D230.**

### D231 — Content-band token rename (normal/wide/full, default=full) + widthMode vestigial sweep; Bean-locked, LANDED 2026-06-18

Follow-up to D230 after the live theme revealed content-size=1200 / wide-size=1400 (not the assumed 780/1200), making the `narrow`/`default` labels wrong. **New `contentWidth` model:** `normal`→content-size(1200), `wide`→wide-size(1400), `full`→no cap, or a literal. **Default value `"default"`→`"full"`** — a blank/defaulted contentWidth imposes NO inner band (content fills the outer `maxWidth`); this also resolves the D230 outer-800+1200-band nuance. Files: container block.json (default), `class-sgs-container-wrapper.php` (`$sgs_resolve_content_width` token keys + empty→full), `ContainerWrapperControls.js` (preset labels Normal/Wide/Full/Custom + `isToken`). Live-verified on the deployed wrapper (do_blocks): normal→content-size var, wide→wide-size var, full + blank→no cap, 900px→literal. **Cosmetic sweep (same commit):** 29 composite block.json had vestigial `widthMode*` declarations removed (the shared wrapper reads align/maxWidth/contentWidth now, never widthMode) + 8 stale render.php doc-comments fixed; 0 `widthMode` references remain anywhere. Conformance 43+41, build green (dead-control 0 net-new). **D-CEILING now D231.**

### D232 — Phase-F step F2 SHIPPED: draft-derived CSS Accounting Ledger input parser; physical-only (no expansion); Bean-locked, council+cross-model gated 2026-06-18

The keystone of the Spec-31 §12.7 clean-rebuild Tier-1 foundation (MF-1). A standalone module `plugins/sgs-blocks/scripts/ledger/{declare_input,models}.py` does an INDEPENDENT tinycss2 parse of a draft's raw HTML+CSS into a surjective `declare_input` set `(selector,property,value,media,tier,source_index,…)` at Stage 0.7 BEFORE any routing — never imports css_router/convert/db_lookup, never queries the DB (STOP-3), so it cannot inherit the converter's blind spots. FAIL-CLOSED: parse error / unknown at-rule / non-font @import / blockless @media / at-rule-in-decl-list all raise `LedgerParseError` — zero silent skips. Captures pseudo-elements, inline `style=""`, custom-props, `!important`, @media tiers. Tier = canonical device thresholds {767/768, 1023/1024, 1024} ONLY; 600/640/781 → `Other:<verbatim>` (D228 device-tier-vs-visual lock; the rt-media-600 CHEAT). 37 fixtures, 515 declarations, 167 tests; deterministic `--check` wired into `package.json prebuild` (not inert). Commit `f8a746c7`.
**Architecture decision (Bean's catch):** F2 does NO shorthand expansion. The DB already owns box-model shorthand→longhand decomposition (`property_suffixes` shorthand+longhand rows + `modifier_suffixes` side/corner) — rebuilding it violates R-22-1, and sourcing expansion FROM the DB would make the ledger circular (STOP-3). So F2 records physical declarations only; partial-shorthand-lift detection is F3's (render-oracle) job. The whole-declaration guarantee (F2) + within-declaration guarantee (F3) compose to the full no-silent-drop spine. This SUPERSEDED the adversarial-council's value-vs-names shorthand debate.
**Process:** brainstorming → 6-persona adversarial-council → Bean design-gate → SDD build → cross-model code review (caught 3 silent-drop holes — empty-value `continue`, nested @supports overwrite, at-rule-in-decl-list `continue` — all fixed pre-commit) → independent verify. Design doc: `.claude/plans/2026-06-18-f2-css-accounting-ledger-design.md` (v2). **STOP-11 correction:** the doc/expected.md "~15 no-suffix-row properties" list is partly STALE — `background-image`/`object-fit`/`opacity`/`aspect-ratio`/`filter` already have `property_suffixes` rows; F2's baseline is measured against the LIVE DB, never the doc. **F2↔F5 join contract FROZEN** (§9): join key `(selector,property,media)`, value compared-not-joined, non-shadowed non-excluded physical rows = the UNACCOUNTED denominator. **NEXT: F3** (differential render-oracle + 3 metamorphic relations). **D-CEILING now D232.**

### D233 — Phase-F F3 re-scoped to F3-core (computed-style-primary LANDED oracle); F3-runtime deferred; render-mechanism fixed. Council-corrected + Bean-approved 2026-06-18

F3 (the differential render-oracle) was designed → 6-persona adversarial-council → Bean gate. The council found F3-as-designed had a FATAL flaw + was over-scoped; Bean approved a re-scope. Design doc: `.claude/plans/2026-06-18-f3-render-oracle-design.md` (v2). NOT yet built — to build in a fresh session.
**Fatal flaw fixed:** the original "render bare draft locally + pixel-diff vs WP-rendered clone" is apples-to-oranges (draft has no theme CSS/fonts/WP resets → even a perfect transfer fails the pixel-diff on chrome → ~100% false-fails). **Corrected:** the PRIMARY LANDED signal is targeted computed-style on the rendered SGS block (environment-comparable); pixel-diff demoted to a deferred secondary against a known-difference baseline. **parity2 must NOT be the LANDED comparator** — it pairs by draft BEM class which native clone output doesn't carry (memory `parity-bem-class-blind-spot`); reuse only its tolerance helpers, pair by rendered block slug + getComputedStyle.
**Re-scope (reverses the earlier "full render-diff on all 37" call, on new info):** F3-CORE (build now, ~2hrs) = the verdict function + 4 false-win guards (empty/element/non-default/NEW height-parity) + MR-2 (name-free routing) proven on ONE fixture, emitting the frozen F3→F5 contract, computed-style primary. F3-RUNTIME (deferred, build lazily when the rebuild first renders many fixtures) = full-37 canary render-diff + content-hash cache (poison-proof key spec'd) + pixel-diff secondary (apples-to-apples fixed) + flake-classification + deploy choreography + committed per-cell baseline (the F2-golden-regen defence) + canary health-gate. Reasoning: building a cache/orchestration for a render loop that doesn't run yet, where a stale cache = a false LANDED, is the stall trap on a 5-times-failed rebuild.
**Folded council fixes:** exhaustive verdict taxonomy with precedence (NOT-RENDERED>GUARD-FAIL>UNVERIFIED>WRITTEN-not-LANDED>LANDED); section_id via `data-f3-section-id` + converter section→slug map; guard-3 default from block.json not the converter DB (independence); F3→F5 join key `(section_id,block_slug,property,tier)` with F2's tier vocabulary; MR-3 re-scoped (raw-px only, re-snap tokens, never scale breakpoints). **NEXT SESSION: build F3-core.** **D-CEILING now D233.**

### D234 — Phase-F step F3-core SHIPPED: the LANDED render-oracle verdict engine + live-canary proof; Bean-built, cross-model+qc-council gated 2026-06-18

The closing-gate ENGINE of the Spec-31 §12.7 Tier-1 foundation (MF-2/MF-3): proves a CSS value the converter WROTE actually LANDED on the rendered SGS block (catches WRITTEN-not-LANDED / wrong-layer transfer in the oracle, not Bean's eye — STOP-4). New module `plugins/sgs-blocks/scripts/oracle/` (sibling of `ledger/`), commit `6b430dae`:
- **verdict.py** — §3 precedence `NOT-RENDERED > GUARD-FAIL > UNVERIFIED > WRITTEN-not-LANDED > LANDED`; tri-state compare (LANDED/NOT_LANDED/UNVERIFIABLE); LANDED via ΔE≤1 colour / ≤1px length REUSING `parity2._colour_delta`/`_parse_px` (R-22-1), NOT parity2's BEM matcher (parity-bem-class-blind-spot — pairs by rendered block slug `.wp-block-sgs-<slug>` + getComputedStyle). **No false-LANDED path** (Opus review + cross-trace: guard-fail/written=False/computed-None/lossy/unparseable all reach UNVERIFIED|GUARD-FAIL before LANDED).
- **guards.py** — 4 false-win guards: empty-section (`innerText.length>0`+present), element-present (slug selector), non-default-value (cell-level, sourced from **block.json default** not converter DB — independence; draft==default → UNVERIFIED), height-parity (relative-OR-absolute, unmeasured→not-confirmed-not-fail).
- **models.py** — FROZEN F3→F5 §6 contract (join key `(section_id,block_slug,property,tier)`; F2 tier vocabulary exactly); `written` precondition (F3 only evaluates converter-written cells — no coincidental-initial-value LANDED, no CSS-initial table); tier-format validation.
- **metamorphic.py** — MR-2 name-free routing (BEM-synonym rename within same slot → JSON-semantically identical AND golden-correct converter output) + coverage line. MR-1/MR-3 → F3-runtime.
- **capture.py** — live-probe interface; `NotImplementedError` stub (F3-runtime wires the automated probe — no fake LANDED).
- **run_canary_proof.py** — F3-core-B "separate named command" (§7.7); fail-closed `ProbeError` on malformed probe.
- **181 tests**, wired into `package.json prebuild` (unit tests only; the live run is the separate command).

**LIVE-CANARY PROOF (acceptance #1, the gate that closes F3-core):** cloned `rt-centred-maxwidth` → published live on the canary (page 1199, `sandybrown-nightingale-600381.hostingersite.com/f3-oracle-rt-centred-maxwidth/`) via the editor `wp.data` path (guard-safe, non-destructive) → probed `getComputedStyle` on the rendered `.wp-block-sgs-container` → **4 LANDED** (max-width `1200px`≠780 theme default — real transfer; padding; background `#f5f0eb`→rgb ΔE0; gap) **+ 2 UNVERIFIED** (align-items=block-default `start` via guard-3; grid-template-columns `repeat(4,1fr)`→`264px×4` lossy via tri-state) — **all CORRECT on a non-default fixture**. `_render-oracle/rt-centred-maxwidth.{landed,probe}.json` committed (reproducible). NB: the fixture's expected.md MF-3 framing (`widthMode`/`customWidth`) is STALE — those attrs were retired v0.4 (D230/D231); the converter's `maxWidth:1200px` is correct for the current wrapper and LANDED.
**Process:** SDD (sonnet impl) → cross-model Opus adversarial review (4 HIGH + 5 MEDIUM, all fixed: colour/length classifier over-match, per-section NOT-RENDERED mis-tag, empty-cells swallow, computed-style serialisation mis-fail, written precondition, named-colour parse, height tolerance) → live proof → plain-summary count-fix + driver fail-closed tidy → qc-council (empirical-baseline hard-gate MET by the live proof; cross-FAMILY Gemini rater tool-blocked in the Windows harness → stood in with a structured branch trace → FIX-M: unparseable length →UNVERIFIABLE for consistency with the colour path). Design doc: `.claude/plans/2026-06-18-f3-render-oracle-design.md` (v2).
**DEFERRED to F3-runtime** (build lazily when the rebuild first renders many fixtures): full-37 canary render-diff, content-hash cache, pixel-diff secondary, flake-classification, deploy choreography, committed per-cell baseline, %/calc/vw container-resolved length comparison, MR-1/MR-3. **NEXT: F4** (closed `excluded_properties` DB table, ships EMPTY) → F5 (build+ARM the 3 gates) → F6 (DB-as-code consistency) → stage-by-stage rebuild. **D-CEILING now D234.**

### D235 — Phase-F step F4 SHIPPED + RE-SCOPED: closed audited `excluded_properties` table (ships EMPTY); the literal-ban gate moved to F5. Bean-approved post-/qc-council 2026-06-18

F4 of the Spec-31 §12.7 Tier-1 foundation (MF-4), commit `870f48aa`. F4 = the audited `excluded_properties(css_property, reason, decided_by, date)` table ONLY — the `excluded` leg of `UNACCOUNTED = draft − (transferred ∪ excluded-with-reason ∪ gap)` (§12.2.1) that F5's pipeline-close ledger checker joins. One dated migration `migrations/2026-06-18-create-excluded-properties.py` (idempotent `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` + `UNIQUE(css_property)`, seeds ZERO rows; the migration is the only seed path). Verified: idempotent (2nd run no-op), table empty, F2+F3 (348) + Gate A (43) green, convert.py UNTOUCHED (D-MODULAR §12.0/§12.4). Design doc: `.claude/plans/2026-06-18-f4-excluded-properties-design.md` (v2).
**Ships EMPTY (Bean-locked, code-confirmed):** no property is excluded-from-CLONE. §12.7's "seed width/max-width" is a misreading — `_LIFT_EXCLUDED_PROPS` (convert.py:966) is DEAD code (max-width clones via the `maxWidth` attr at 4560/4673); `_CROSS_NODE_EXCLUDED_PROPS` (2206) is a PLACEMENT rule (don't inline-lift across nodes — GAP-3/R-22-6), and its members ARE cloned (`display` via the `layout:grid` attr → wrapper CSS, VERIFIED on the F3-core live render; `grid-template-*` via `gridTemplateColumns`). Excluded-from-lift ≠ excluded-from-clone (§12.2.4). Bean's "why would max-width be excluded?" challenge surfaced the dead code.
**RE-SCOPE via /qc-council (3 raters — spec-fidelity / adversarial-gamer / D-MODULAR):** the originally-proposed literal-ban GATE OVERCLAIMS. A static literal scan is a narrow tripwire catching only "a new named denylist set in converter_v2/"; it is blind to inline `if prop=="x":continue`, anonymous local sets (`_area_excluded`), `.startswith("--")` guards, value-transforms returning ""/None, DB-lookup-None, broad-except, and drops in `css_router.py`/`db_lookup.py` one dir UP the scan never opens. **The real no-silent-drop guarantee is F2 (draft ledger UNACCOUNTED) + F3 (LANDED) + the css_router coverage invariant (count-in == count-routed) + F5's checker** — NOT F4's scan. Bean re-scoped: F4 = table only; the gate moves to F5. The council's hardened gate requirements (coverage-invariant anchor, import-graph-wide scan, content-hashed self-blessing-proof baseline, Python pre-commit wiring, explicit delegation of transform/None/except drops to F2/F3/lint) are recorded in the design doc §3 as the F5 hand-off so they are not re-derived. AC1 also corrected (`/sgs-update` does NOT auto-run migrations — they're manual). **NEXT: F5** (build+ARM the gates per the §3 hand-off) → F6 → stage-by-stage rebuild. **D-CEILING now D235.**

### D236 — Phase-F F5 STARTED (partial): check_no_mirror armed with a committed legacy baseline; the other F5 gates remain OPEN. Bean-directed SDD+qc-inline 2026-06-18
